Chapter 3051: Chapter 3049: King Kun: I’m going to die, I’m going to die!

The main issue is that transferring a complete path to immortality is riskier, and not as compatible as the ’embryonic form of the path to immortality.’

Otherwise, give Senior White a bit more time, and he could directly deduce the ‘Karma Virtuous Path to Immortality’ to the level of a complete path to immortality—after all, both karma and virtue are integral parts of what Senior White studied.

The ’embryonic form of the path to immortality’ that Senior White himself initially concocted involved both karma and virtue.

So, after obtaining the informational data from Song Shuhang, revising the Karma Virtuous Path to Immortality for Song Shuhang was a piece of cake for him.

“Even I, back when I was at the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm, was not such a monster,” thought the Dark Sun, comparing his former self to the Immortal White before him...

To become immortal through proving one’s Dao, almost everyone’s innate skill had reached a level that shook the heavens and earth.

But recalling the time he initially concocted the ’embryonic form of the path to immortality’, even converting that time into Immortal White’s time units, it still measured in ‘years.’

The difference between years and hours is indeed substantial.

“Stay calm, stay calm. There’s definitely more to this; deducing an ’embryonic path to immortality’ within an hour is too exaggerated... Maybe they’re playing mind games.” The Dark Sun stabilized his emotions and began to speculate and guess.

Meanwhile, outside, Song Shuhang and Senior White had already started to take action.

Both were men of action; after confirming the plan, they briefly reviewed the process and then got straight to work.

The Confucian Sage Book was summoned by Song Shuhang.

The cover that Daozi added immediately started twinkling, protecting the ‘Dao’ within it from being sacrificed.

“Now, come out @#$&%!” Song Shuhang called out handsomely.

The virtuous lamia responded to his call, emerging from behind him.

The first thing she did after appearing was to wrap her tail around Song Shuhang, constricting him tightly like a giant snake capturing its prey, as if she intended to hunt Song Shuhang alive.

“Stop messing around, we have serious business, Fairy,” said Song Shuhang.

Give me some face!

Moreover, with his current constitution, even if the virtuous lamia exerted all her strength from the eggshell, she couldn’t make Song Shuhang feel the slightest pressure.

The virtuous lamia was choked up with frustration.

“Fairy, gouge out the eyeballs,” Song Shuhang reminded.

Don’t disrupt the rhythm!

Upon hearing those words, the virtuous lamia’s eyes lit up. She placed her hands on Song Shuhang’s eye sockets and gently scooped out both his eyeballs.

Then, Song Shuhang was blinded.

It was the virtuous lamia’s minor act of retaliation.

But still...

“Well done,” Song Shuhang nodded in satisfaction.

True to her name, the virtuous lamia didn’t need much explanation to fully grasp his intent.

Then Song Shuhang pointed his finger, and the ‘Scholarly Sage’s Eye’ that was replaced reverted back to its Golden Core form and returned to the ‘External Dragon Network System’, swapping out another Sage’s eye that hadn’t been sacrificed, and installed it in Song Shuhang’s right eye.

Then, the other ‘ glazed eyeball’ held by the virtuous lamia gently floated up.

“Come out, Tyrant!” Song Shuhang summoned again.

Three Corpses • Tyrant came through the ‘main world’ as a transit, crossing space to arrive.

As he returned, he also brought along the ‘egg of King Kun’—his original task was to go to Senior White two’s Sinful Black Lotus world to bring back the egg of King Kun.

Previously, the egg of King Kun was still under study by Senior White two’s research manifestation.

Now, as the research ended, Tyrant conveniently brought it along.

...

...

When the egg of King Kun was brought over, it just so happened to see the scene where Tyrant Song gouged out his eyeballs and summoned the ‘Confucian Classics.’

— Fuck, wasn’t this the scene from earlier where Tyrant Song sacrificed his own ‘path to immortality’ in front of the myriad practitioners in the universe?

Is Tyrant Song doing this again?

Is he going to sacrifice another path to immortality and a Scholarly Sage’s eye?

— Tyrannical Song’s own path to immortality had already been sacrificed once.

Even if Tyrannical Song were a monstrous genius, there was no way a third ‘immortal path’ would be seamlessly waiting for him at this time!

Such a monstrous existence was impossible in this world!

Therefore, if Tyrannical Song were to conduct a sacrificial ritual this time, he would definitely sacrifice someone else’s immortal path.

It was obvious to anyone with a brain that Tyrannical Song would never allow himself to fall below the realm of ‘Immortal’!

Under this premise, he had been brought before Tyrannical Song by the Three Corpses Evil Corpse.

Was there even a need to guess the outcome?

Indeed, the next sacrifice would be me, right?

The ‘immortal path’ I’ve diligently cultivated is about to become Tyrannical Song’s sacrificial offering.

How tragic, being a Kun, it’s too tragic.

Clashing with Tyrannical Song felt exhilarating for a moment, but after being captured alive by Tyrannical Song, the past delights turned into present miseries.

I’m going to die, this time I’m definitely doomed.

I don’t even know if the immortal path, once sacrificed, will still have a chance to be cultivated again?

During the process of sacrifice of the immortal path, will it be painful?

Escape was already impossible, the egg of King Kun knew it could never escape from the palm of Tyrannical Song... At this point, it could only hope that Tyrannical Song would be a bit gentler later.

Inside the egg of King Kun, the consciousness of King Kun was filled with despair and trembling.

It closed its senses, quietly awaiting the merciless fate about to fall upon its head.

...

...

Song Shuhang summoned Tyrant after, pointing at that ‘glazed eyeball’—this glazed eyeball contained the Mysterious Principles of the ‘knowledge and language longevity technique.’

Tyrant nodded, then turned to face the virtuous lamia.

The virtuous fairy stretched her hand into Tyrant’s eye socket and, while at it, fitted the ‘glazed eyeball’ inside.

“So, main body, Senior White, @#%× Fairy, I’ll take the lead,” Tyrant bowed to them.

Afterward, he returned to the main world and dove into the Netherworld Realm.

Then from the Netherworld Realm he boarded the ‘small-black-room-breaking disposable flying sword’ to enter the small black room of the Will of the Heavens and disappeared from the memories of the practitioners in the universe.

“Ready,” Song Shuhang activated his Magical Techniques, conjuring a new glazed eyeball in his empty eye socket.

Next step.

The Confucian Classic brightened.

Song Shuhang activated the modified ‘Saint’s secret technique.’

The other ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ in his eye socket burned with golden flames, becoming a sacrificial offering.

“Very good, everything is smooth, next step,” Song Shuhang continued.

“I understand, be gentle, Tyrannical Song,” the egg of King Kun trembled as it transmitted its thought.

Song Shuhang: “???”

Be gentle my foot!

Your sudden sound transmission almost interrupted my ritual.

“Shut up,” Song Shuhang said.

Then, the secret technique of the Sage’s Eye enveloped him, and the freshly minted New Immortality ‘knowledge and language path to immortality’ was also integrated into the Saint’s secret technique, becoming a sacrificial offering.

Song Shuhang’s realm began to weaken once more.

The ‘full moon of Immortal’ above his head started to dim.

[Not sacrificing me?] thought the egg of King Kun.

Or perhaps Tyrannical Song, distracted by my disruption, accidentally sacrificed himself?

Chapter 3052: Chapter 3050: Come, Senior White, swallow me!

“[Ruthless.] When the Dark Sun behemoth witnessed this scene, his heart stirred.”

“Within a single day, sacrificing his own way to immortality twice, such ruthlessness toward oneself, the likes of which even the Dark Sun behemoth, who had lived for so long, had never before encountered.”

“It was almost as if he bore a grudge against himself.”

“Truth be told, such ruthless people are the last ones you should provoke... If he doesn’t even cherish himself, what makes you think he would care about the world?”

“But from a certain perspective, might this guy have much in common with him?”

“Perhaps, later on, he might try to tempt this guy and see if he could recruit him to his own camp?”

As he pondered this, Song Shuhang’s secret technique was already complete.

“Once is happenstance, twice is familiarity.”

This time, the ‘Sage’s secret technique’ was completed 20% faster than before, improving the efficiency significantly.”

As the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ in his eye sockets again dried up to only a Golden Core membrane, and all of the ‘language and text’ paths to immortality within him were sacrificed, Song Shuhang opened the “Confucian Classic,” directing it toward Senior White.”

The Sage’s innate ability merged into Senior White’s body.”

“The inheritance of Sage’s innate ability is chancy... But no matter how slim the chance is, even one in a billion, if it benefits Senior White, then this chance is no different from one hundred percent.”

“Now, acquiring the Sage’s talent is precisely the outcome Senior White desired.”

“The entire inheritance ceremony went off without a hitch.”

“[Now is the moment!] At this moment, King Kun saw Tyrannical Song’s weakness.”

“Falling from the ‘Immortal Realm’ would indeed leave him weak for a little while.”

“King Kun felt that his opportunity had arrived—the gates of freedom seemed to be opening for him.”

“But just then, Tyrannical Song’s aura suddenly shifted.”

“An aura that could swallow mountains and rivers, wanting to consume all things, surged from Tyrannical Song.”

“Not only that, an aura that made the shell of King Kun tingle emerged from Tyrannical Song—the aura of a Confucian Sage!”

“As an Immortal who had been beaten and taught by a Confucian Sage, the moment King Kun sensed this aura, his legs went weak.”

...

...

“Following Senior White’s instructions, as the ‘Sage’s talent inheritance ceremony’ was in its final stages, before the ‘Immortal full moon’ behind Senior White’s head completely faded, Song Shuhang applied the ‘Confucian Sage Talent’ to Senior White.”

“On the other side, Senior White did not resist but actively worked with Song Shuhang’s application of the ‘Sage’s talent,’ and also offered up the already prepared ‘karmic and virtue embodiment of the embryonic form of the way to immortality.’”

“They swallowed parts of each other’s ‘existence’—a crucial part of the planned strategy of [two different entities proving their Dao simultaneously] devised by Song Shuhang, Senior White, and Senior Two.”

“No need for too much, just a small portion of each other’s ‘existence’ was enough.”

“With Senior White not resisting and cooperating with Song Shuhang’s actions, the process went very smoothly. Since it was Senior White’s own intent, Song Shuhang did not have to worry about any ‘calamities’ befalling him during the process.”

“Sage’s talent returned.”

“It brought back a small part of Immortal White’s existence, along with the embryonic form of the way to immortality.”

“This embryonic form of the way to immortality, initially derived by Immortal White based on the insights and information given by Song Shuhang, was supremely compatible with Song Shuhang himself.”

“Upon accepting this part of ‘the embryonic form of the way to immortality,’ Song Shuhang instantaneously comprehended and understood this way to immortality.”

“At the same time, ‘Heavenly Dao’s Deduction Ability’ loaded upon him.”

Under the deduction of the Heavenly Axiom level, the original embryonic form of the Dao of Longevity was forcefully expanded into a spacious and complete path to immortality.

The ‘full moon’ of the immortal that was originally dim behind Song Shuhang’s head brightened up once again!

The whole process ended in the blink of an eye.

The time it took for the egg of King Kun to be stunned... and then Tyrannical Song regained the Immortal Realm once again.

This path involving karmic and the light of virtue was upright and direct, a King’s Immortality method, and its level was likewise not inferior to the ‘Seeking Life Through Death Method’ and ‘Language, Writing Longevity Method’.

Not only that, in a cycle of destruction and establishment, establishment and destruction, and establishment after destruction, the aura on Tyrannical Song became even more terrifying.

Every cycle made Tyrannical Song stronger.

As long as it was not the setback of death, it would make a person stronger!

Feeling that Tyrannical Song had become more terrifying and stronger, the egg of King Kun instantly chickened out.

Could you believe Tyrannical Song actually had a third path of immortality for backup? Was this the work of a mortal?

[Fortunately, I hadn’t started my ‘escape’ action yet... Otherwise, just as I started to run, I might have been captured by Tyrannical Song. Then I would be waiting for the frying pot and the barbecue grill.] King Kun felt a wave of relief inside.

It clearly remembered that several of the pendants on Tyrannical Song, upon hearing its identity as ‘Kun,’ immediately started clamoring for barbecue.

If Tyrannical Song caught the opportunity, it would probably really roast him.

What’s worse, as an existence at the Immortal level, even if a portion of him was sliced off for barbecue, it would grow back after a while.

Then what awaited him would be the real hell.

Being cowardly brought a peaceful interlude...

So, the egg of King Kun quietly calmed down.

Senior White opened his eyes and asked, “Was it successful?”

“Yes, Senior White, very successful,” Song Shuhang replied.

The path to immortality that combined karmic and the light of virtue was more successful than imagined, and better suited to become the ‘fiber of the Cultivator Chat System’.

Originally, Song Shuhang had only thought about using either the light of virtue or karmic, with a personal preference towards using the power of ‘light of virtue’ to weave a path to immortality.

But Senior White directly mixed the two together.

Now, Song Shuhang was trying to use this new path to immortality to weave the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group into this network, connecting them together for the distant future.

However, the ‘portion of existence’ he obtained from Senior White was still operating peacefully within Song Shuhang’s energy system.

This portion of existence, unlike the ‘existence of the fat ball’ that was swallowed before.

The portion of the fat ball’s existence that was swallowed was then transferred to ‘Dark Song’, quickly merged with Dark Song, and was absorbed completely by her.

However, the portion of ‘existence’ from Senior White that entered Song Shuhang’s energy system operated along with his immortal energy without showing any signs of fusion.

They still remained two completely different entities.

If they cannot merge, remaining two different entities, would the future plan of [two different entities proving their Dao simultaneously]not be doomed?

“Is something missing?” Song Shuhang wondered aloud.

“Is there a problem?” Seeing Song Shuhang’s serious expression, Senior White asked.

“Unable to fuse,” Song Shuhang described his current situation.

“Hmm... what’s missing might be because you are still ‘complete’. Since you are still complete, adding another portion would become superfluous,” Senior White speculated.

Chapter 3053: Chapter 3051: Shocking, Eternity Could Actually Be Devoured!

Song Shuhang suddenly had an epiphany.

It made sense.

If you have two hands, wouldn’t adding another simply make three hands?

And normal people don’t have a place to attach a third hand anyway!

Therefore, to fuse the ‘portion of existence’ obtained from Senior White, one needs to enter the next phase!

“Come on, Senior White, devour a portion of my existence,” Song Shuhang said boldly.

The atmosphere turned solemn.

[That’s so ruthless!] The watching Dark Sun involuntarily shrank back its light.

Not only has he sacrificed his ‘way to immortality’ over and over, but now he’s even ready to relinquish his ‘existence’ to let someone else devour it... It’s like he doesn’t consider his own body as anything valuable, this is self-abuse!

The egg of King Kun kept a low profile, reducing its aura to the limit.

Fearing that any accidental leakage of its aura could affect Tyrannical Song, and then it would get swallowed in one gulp.

On the sealing track.

Senior White first operated the ‘Confucian Saint Talent’ to get familiar with the operation process and effects of this innate skill.

“Ready,” Senior White notified.

He raised his two fingers in front of his eyes, and the Sage’s talent activated.

Song Shuhang took a deep breath, trying hard to relax himself and cooperate with Senior White.

[Here it comes again, here it comes again.] The egg of King Kun sensed the aura of the Confucian Sage once more.

But this time, the source of the aura was Immortal White.

[Just how many contingency plans did the Confucian Sage leave behind!] The egg of King Kun felt desperate.

Why did it seem like the Confucian Sage’s presence was everywhere?

Especially since it was captured by Tyrannical Song, it always felt like the Confucian Sage was related to everything in the myriad practitioners in the universe; everyone appeared to be a rebirth of the Confucian Sage.

Once again, the Sage’s innate ability activated, enveloping Song Shuhang.

“It feels like something in the dark is being grabbed, about to be sliced off. I feel anxious, as if I’m about to lose something important... Is this how the fat ball felt at that time?” Song Shuhang keenly savored this anxious emotion.

Whether it was pain or tribulation, it was all worth savoring, analyzing, and ultimately transcending all this pain.

Szzzzz~

While he was pondering, a grating sizzling sound started ringing in his ears. It was like the noise of a cutting machine slicing through metal, quite uncomfortable to listen to.

“What’s happening?” Song Shuhang wondered.

Then, he found that his entire body was enveloped and protected by the power of eternity.

Some sort of defensive measure from the fat whale golden core seemed to have been activated.

The Confucian Sage’s Devouring Talent was being blocked.

“Disengage the defense!” Song Shuhang quickly commanded—he needed to cooperate with Senior White, allowing a part of himself to follow Senior White instead of blocking the Sage’s talent here.

But this layer of ‘Immortal Power Defense’ was like the skin of an ordinary human.

It wasn’t temporarily activated, it had always been there, always protecting the individual that was Song Shuhang.

Forcing this layer of ‘Immortal Power Defense’ to be removed required Song Shuhang to operate with precision, actively peeling it away!

[Immortality, it really is a secret technique developed against immortality!] When the Dark Sun saw this scene, it was thrown into disarray.

This secret technique was indeed an attempt targeting immortality!

If this was successfully executed on this ‘Tyrannical Song’... then the next one to be targeted by this secret technique would definitely be him!

[But, how could the power of eternity be so easily affected? A mere secret technique, still a mortal one, is utterly incapable of shaking immortality!] The Dark Sun murmured.

Boom~

Just at that moment, behind Immortal White, a boundless galaxy spread out.

Yet another aura of eternity!

The same ‘immortal’ power surged from the endless galaxy, enhancing Immortal White.

The eternal energy of the fat whale golden core and the endless galaxy’s eternal power cancelled each other out for a moment.

In that brief moment, Senior White, who had activated the ‘Confucian Saint Talent’, had successfully taken a portion of ‘existence’ from Song Shuhang and brought it back to Immortal White.

Although there were some minor accidents along the way, overall, the goal of Song Shuhang and Senior White had been smoothly achieved!

The Immortal Defense was broken?

A secret technique that could even ‘devour’ immortality?

“Gulp~” The Dark Sun giant, witnessing the scene, gulped down some nonexistent saliva.

It’s confirmed!

This alpaca’s secret technique was specifically developed ‘against immortality’, targeting it!

Moreover, Tyrannical Song and Immortal White purposely experimented with this technique in front of it... a heart-piercing move.

This couldn’t go on.

If this continued, the next step would be Tyrannical Song and Immortal White joining forces to take action against it!

Even ‘immortal’ power probably wouldn’t be able to protect it.

Immortality had been the Dark Sun’s confident capital; now, this capital was being shredded before its eyes by Tyrannical Song and Immortal White.

After all, the Dark Sun was not the ‘Heavenly Dao Body’ and because it was the Netherworld Ruler Body that had been forcibly seized by remnants of the Heavenly Dao, the Dark Sun had many hidden dangers.

In handling certain emergency situations, its processing and reaction abilities would be slightly delayed.

At this moment, the Dark Sun frantically began to deduce, trying to find a way to ‘free’ itself.

But the more anxious it became, the more turbulent the deductions, unable to stabilize.

“What to do, am I really just waiting for death?”

The Dark Sun certainly didn’t intend to just wait for death.

It began to struggle frantically again, deducing continuously, while trying its best to send out the signal that it was in ‘crisis’.

It didn’t know to whom to send the signal.

Regardless, the signal had to be sent out!

...

...

At the same time, the ‘aura of eternity’ on both Song Shuhang and Immortal White simultaneously retracted.

After exchanging glances, they almost simultaneously turned their gaze to the ‘Dark Sun’ sealed within.

Combined with the ‘immortality’ attribute, the Confucian Sage’s ‘Devouring Talent’ seemed to be able to break through the defense against immortal information... then, it might also be effective against the Dark Sun!

The current state of the Dark Sun was somewhat similar to that of Song Shuhang.

It was not truly ‘immortal’ but relied on the remnant undying body of the Great Way to obtain the mode of immortal information—Its advantage over Song Shuhang was that the ‘Immortal Material’ inside it was the actual remnants of the Heavenly Dao. Unlike Song Shuhang, who had clumsily evolved his own immortality.

“Should we try it?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Theoretically, it is feasible,” Senior White replied. “But let’s notify Confucian Daoist to come over first... let him take command.”

Meanwhile, both he and Song Shuhang needed to adjust their states.

At this point, Song Shuhang and Immortal White both were in an ‘incomplete’ state, and each of their energy systems contained ‘a part of the other’s existence’, which could be used to complete themselves.

“I’m here,” Daozi’s voice sounded directly in the vacuum.

At the same time, in the special dimensional world belonging to the Heavenly Dao, Daozi’s main body set aside the experiment in his hands.

He was fiddling with the data from half of the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ obtained from the ‘Dark Sun’.

Of course, Daozi would not attempt to create ‘stellar viruses’.

What he was experimenting with at the moment was the process of reversing this, dissolving the virus at its root.

Chapter 3054: Chapter 3052: Infinite Karmic Flames

Daozi’s portion of intent had always followed by Song Shuhang’s side.

Once he learned that Song Shuhang and Immortal White had figured out a method to “restrain” the Dark Sun, he immediately put down his own experiments, took his real body out of the Heavenly Dao Dimension World, and fled into the place where he was sealed.

If Tyrannical Song and Immortal White really could swallow the existence of the ‘Dark Sun,’ causing it to fall into a ten thousand year unconsciousness like the ‘Fat Ball Netherworld Ruler,’ then he would be able to retire peacefully.

Ten thousand years was already quite enough.

If not ten thousand years, a thousand years should suffice.

Tyrannical Song and Immortal White, together with the former rulers of the Netherworld, could definitely arrange the ‘Dark Sun’ completely clear and bright within a thousand years.

After Daozi’s real body arrived, he couldn’t wait to say, “Tyrannical Song, Fellow Daoist White... just cast your spells, I will defend for you. If you really can break through its ‘Immortal Data Defense’ and swallow its existence, swallow as much as you can, don’t be polite.”

Although Daozi remained expressionless... anyone could hear the excitement in his tone.

If he could solve the hidden danger of the Dark Sun before his ‘retirement,’ even if it required a cost, he was willing to do it.

Some calamities, if they can be solved in his generation, he didn’t want to leave them to the next.

Song Shuhang and Senior White silently nodded, but didn’t speak—they were both still completing the ‘complementing themselves’ step.

Inside the seal.

The Dark Sun grew more and more restless.

The arrival of the Heavenly Dao Body meant it had reached a dead end.

Even if it figured out the loophole in this seal and broke out... it would be suppressed by the Heavenly Dao in an instant.

Apart from waiting for death, it had no other options to choose from.

How desperate must it feel when one faces a significant life decision, but it’s a single-option question, and that single option is not only the only one available but also a wrong answer?

“Heh, you’re still thinking about sending out rescue signals?” After Daozi’s real body approached the seal, he said indifferently. He reached out and pinched in the vacuum.

With a crisp snap—a sound was heard.

The numerous ‘Rescue Signals’ desperately sent by the ‘Dark Sun’ within the seal were grabbed by Daozi and, like fragile goods, crushed into pieces!

Then Daozi reached out again and plucked out several ‘Rescue Signals’ from the vacuum, as if catching loaches, crushing them all.

These ‘Rescue Signals’, without a definite ‘recipient,’ were just signals that the Dark Sun desperately sent out in despair, spreading randomly. The Dark Sun itself did not know whom to send these signals to.

When Daozi caught them, he pondered over them for a while... but did not figure out the ‘object of the rescue.’

Even so, Daozi had no intention of allowing these few ‘Rescue Signals’ to spread out—he intended to kill all possible ‘accidents’ in the cradle, not giving the ‘Dark Sun’ any chance.

“If you don’t want to taste the heavenly punishment, then stay put,” Daozi said solemnly.

After mastering many Heavenly Dao Authorities, he finally activated the authority for ‘heavenly punishment to descend.’

Heavenly punishment can’t destroy ‘eternity,’ but it can bring great pain to the Dark Sun.

“Heavenly punishment?” When it heard the option of heavenly punishment, the Dark Sun did not feel fear but instead became more agitated.

It seemed to remember something, and even had an urge to face the ‘heavenly punishment’ as soon as possible!

Daozi: “...”

He silently withdrew the option to ‘activate heavenly punishment.’

No matter whether the Dark Sun within the seal was acting or not, but when the opponent showed a desire to ‘eagerly accept heavenly punishment,’ Daozi immediately lost the intention to lower the heavenly punishment.

Every generation of the Heavenly Dao are monstrous geniuses. Perhaps the real body of the Dark Sun, like Tyrannical Song, enjoys heavenly tribulations and adores heavenly punishments?

Thinking this, Daozi turned his head and glanced at Song Shuhang.

Coincidentally, Song Shuhang also opened his left eye... his right eye was still blind, with the ‘Sage Eye Golden Core’ inside it recovering with the aid of the fat whale golden core’s power.

As Senior White had guessed, after both he and Senior White became ‘incomplete,’ they started to complement themselves with the parts swallowed from each other.

Even without the harvest from the ‘hundred joint attacks,’ Song Shuhang could perfect the fat whale golden core in a short amount of time.

The harvest from the hundred joint attacks consumed only a little on the fat whale golden core.

The surplus harvest was absorbed by the fat whale golden core, transformed, and then burst forth as ‘fountains.’

The ‘fountains’ turned into ‘Immortal Light’ like silk, starting to encase Song Shuhang by his side.

—Spinning cocoons was something Song Shuhang was now very skilled at.

He had once spun a perfect grand cocoon.

This time, the challenge was even smaller; he merely needed to control the silken rays of light to spin the cocoons with his mind.

Starting from Song Shuhang’s ‘head,’ the Light Cocoon began to condense.

The ‘power of eternity,’ transformed by the fat whale golden core, continuously erupted in the form of fountains, turning into light silk.

Tens of breaths later.

Song Shuhang’s head was now completely enveloped within the ‘Immortal Light Cocoon.’

But at that moment, the fat whale golden core stopped its ‘fountain’ action.

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

Hum~

Above his head, only a head’s worth of Light Cocoon was woven; it could only hastily close... The Light Cocoon enveloped and wrapped around Song Shuhang’s head.

It looked as though Song Shuhang’s body had been fitted with a glowing round egg.

Daozi: “...”

If he wasn’t currently expressionless and unable to effectively convey his emotions, he would have burst into laughter by now.

Senior White: “...”

“Senior, if you want to laugh, just laugh,” Song Shuhang shook his head, and the light cocoon on top of it scattered beautiful, flowing rays of light as it swayed.

“Actually, there’s nothing funny,” Senior White said calmly. “I was just wondering if this light cocoon tastes good?”

Song Shuhang: “!!!”

How could this thing even be edible?

Could it be... Senior White is craving something to nibble on?

“By the way, Shuhang, what’s going on with you?” Daozi Senior couldn’t help but ask.

What’s the use of spinning this light cocoon?

“I don’t quite understand it myself. Just now, I suddenly felt an urge to spin a cocoon, so I followed my heart and prepared to spin one... and as you see. I was only at the head part when the thread suddenly broke,” Song Shuhang poked at the cocoon on his head.

As his fingers gently poked, the light cocoon on his head suddenly burst open.

The power of the immortal light cocoon, with the bursting of the cocoon, infiltrated into Song Shuhang’s head, beginning to strengthen this area of his body.

The first aspect to be reinforced was “Tyrannical Song’s face.”

As a strong man, it’s essential to have a strong facade, both physically and spiritually.

On the physical level, a strong facade can keep a cultivator’s face fresh and maintain their demeanor, even in the harshest environments.

On a psychological level, the facade is one of the points most valued by bigshots, related to the issue of whether or not others give them face.

“Tyrannical Song’s face” was already one of the strongest parts of his body, which not even “heavenly punishment” could destroy.

Now reinforced, “Tyrannical Song’s face” faintly displayed a hint of ‘eternal’ radiance, a level higher than ‘pseudo-eternal,’ and just below the immortalized fat whale golden core—barely qualifying as ‘Sub-immortal.’

If he could gain an opportunity similar to the ‘fat whale golden core,’ perhaps in the future, it could evolve into a truly ‘immortal face’!

The power of the immortal light cocoon continued to permeate.

After “Tyrannical Song’s face,” Song Shuhang’s skull was also strengthened.

The light of the cocoon penetrated every part of his skull in a 360-degree angle without any dead ends.

Similar to the face, Song Shuhang’s skull also began its sub-immortalization, advancing beyond the ‘pseudo-eternal’ state.

“The skull and the face...is this the rhythm of sub-immortalization from the inside out?” Song Shuhang reached out and touched his face.

The power of the light cocoon slowly progressed in modifying Song Shuhang’s head; it wasn’t an immediate transformation.

The predicted time required for the upgrade was about a day...

A day isn’t too long; just entering the ‘time-distorted secret realm,’ a day will pass in an instant.

Roughly estimating, the energy from a hundred joint attacks could almost complete the sub-immortalization of a ‘skull’ plus ‘skin.’ To achieve full-body sub-immortalization of bones and skin without any hitches, it could be completed within about ten times!” calculated Song Shuhang internally.

About ten times—with the aid of the ‘time-distorted secret realm,’ it would be completed very quickly!

“Once the bones and skin of my entire body achieve sub-immortalization, I can further attempt to upgrade my flesh and blood... If I were to turn my whole body into a ‘Sub-immortal’ state paired with ‘fat whale golden core,’ it would almost be akin to a budget version of immortality,” Song Shuhang said, pinching his face.

It’s a bit of a beautiful thought, but living in this world, one must indulge in beautiful thoughts. Life is already so hard; if we don’t harbor beautiful thoughts, how can we continue day by day?

“No choice, I have to make a move,” the Dark Giant stated.

If it didn’t act now, it would be ejected from this world again, only able to wait for the next “Heavenly Dao Reincarnation” to commence.

It didn’t want to wait for another cycle anymore!

“Fortunately, I’ve made some modifications to the ‘Domination Secret Method’... Now is the perfect time to use it,” the Dark Giant said and began to activate the incredibly precious secret method that took tens of thousands of years to condense.

[That secret method,is called ‘Domination Secret Method’? Such a blatant and straightforward name?]Song Shuhang’s attention shifted from the Sage of Confucianism and the fat ball back to the Dark Giant.

Any secret method that includes the word ‘domination’ always inexplicably felt familiar to him.

Although the ‘Domination Secret Method’ sounded blunt, Song Shuhang felt a connection with it and instinctively wanted to keep a closer eye on it.

By coincidence, the ‘gaze’ of the Dark Giant also shifted from the Sage of Confucianism back to itself.

A pair of pitch-black gravelly palms condensed and slowly began to form a modified seal—since this was the Dark Giant’s first time using it, he was very cautious.

Its caution provided Tyrannical Song a chance to learn.

Deep down, Song Shuhang truly was a top-notch scholar...

The reason he seemed like a poor student in ‘foundation establishment cultivation knowledge’ was mainly due to time constraints.

If he were a normal Immortal big shot, gradually advancing through small realms every few years, large realms every few decades, condensing a Nascent Soul in a few hundred years, becoming a Profound Sage in a few thousand years, and a Tribulation Transcender in tens of thousands of years, then his cultivation knowledge would absolutely match his own realm, becoming that of a ‘scholarly, reliable senior.’

Despite only having cultivated about a year, Song Shuhang’s grasp of cultivation knowledge, space spell theories, and combat skills far exceeded any other cultivator who had only cultivated for a year!

Song Shuhang stared at the pitch-black gravelly hands, watching the series of seals, and firmly memorized them.

[Hmm, I’ll go ask Senior White to see if we can decrypt this ‘Domination Secret Method’ and perhaps simplify it to just three formation runes, which seems more suitable for me]Tyrannical Song concluded.

Ever since having many senior pendants, Senior White, Daoist Senior, Senior Three Eyes, Father Goudan, and other big shots around him, Song Shuhang’s ‘scholar attribute’ gradually had fewer opportunities for use.

...

...

The highly precious ‘Domination Secret Method’ that the Dark Giant had condensed was successful, then it began to lock its gaze on the Sage of Confucianism.

—Although the battle had been prolonged so long without ending, from the look of the scene, the entire battle situation had already entered into the phase where the Sage of Confucianism controlled the environment.

The Sage always managed to identify the fat ball’s weaknesses, launching a series of strikes on it.

The fat ball could still barely defend itself, but its defenses were less and less effective against the Sage. The Sage had found a pattern and could easily break through those defenses, stringingly striking at the fat ball’s essence.

At this rate, even if they dragged out the time a bit longer, the ultimate winner would surely be the Sage of Confucianism!

Even among past Heavenly Dao figures, before proving his Dao, the Sage of Confucianism’s performance could be ranked very high!

Such an existence, it would be difficult for the Heavenly Dao not to acknowledge him!

The Dark Giant believed in its own judgment.

Therefore, it still planned to take a shot at the Sage, setting the Sage as its primary target.

Buzz—

The modified ‘Domination Secret Method’ was cast, aiming towards the Sage of Confucianism from afar.

—This peculiar ‘Domination Secret Method’ had an extremely low presence, basically impossible to detect.

The first time, even the Wielder of the Will White had been directly hit.

The Sage of Confucianism was no exception; just like the previous Wielder of the Will White, he completely received the effect of this ‘Domination Secret Method’.

Seeing the Sage of Confucianism receive the ‘Domination Secret Method,’ the Black Sun emitted a joyful laugh.

“Excellent, just like that. I believe you have a better chance of seizing the Heavenly Dao... However, given that bizarre and handsome predecessor’s example, I must make some changes,” the Dark Giant once again began to form the secret method.

But this time, he wasn’t rubbing the “Domination Secret Method.”

The Domination Secret Method, extremely tyrannical... it could only condense once every tens of millions of years. Moreover, given its bodily state, it could only store one shot. If it wanted to condense a second one, the energy would be directly swallowed by the first shot of “Domination Secret Method.”

This was a very tyrannical and aggressive rule of secret technique.

Since he couldn’t condense a second shot, he could only improve the effects of the first one.

After the secret technique was rubbed out, the Dark Giant secretly pointed at ‘fat ball,’ leaving a ‘mark’ on it without a sound.

Though the likelihood was very, very small, if by chance the last one to prove his Dao was Fat Ball, then this ‘mark’ could quietly transfer the Domination Secret Method from the Sage of Confucianism once Fat Ball started proving its pseudo-immortal body.

After undergoing the transfer, the ‘Domination Secret Method’ would certainly be somewhat inferior, but having something was better than nothing... If need be, it could patch things up afterward.

“Prepare for both hands, even if at the end, this Sage turns the Heavenly Dao seat over to Ball in the plot, my plan will not fail,” the Dark Giant said satisfied.

Then, its existence began to be repelled by ‘myriad practitioners in the universe,’ forcing it to retreat quietly.

“This time... I will go back and wait to receive the successful news of the ‘Domination Secret Method,’” the Dark Giant elegantly exited the scene.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang had recorded the entire process of the ‘Domination Secret Method’ and its ‘Domination Secret Method Mark Two.’

Later, he would discuss it with the seniors.

I really like your ‘Domination Secret Method’—later on, it will be mine.

Moreover, I don’t just want to dominate your ‘Domination Secret Method,’ I also want to improve it—the tens of millions of years is just too long, holding a move for so long practicality. Thus, the qi gathering time must be improved!

Thinking about this, Song Shuhang also left the scene, satisfied.

But this time was somewhat different from the previous rounds.

In the previous rounds, after leaving the scene, the Dark Giant would fall into a dark slumber.

But this time, Song Shuhang, in the darkness, could still hear its voice.

“Eh? It’s not done yet? It’s been over a year now.”

The darkness continued for a long time.

“Ten years now, ten years!”

The darkness persisted.

“Twenty years now, a full twenty years!”

The darkness remained.

“How much longer must I fight, it’s been thirty years now,” the Dark Giant started to grow restless.

The darkness continued its diligent sequence.

The Dark Giant was like a code monkey pulling an all-nighter, clearly very sleepy, yet still striving to stay awake.

“Buzz, what’s happening? Three thousand years now, it’s been three thousand years!”

Song Shuhang: “???”

Three thousand years?

The darkness was still emotionless.

“Ten thousand years now, ten thousand years? A Heavenly Dao struggle, ten thousand years?”

Song Shuhang pinched his chin.

A moment later, he laughed out loud, pleased.

Chapter 3067: Chapter 3065: Under the Will of the Heavens, I Am Supreme!
Father Goudan, who had been monitoring Song Shuhang’s condition in secret, felt utterly hopeless at this moment.

“It’s over, there’s no hope left. Tyrannical Song’s daughter is gone, and his granddaughter is gone too...” Father Goudan, in this instance, resembled an elderly father lamenting over his sterilized child.

“Actually, Mister Song still has a biological daughter,” the Heavenly Emperor’s child hinted on the side—the mechanical girl, Xiao Lingxiao, was indeed Tyrannical Song’s genuine biological daughter.

In order not to become Heavenly Goudan or Emperor Goudan, she too was taking action.

“Xiao Lingxiao surely counts, but Tyrannical Song doesn’t have a son, and no son means no granddaughter. Besides, from the bottom of my heart, I also hope that Tyrannical Song can have a somewhat normal biological daughter. In this regard, I am both open-minded and conservative,” said Father Goudan as he affectionately picked up Xiao Lingxiao with his dragon mustaches.

“The life element’s path to immortality doesn’t work for Mister Song anymore?” Black-skinned Soft Feather asked cautiously.

“It’s ineffective, he’s sub-immortal... This kind of sub-immortality is actually a prototype of true immortality, much more advanced than the pseudo-eternal smoky form. At this level, sterilization is quite thorough,” the three-eyed young senior replied from the side.

Black-skinned Soft Feather nodded thoughtfully.

...

...

On another side.

The Dark Giant took a deep breath, conducting one final check of all the ‘tactical preparations’.

A moment later, fighting off the increasing weariness, he ordered, “Tactical scheme, activate!”

At the same time, he covertly manipulated a ‘Heavenly Dao regulation script’s back door and activated it.

– Every Heavenly Dao, before retirement, can leave behind some ‘Heavenly Dao regulation scripts’ for the next Heavenly Dao to activate and use, to quickly grasp the laws of the Heavenly Dao. For example, the ‘modification of the ruler of the Netherworld’s memories script’ that Daozi had previously activated belongs to this category.

Apart from the ‘modification of the ruler of the Netherworld’s memories script’, the Dark Giant, during his time in charge, also left behind a ‘myriad practitioners in the universe major calamity alarm program’... When a major catastrophe occurs in the array of worlds, this program will trigger an alarm.

This Heavenly Dao regulation script had always been operating normally, so the Heavenly Dao who succeeded him did not remove this script.

And within this ‘major calamity alarm program,’ the Dark Giant had hidden a back door. Even after leaving office, he could activate it through specific means!

The Dark Giant was neither the first ‘formal’ Heavenly Dao to do such a thing nor would he be the last.

Once the script was activated, Daozi was immediately awakened.

The next moment, Daozi sensed that a ‘gigantic calamity’ red dot flashed in every realm of the myriad practitioners in the universe.

The calamity alarm filled Daozi’s consciousness with messages.

Instinctively, Daozi expanded the ‘Heavenly Dao’s View,’ scanning each location that triggered the alarm.

[Now is the moment!] The Dark Giant seized the opportunity.

Opportunities were fleeting. The Heavenly Dao might react, close the program warning, and delete the back door in just a few seconds.

And he needed to seize this very brief moment to act!

First, three ‘Artificial Constant Stars’ were compressed and transported over, thrown into the Sealing Array formed by the 1-33 Unknown Whites.

Each of these Artificial Constant Stars contained the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus.’ Once detonated, they would release explosion attacks imbued with a trace of the ‘aura of eternity,’ along with the transmission of the virus.

If possible, the Dark Giant really wanted to directly move three stars for detonation... But the Eighth Heavenly Dao was watching from outside; he didn’t dare to make such a huge move, fearing it would attract the attention of the Heavenly Dao.

The three Artificial Constant Stars exploded, and the terrifying impact force peeled back the sealing shell of the 1-33 Unknown Whites, revealing the true forms of the 33 Unknown Whites.

The consciousness of the Dark Giant, attached to the Virtuous Daoist Body, saw this scene and involuntarily made a swallowing motion... Merciless! Were there truly 33 of those beautiful troublemakers similar to that beautiful scoundrel?

This left him no way out.

Mark them all, every single one.

The thirty-three ‘beautiful troublemakers’ didn’t impress him as much as the ‘sheep-shearing’ troublemaker, yet they still had to be taken seriously!

Moreover, there were thirty-three of them, an overwhelming number. If he wasn’t careful, any one of them could cause trouble, and accidents could happen.

However... Now was not the time to consider so many things with such pressing urgency.

Rough markings completed, after the outer shell of the Sealing Array burst open, the Dark Sun immediately sent the “Heavenly Dao Molt” it had collected into this world.

Hundreds of Dark Mini-Suns, composed of black particles, tumbled into the Sealing Array, crashing and slamming violently.

Heavenly Dao Molts are monsters that know only destruction and lack intelligence.

But they are extremely easy to use, especially because they have an “Black Hole Devouring Talent,” making them the perfect weapon for creating chaos when unleashed.

As each dark “Heavenly Dao Molt Mini-Sun” tumbled, it transformed into a black hole that devoured everything in the main world.

Song Shuhang had encountered these black holes before—he had nearly been swallowed by the black hole of a Heavenly Dao Molt Ball!

“Rotate!” exclaimed Unknown White No. 31 softly.

The entire Sealing Array revolved and shifted, exposing the trump card “Senior White two’s golden thigh” and the black horse’s flair for drama.

The drama king horse leapt out excitedly, directly stomping towards the black hole of a “Heavenly Dao Molt Mini-Sun,” shattering a small black hole and obliterating it with a single hoof.

However... with such a vast number of small black holes around, even at one stomp per hole, it would take some time to clear them all.

Moreover, the Heavenly Dao Molt Suns were not so easily obliterated.

After the small black holes were smashed, the mini-suns turned into rubble, which, after recombining and merging, would form an even larger “Heavenly Dao Molt Sun,” continuing to open black holes tenaciously.

[Now is the time, come out!]The Dark Giant issued a silent command to the ‘Dark Sun’ within the seal.

In fact, even without the Dark Giant’s silent instruction, the Dark Sun knew that its time of freedom had come—after ‘burdens’ were devoured by Tyrannical Song and Immortal White, the Dark Sun’s brain functioned more flexibly.

It actively began to break through the seal!

The Dark Giant assessed the situation in secret.

[More power is needed... it’s a pity, I had wanted to keep this trump card hidden and not expose it.]

But now, it was time to unveil it.

The body of Virtuous Daoist, burning with karmic flames, stepped forth, exposed in the vacuum.

Both the drama king horse and Senior White two’s golden thigh sensed each other’s presence instantly.

Between the three, there was a sense of resonance.

Both the drama king horse and the White two golden thigh paused momentarily.

And just at that moment, the body of Virtuous Daoist burst into Unknown White’s Sealing Array No. 1-33, breaking through all the way to Song Shuhang and White.

[What about taking this opportunity to blast this ‘beautiful troublemaker?]Such a thought flashed through the mind of the Dark Giant.

But that was all it was—a fleeting thought.

At the critical moment, it made the most correct decision—its goal was to rescue the ‘Dark Sun,’ and everything else could be put aside.

Virtuous Daoist threw a punch, aiming to smash at the Sealing World and help the Dark Sun break the seal.

Just then, the very ordinary-looking fellow suddenly appeared, stretching out his hand to execute the most basic fist technique, blocking Virtuous Daoist’s punch head-on!

Boom—fists collided.

[So reckless? Is he asking for death?]Though Virtuous Daoist’s body had lost its divinity and even the aura of immortality had faded, its constitution was still at an immortal level!

To the surprise of the Dark Giant, the very ordinary-looking fellow actually managed to withstand Virtuous Daoist’s punch!

Then, an intense ‘immortal’ radiance shone from the young man.

While not as advanced as true immortality, it was still a state of ‘sub-immortality.’

Most importantly, this person was not the Will of the Heavens.

Beneath the Will of the Heavens, this young man was supreme!

Chapter 3068: Chapter 3066: Outline Boxing Technique, I’m Fond of It!
I’ve lived so long but I’ve never seen anything like this!

On the surface, this indeed appears to be a human being. At the root, is it also a human?

But how could an ordinary human achieve this state—resisting the retired Will of the Heavens without having proved his Dao?

Other cultivators, even in their dreams, wouldn’t dare to conjure such an absurd fantasy.

Reality indeed is more ludicrous than dreams!

With such an entity present in the myriad practitioners in the universe, what’s the point in fighting in the Ninth Heavenly Dao’s battle for supremacy?

This fellow merely standing there, releasing his ‘Sub-immortal Data,’ is an incredibly powerful combination of ‘Information Interference Secret Method’ and ‘illusion spells’!

Immortals with insufficient comprehension skills, upon encountering this data, would immediately indulge in this ‘Sub-immortal State Information,’ unable to extricate themselves.

—Although it’s not like true immortality, which could allow the top Immortals to enter slumber. However, this ‘Sub-immortal State Information’ effortlessly distracts ordinary Immortals for a few minutes or even days.

A few minutes or even days are long enough for Immortals to accomplish much—A few minutes might not be enough to completely kill an Immortal, but certainly enough for a lucid Immortal to wash the face of another ‘information-interfered’ Immortal, apply some nice makeup, pick a good spot, prepare a specific seal, and thoroughly seal them away!

And this seal could additionally stack up to a hundred or more layers!

“This is not good news for me...” the Dark Giant felt an unusual agitation within.

If this fellow also participates in the battle for the Ninth Heavenly Dao when the reincarnation commences, he might secure the position in a very short period, leaving no room for others.

And since this fellow is already in a ‘Sub-immortal’ state, the speed of inheriting the Heavenly Dao might be very fast, leaving very little time for him to deploy the ‘Domination Secret Method.’

“Besides him, there are others... No, there are another thirty-four handsome fellows who have tricked me.”

The difficulty of manipulating the Ninth Heavenly Dao just rocketed to a nightmare level.

“No, I can’t let these two... these thirty-six guys continue like this.”

“I must find an opportunity, before the ninth reincarnation of the Heavenly Dao commences, to deal with them. Killing them is tough, but at least I could try to seal them for tens of thousands of years!”

He had already secretly calculated that the Ninth Heavenly Dao’s battle will definitely commence within ten thousand years!

“But now is not the time to tangle with this guy. The tactics of the Eighth Heavenly Dao can’t last long. The Heavenly Dao turning back might even suppress the virtue-cultivated body I now control.”

So, although it’s a pity... now is not a good time to target this fellow and the handsome trickster.

I can’t afford any more distractions now.

As these thoughts flashed through his mind, the Dark Giant, controlling the body of Daoist Priest Virtue, launched a knuckle of causality-reversing technique towards Song Shuhang.

The body of Daoist Priest Virtue, swiftly swung his fists toward Song Shuhang’s location, delivering tens of thousands of punches in an instant.

Each punch possessed the destructive power of creation, but because they were within the Sealing Array range of Unknown White No. 31, the punches’ power was heavily suppressed.

However, even suppressed, if any of these punches landed solidly, they could blast an Immortal into oblivion.

But...

The Daoist Priest Virtue seemed to be flailing wildly, some of these punches targeted Song Shuhang’s body, while others exploded around him. The trajectory of the fists resembled a massive cage, enveloping Song Shuhang within it.

Song Shuhang tried to dodge a few punches... and then he gave up.

His current ‘Tyrannical Song Skin + Tyrannical Song Bone’ had ascended to sublimation, but his flesh and organs had not yet completed reinforcement.

In terms of battle awareness, he couldn’t directly face a frontal assault from a “Heavenly Dao” level existence.

So after dodging a few punches initially, he just obediently put up all his defenses, protected his vital areas, and took the hits to the end.

Now that his “Tyrannical Song Skin” and “Tyrannical Song Bone” were immortalized, his ability to withstand hits was absolutely top-notch, and he couldn’t be killed in a short time.

Song Shuhang had prepared himself to endure a real beating.

However, ultimately, only one punch solidly hit his crossed arms, knocking him back a step... The damage from this punch was all blocked by his defense and Tyrannical Song Skin; other than &#@#%&#% Fairy being blown up, he didn’t sustain any actual harm to his bones.

The rest of the punches just whizzed past his body.

Song Shuhang was stunned, “Outline Boxing Technique?”

Did the Virtue giant on the other side have a curse of ‘difficulty hitting the enemy’?

Or perhaps... was he going easy?

Across from him, the body of Daoist Priest Virtue, having thrown the punches, couldn’t wait to rush towards the sealed world of the “Dark Sun.”

Senior White, Senior White Two, and the drama king White Horse hadn’t recovered from the ‘Resonance Reaction’ yet.

“If you want to break the seal, step over my body!” behind Song Shuhang, the Fairy that had just been blown up by a punch reassembled and recited the impassioned lines.

Song Shuhang also reacted quickly, taking a step forward.

But just as he took a step, many ‘fists’ suddenly came flying toward his body and face from the vacuum!

It was the ‘Outline Boxing Technique’ of the previous Daoist Priest Virtue!

After these fists were thrown, their destructive power was somehow set in the ‘vacuum,’ undispersed. As soon as Song Shuhang stepped forward, these ‘fists’ were triggered.

Song Shuhang’s body instinctively retreated back to its original position.

Those ‘Outline Boxing Technique’ fists again whistled past his body.

“This move is strong, and it feels like it matches well with my Heavenly Horse Style... Basic Boxing Skill·Two. This fist technique involves the power of karma, and what I am now condensing is the ‘Virtue + Karma’ path to immortality, what a coincidence!” These thoughts flashed through Song Shuhang’s mind.

As the thought arose, in his dantian, the fat whale golden core that had fused the ‘Virtuous Seed’ began to stir.

From the virtuous network, a part of the information about the ‘Outline Boxing Technique’ emerged, transmitting to Song Shuhang.

Simultaneously, the Sage Eye Golden Core in Song Shuhang’s external elixir field lit up, working with the virtuous network to analyze the data from the recent ‘Outline Boxing Technique.’

From today onwards, any fist technique used against Tyrannical Song once, as long as it wasn’t too complex and matched Tyrannical Song’s attributes, could very likely become Tyrannical Song’s fist technique!

Besides his astonishing saber techniques, Tyrannical Song’s innate skill for fist techniques was actually not bad either.

Meanwhile.

Seizing this slight time difference, Daoist Priest Virtue’s body finally successfully blasted open the seal of the ‘Dark Sun’s small world.’

The Dark Sun, already ready, coordinated with the breaking of the seal to emerge!

Freedom at last!

The Dark Sun, which had been tormented by Immortal White and Tyrannical Song for several days, felt as if it was in a dream.

Chapter 3069: Chapter 3067: Become the Strongest Tool Person!

After the seal was broken, Dark Sun had originally wanted to say a few words to Tyrannical Song and Immortal White — those who had not experienced its situation could not possibly imagine how it had felt these past few days being jointly attacked with “Joint Attack” by Immortal White and Tyrannical Song.

It was a double strike, both psychologically and physically!

However, Daoist Priest Virtue’s body did not give it the time, directly pulling it up, tearing open space, and escaping into it, vanishing without a trace.

Neat and tidy!

And almost at the exact moment Dark Sun and the body of Daoist Priest Virtue disappeared, Daozi’s will crossed the void and arrived.

But it was already a step too late.

Looking at the already destroyed Sealing World, Daozi clenched his fist, “I’ve been outmaneuvered.”

After all, he was a genuine scholar, and he could not compare to the successive Heavenly Daos in terms of cunning tactics.

Just how many contingencies the successive Heavenly Daos had arranged within the ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ before their retirement, was truly unknown to anyone.

“Rescued, huh,” Senior White slightly smiled and said.

“Senior White’s smile, I shall protect it!” the virtuous lamia, having just resurrected her head, rushed to steal the line, leaving Tyrannical Song speechless.

Daozi was startled, “???”

In Fellow Daoist White’s smile, there seemed to be a reassuring power.

Daozi, who was originally frustrated from being outmaneuvered, instantly calmed down.

Suddenly, he was struck by the thought and emotion that even if Dark Sun was rescued, it was no big deal.

Could it be... Fellow Daoist White had already perceived it and made arrangements and preparations?

Otherwise, for someone capable of obliterating the myriad practitioners in the universe to break free, Fellow Daoist White should not be so composed.

“Right, Confucian Daoist, have you researched something called the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’?” Senior White’s second golden thigh suddenly asked.

Daozi nodded his head, “Yes, I wanted to study how to reverse the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’, so after returning to the Heavenly Dao dimension, I tried to research the rudimentary form of the Stellar Destruction Virus... but I failed.”

“If you have already begun researching, then it’s a bit troublesome,” Senior White’s second golden thigh said, “We probably have to start preparing for the transfer of the Heavenly Dao in advance.”

Having said that much, Senior Daozi immediately understood, “That ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ manufacturing scheme, was it a trap in itself? Even for the body of the Heavenly Dao, would there be problems as soon as one begins researching—whether reversing or normal—the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’?”

Senior White’s second golden thigh replied, “Yes, whether it’s reversing the research or conducting it normally, as soon as one starts to interact with the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’, they will be affected. If it’s a complete Heavenly Dao, this influence might be negligible. But...”

“But I am only an 8.5 term Heavenly Dao.” Daozi understood, which meant that the effect on him could potentially become magnified.

A virus that would at most cause a minor cold in a complete Heavenly Dao might be fatal to him.

[Was it a trap the moment the top half of the original template for the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’ was handed to me?]

“Senior White, where did you get this information?” Song Shuhang asked, puzzled.

How did it feel like Senior White had suddenly gained a lot more ‘knowledge’ and become suddenly erudite about the ‘Stellar Destruction Virus’?

“I’ve just recharged,” replied Senior White as the golden thigh two.

Upon hearing this, Song Shuhang seemed thoughtful, then he turned his head to look at Senior White and the theatrical horse, “Are Senior White and Senior Ma also...?”

“Mm-hmm,” replied Senior White.

“I see,” said Song Shuhang, nodding—was it due to the body of Daoist Priest Virtue? The reaction that the body gave when it last saw Senior White was considerable.

“I was hoping... that at least while serving in my position, I would do my best to resolve this catastrophe,” Senior Daozi sighed.

His generation all had a nature hardened by hardships. They always hoped to shoulder the hard and exhausting work themselves, allowing the next generation to enjoy their blessings.

“Don’t worry, Senior Daozi. You’ve already done very well,” Song Shuhang consoled: “If it weren’t for your support, perhaps the myriad practitioners in the universe would’ve already met their end.”

This was no exaggeration!

“So, moving on... I will first arrange for my revival in the identity of ‘Chief Disciple of Confucianism.’ After I resurrect, all my memories and experiences regarding the Will of the Heavens might be completely erased. Before that happens, I’ll try my best to give you another push,” Daozi said, pointing at himself, “You need more ‘eternity data,’ don’t you?”

“It’s pointless, Senior Daozi. You’re currently in the true ‘Heavenly Axiom-level’ state. Even if Senior White and I jointly attack, we won’t be able to obtain ‘eternity’ data from you,” said Song Shuhang.

“Moreover, you don’t have to worry, Senior Daozi. I still have the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ and Senior Three-Eyes’ ‘big-eyed planet,’ two primordial treasures. Just give me some time, with the aid of these treasures, I will be able to completely transform the flesh and blood in my body into ‘Sub-immortal’ state.”

The sheep that was the Dark Sun had run away, but he could still acquire wool from other sources.

Full-Body Semi-Immortalization wasn’t a difficult task for him.

Father Goudan was taken aback: “!!!”

Can Semi-Immortalization work on flesh and blood in addition to skin and bones?

Senior White reminded, “Just now, I’ve sent a question on how to achieve Shuhang’s Semi-Immortalization using the power of theprimordial treasures without damaging them to the research group for everyone to discuss.”

On hearing this, Senior Daozi nodded approvingly.

Once Tyrannical Song achieves Full-Body Semi-Immortalization, there would be no accidents for the next Heavenly Will.

Even if something as unexpected as the fat ball popped up like the previous Heavenly Will, with Tyrannical Song’s state, he could grind down the opposition!

Senior Daozi continued, “The aid I’m going to give you isn’t the ‘Semi-Immortalization’ part. I’m considering, when I retire... leaving you a powerful external computational core. It will match your ‘Semi-Immortal’ body’s capability with calculation ability.”

Unlike the previous Heavenly Wills, Senior Daozi felt that if he were to retire, he probably couldn’t leave behind a ‘Body of Eternity’ and might end up like the fat ball, collapsing completely, or even merging into the ‘Will of the Heavens.’

Therefore, he wanted to maximize the use of this ‘Body of Eternity’ and ‘Heavenly Dao Authority’ to become the ultimate tool-person.

“An external calculator? That can be done?” asked the three-eyed young senior.

“Tyrannical Song’s body has the ‘undying fat whale golden core,’ which is fully capable of withstanding a portion of the calculation strain at the Heavenly Axiom level... Sub-Heavenly Dao level calculations. Moreover, as the Eighth and a half Heavenly Dao, I also have some unique aspects. I got into my position by exploiting a BUG in the ‘Completion Plan’ of the Eighth Heavenly Dao. So when I leave my position, I should be able to similarly leave something behind through another BUG exploit,” said Senior Daozi calmly.

According to the ‘Completion Plan’ of the liquefied metal ball, after the Great Dao of the ancient Heavenly City is complete, it will definitely expel some ‘residuals’ to prevent them from affecting the ‘perfect’ Heavenly Dao Authority.

And this function of expelling ‘residuals’ can be utilized.

Chapter 3070: Chapter 3068: I’ll Wait for You in the Distant Future, Senior Song!

“Before stepping down, I will focus on researching how to package the ‘Heavenly Dao’s Calculation Ability’ into an innate ability, and then, through the ‘impurity expulsion’ channel previously set up by the liquefied metal ball, I will produce this ‘Calculation Ability Compression Package’ before my resignation and hand it over to Shuhang,” Daozi shared his idea in the ‘research group’.

Heavenly Emperor’s Son: “...”

The ‘impurity expulsion’ channel set up by the liquefied metal ball, it wouldn’t be her who was supposed to be expelled, would it?

I can’t help but feel a little wronged.

“Daozi, you focus on tackling the issue of the ‘Heavenly Dao Level Compression Package’. We can’t help much with this research,” suggested the three-eyed young senior. “Shall we just focus on the study of ‘primordial treasures’ instead? Any other issues?”

Song Shuhang hastily spoke up, “Seniors, there’s another matter here that requires your technical support. This also relates to the Dark Sun... I’ve discovered there’s a ‘pulling the strings’ behind the ‘Dark Sun’, for now let’s call it the ‘Dark Giant’. Earlier, I managed to scrounge an interesting secret technique, the ‘Domination Secret Method’, from it through a dreamland technique. I want to ask the seniors to help me simplify the process.”

Well, it would be best if we could reduce it to the complexity of around three formation runes. And if possible, the time to accumulate mental energy must be shortened. Otherwise, just accumulating energy would take tens of millions of years, what use would that be?

Subsequently, Song Shuhang recounted in detail to the ‘research group’ the hidden enmity between the ‘Dark Giant’ and past Heavenly Daos.

After hearing Song Shuhang’s narrative, the members of the group fell silent for quite a while.

After a long time, Heavenly Emperor’s Son spoke up, “I don’t even know what to say about this guy, pretty unlucky, huh.”

This is the first time she’d seen a villainous boss so pitiful.

“It could also be because Fellow Daoist White is just too lucky,” Father Goudan reminded.

“My teacher is also awesome,” added Daozi.

Song Shuhang: “...”

Senior White two: “Anyway, focus on the main point. The key is that when the Ninth Heavenly Dao comes around, this guy will come out again to offer someone the ‘Domination Secret Method’, right?”

“Absolutely. Whether it’s Fellow Daoist White or Shuhang who takes office, he won’t miss this opportunity,” the three-eyed young senior stated.

The ‘Dark Giant’ is truly pitiful. He has methods, strategies, patience, and he’s cautious enough. But he could never have imagined that his hidden plans would be thoroughly exposed by Song Shuhang through a dreamland skill, and even the ‘Domination Secret Method’ was plundered by Tyrannical Song.

“This Domination Secret Method might be of use to us,” said the main world’s White after a brief contemplation. “If we are to take the final step of ‘two different entities proving their Dao simultaneously,’ we might need to use this ‘Domineering Secret Method’ to perfect the last link.”

He and Song Shuhang had already absorbed a portion of each other’s existence, theoretically meeting the condition for ‘different entities proving Dao simultaneously.’

However, if they could supplement each other with a ‘Domination Secret Method’ in the instant before proving their Dao, they could make their connection more stable and ensure a smooth process.

“That means we need to decipher the ‘Domination Secret Method,’ and we also have to come up with a solution to counteract its effects to avoid falling into the ‘Dark Giant’s’ trap,” Father Goudan proposed after pondering for a moment. “In that case, let’s start with ‘absorbing the energy of the Dark Giant’s Domination Secret Method.’ When the Ninth Heavenly Dao segment arrives and he casts the secret technique on Shuhang or Fellow Daoist White, we’ll absorb and transform the ‘secret technique,’ turning it into energy for us to use when we cast the ‘Domination Secret Method’.”

The Domination Secret Method requires gathering the power of tens of millions of years before each casting.

Such power can’t come from nothing...

There’s only one solution—borrow and utilize force, absorbing and transforming the ‘Dark Giant’s tens of millions of years of secret technique energy.’

Killing two birds with one stone.

“Father Goudan, you truly are worthy of being the ruler of the Netherworld, such a dirty mind,” the three-eyed young senior taunted.

Father Goudan: “...”

Isn’t your alpaca the ruler of the Netherworld?

Is it fun to hurt oneself in the process of defeating the enemy?

Hmm... it really does seem quite interesting!

“So, I’ll leave the Domination Secret Technique, research on primordial treasures, and the Heavenly Dao Calculation Compression Package to the seniors. Right now, I’ll focus on perfecting the ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path.’” Song Shuhang summarized.

With his body’s ‘Sub-immortal Transformation’ and continuous insights from the Immortals flowing back to him, Song Shuhang clearly sensed his progress bar on the ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ rapidly filling up.

He estimated that once he completed the immortalization of his flesh through the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ and the ‘big-eyed planet’, he could then sacrifice his ‘light of virtue and karmic immortal path’ within him, and take the final step in ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’!

Using the ‘immortal information’ left by different Heavenly Daos to enrich his ‘Sub-immortal State’ was indeed the correct choice—the ‘immortal information’ from various sources was the greatest aid in perfecting his ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’!

By then, his ‘Cultivation Chat Immortal Path’ would integrate the strengths of a hundred paths, amalgamating the ‘immortal information’ left by past Heavenly Daos, to forge the mightiest path to immortality!

...

...

Main World.

The New Year feast had ended several days ago.

But the members of the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ hadn’t dispersed yet... at the moment, most of them were passed out within the Main World.

A few clear-headed and reliable group members were responsible for taking care of the intoxicated ones.

Due to the lack of helping hands, this time even little Li Yinzhu was assisting.

“What exactly did the seniors drink this time? Why is it so potent?” Loli Zhu said, her gaze involuntarily drifting towards the side of the wine jar.

There was still a small amount of wine left in the jar, emitting an enticing aroma.

If not for Loli Shi keeping an eye on her, the curious Zhu might have already sneaked up and sneakily licked it.

“A part of it was brought by the seniors themselves, and another part... seems to have been brought out by the ‘Inner World Assistant’? Was it Mister Song’s private collection?” Loli Shi recalled.

The Inner World Assistant blinked its eyes—ah, that part of the wine was indeed brought over from Lady Kunna.

During the banquet when they were running low on wine, it went back to the Dragon Network World and brought some over.

“I wonder how Mister Song’s progress is coming along?” Soft Feather sat on a branch, leaning against the trunk, her legs gently swinging.

In her hand, she held a jade wine plate.

She gracefully pinched the wine plate and took a delicate sip.

“Things will change, right? Everything will get even better, right? This is the one past that Senior White never left behind,” she said, raising her head and looking up.

Detach yourself, Mister Song.

Surpass everything, no longer bound by time, space, or dimension.

And then... I’ll wait for you in the distant future.
