“This should be my last visit to this time-space node, and I’m afraid I won’t be able to see how the future unfolds from here on... I really wish I had a few more opportunities to come here... at least to see Senior Song safely prove his Dao.”

“Sometimes, I wonder if I’m dreaming, if the me in the dream is desperately changing the past, changing everyone’s past. But when I wake up, the future remains unchanged.” Soft Feather’s lips left the rim of the wine cup.

Merely changing the past cannot change the future.

She was beginning to struggle to hold on.

But fortunately, this time she finally saw a glimmer of hope.

“Only after reaching the ‘transcendence’ mentioned in the information from Senior White, the Wielder of the Will, no longer limited by time, space, dimensions, and everything else, is it possible to twist all of the past, present, and future together.”

Senior Song here is more lively than ever, bouncing around, even though a salted fish, he is spirited and causes mischief.

Those who cause mischief usually die quickly... but as long as they don’t die, they become legendary figures!

So, Senior Song will become a true legend.

The wine was personally blended by Lady Kunna, far more potent than the legendary Immortal Wine. Any more and she might just fall asleep on the spot.

And even though she was being very restrained, Soft Feather was slightly tipsy.

“I’ll stay a little longer.” She leaned against the tree, softly humming a short melody.

For some reason, as long as she stayed at this time-space node, her mood would lighten.

She looked at the Senior members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group who were drunk in the distance, familiar yet strange.

It made her reluctant to leave.

If she could choose... she would want this moment to last forever.

After a long while.

Soft Feather slowly closed her eyes, the elegance about her gradually fading.

Intoxication flushed her cheeks red as she leaned against the trunk and fell asleep.

...

...

In the main world, inside a resting palace in a fragment of the ancient Heavenly City.

Sixteen struggled to push Su Clan’s Seven, who still wanted more drink, back to bed.

“Should we tie up Seven?” suggested the ghost spirit fairy maiden from within.

“No need, she’s already asleep,” said Sixteen with a sweet smile.

Then, she stood up, pushed open the palace gate, and gazed into the distance... immediately spotting Soft Feather sleeping on the tree branch.

“It’s the normal Soft Feather now,” the ghost spirit fairy maiden said.

You couldn’t tell the difference from the outside.

But from her ‘aura,’ one could determine if it was the normal Soft Feather or not.

“Yeah, Future Child must have left already. To be honest, the future Soft Feather really moves my heart,” Sixteen confessed sincerely.

The Soft Feather of the future is much more threatening than the current one...

The elegance in her very bones, and the occasional sorrowful expression in her brows made even Sixteen’s heart stir—if it wasn’t for Song Shuhang, she would be willing to choose Soft Feather as her dao companion, no joke.

“She is indeed moving... Wait, this sort of heart movement isn’t right, we must have been influenced by Fairy Cheng Lin,” the ghost spirit fairy maiden hastily interjected.

A moment later, she added, “Moreover, I think you need to be concerned about yourself. We are bound by a contract, and I can clearly feel something is off with you. I’ve finally made up my mind to align with you; you better not have any issues.”

“My condition is actually just... my time as the auxiliary consciousness has come, and soon I’ll switch to running in the background. Then, the real Sixteen will be switched back. Don’t worry, the fully restored me will have all the memories and emotions. The real me has always been operating in the background, there’s no real difference between us. Senior Sister Ye Si, you don’t need to worry about any mishaps,” Sixteen explained.

Ghost Spirit Fairy Maiden: “...”

You personalities are such players. Last time, I heard you mention that you wanted to restore the real Sixteen. Has it been ongoing in the background all this time?

Su Clan’s Sixteen smiled as she opened an umbrella, took a light leap, and jumped onto the rooftop of the Heavenly Palace Fragment, sprinting across it toward the depths of the main world.

The Inner World Assistant appeared before her, floating and silently guiding her way.

The place they were heading to was Song Shuhang’s treasure trove.

In the main world, the Inner World Assistant had a clear record of all the treasures Song Shuhang had hidden.

If Song Shuhang needed to use them when spending money on upgrades, she could dig them up immediately.

However... the place she was taking Su Clan’s Sixteen to was not a common treasure.

It was a safety measure once left behind for Song Shuhang by ‘Song Wood’.

“Once the real me fully recovers, that thin-skinned, proud character will come back. The real me would never do something bold. So before the assistive personality switches to the background, I want to do something big for my main body!” The ‘Tyrannical Song’s heart’ in Su Clan’s Sixteen’s chest began to beat powerfully.

Clearly, she was not as bold as she claimed to be; she was equally nervous at this moment.

As she ran... scenes from the past surfaced in her mind.

Last year, after Sixteen formally began the ‘Spirit River Su Clan Trial’, a copy of her personality with most of Sixteen’s memories was born.

When this personality was first created, it was like a blank slate.

‘Memories’ for her felt more like watching a very long movie—part of her character setting, somewhat illusory, not quite real.

Among them, the memories of interacting with Song Shuhang left a deeper impression on her—these were the most recent memories and parts of Sixteen’s life where her emotions were the most volatile.

Add to that, during the secluded meditation, Song Shuhang had Su Clan’s Seven send the ‘skeletal dragon’s withered vine’ to assist her.

So, the pure and blank slate she was began to look forward to the end of her secluded meditation, to meet the ‘Song Shuhang’ from her memories.

Several months later, she came out of secluded meditation.

She felt somewhat apprehensive.

The actual first encounter... happened after she was tricked away by Senior Dharma King Creation at the end of a live broadcast.

It was raining.

She held an umbrella and walked toward the passenger transport center.

At that time, she did not know that Song Shuhang had quietly come over to pick her up—because according to the chat records in the Nine Provinces Number One Group, Shuhang should have been in space, having been launched there by Senior White.

The rain grew heavier.

She thought about how to meet ‘Song Shuhang’ in the future, and was slightly distracted.

Under the eaves in the distance,

A big fellow leaned against the wall, his body soaked by the rain, every breath turning into mist.

All of a sudden, this big fellow jumped out.

It startled her.

Without recognizing who it was, she instinctively gave him a palm strike.

It wasn’t until after he was sent flying, letting out an ‘ahhh~ah’ scream,

That she truly met ‘Song Shuhang’ for the first time, in the true sense of the word.

He was more interesting than the ‘memory,’ and had changed a lot.

But he was more real and tangible.

At that moment, Song Shuhang became more than just a character from her memories; he was a real entity to her.

“`

After the Inner World Assistant took Sixteen far away...

In the grass near the ‘living spring’ in the main world, Steel Song Shuhang’s manifestation calmly climbed out, brushing off the grass clippings from his body.

“Were you hiding from Sixteen?” Pavilion Master Chu swam to the shore, crossed her arms, rested on the edge, and asked, “Is Sixteen off to find something?”

“If I’m not mistaken, she should be looking for a treasure that would make the Goudan family flourish. So, to avoid the embarrassment of her meeting me, I decided to hide for a bit,” the steel manifestation replied.

At the same time, he synchronized this scene with his main body.

In fact, everything in the main world couldn’t escape Song Shuhang’s observation. Even the guidance offered by the Inner World Assistant was tacitly approved by Shuhang.

“Youth is wonderful...” Pavilion Master Chu sighed softly, “If I had been so impulsive in my youth, I wouldn’t have ended up like I am now.”

Steel manifestation subconsciously wanted to voice its support for Pavilion Master Chu—but then it suddenly remembered that ‘Song Wood’ was petty ghost spirit number one, instantly feeling a pang of guilt, he dared not continue this topic to avoid drawing fire upon itself.

“Since you don’t oppose it yourself, I’m going to lend Sixteen a helping hand.” At this moment, the voice of The White Dragon suddenly sounded behind Steel Song Shuhang’s manifestation.

The already sheepish steel manifestation felt even more uneasy upon hearing The White Dragon’s voice.

The figure of The White Dragon slowly appeared with the sound, coiling above the steel manifestation’s head.

“Good evening, The White Dragon. By the way, hasn’t your fleshly body resurrected yet?” the steel manifestation looked up at The White Dragon and asked.

At this moment, The White Dragon still appeared in a state similar to a ‘body of virtue’.

“No rush, it will come back to life when it’s time to resurrect,” The White Dragon swam around in the vacuum before looking at Pavilion Master Chu in the living spring, “You should be almost fully grown, right, Slow-Witted Song?”

“Just the calves left,” replied Pavilion Master Chu lazily.

“Once you’re fully grown, where do you plan to go? Will you start rebuilding your Crystal-clear Water Pavilion?” The White Dragon asked calmly.

Pavilion Master Chu leaned on the shore, shook her head, and said leisurely, “The obsession with Crystal-clear Water Pavilion was given to Chu Two when the path of immortality was divided. I will not rebuild an illusory Crystal-clear Water Pavilion again.”

Illusory things are, after all, illusory.

The current Pavilion Master Chu, with realistic hopes, naturally wouldn’t reconstruct an illusory Crystal-clear Water Pavilion.

“So, are you saying that when you are fully reborn, you will have nothing to do? Then, would you like to accompany me to the ‘Dragon Realm’ to find a treasure that could speed up Song Wood’s recovery?” The White Dragon made an invitation.

The sheepish manifestation quietly recoiled inside—Fairy Cheng Lin and Song Wood self-ruptured to buy time. Unexpectedly, The White Dragon had a way to hasten Song Wood’s recovery?

“I’ll pass... I think I’ll soak in the living spring of the main world for a while longer,” Pavilion Master Chu said with a slight grin, “The Dragon Realm is your hometown; I’m afraid if I go there, I might end up being suppressed.”

The White Dragon rolled her eyes, “Am I that kind of dragon?”

As the conversation didn’t go smoothly, The White Dragon turned and veiled towards Sixteen’s last seen direction.

After The White Dragon left...

Pavilion Master Chu looked at Steel Song Shuhang and asked, “What do you plan to do about Tyrannical Saber Song One?”

Steel manifestation: “!!!”

“Don’t be stunned; my dazed hair has always been rooted at the top of your head. Some things can be inferred through numerous clues. Don’t underestimate a woman’s intuition,” Pavilion Master Chu said slowly.

“Actually, the plan for dealing with Tyrannical Saber Song One... has already come out, hasn’t it?” the steel manifestation tried to remain calm, then he looked towards where Sixteen and The White Dragon disappeared, “I will inherit a portion of Song Wood’s karma. One of his obsessions I will fulfill for him. As for other karmic bonds, he can solve them himself after he’s born.”

If the obsessions and sorrows of Pavilion Master Chu and the Crystal-clear Water Pavilion cannot be saved, Song Shuhang will resolve them.

The other consequences can wait for ten months.

Pavilion Master Chu rubbed her temples—do you really plan to give birth to him?

How will we face you then?

You might as well have him go through Mama Song’s way.

“My main body is going to start touching on ‘primordial treasures,’ so this side is going to enter standby mode... Senior Chu, talk to you later,” the steel manifestation waved at Pavilion Master Chu and then actively shut down its power.

Pavilion Master Chu like a mermaid retreated a distance, leisurely began blowing bubbles.

“`

“`

...

Meanwhile.

Inside the Heavenly Dao Time Secret Realm.

Senior White, Immortal White Two, Senior Three Eyes, Father Goudan, and a group of members had already preliminarily worked out a plan to use the “primordial treasure” to perfect Song Shuhang’s “Sub-immortalization.”

The process for “Sub-immortalization” was laid out; the main objective this time was to achieve it “without damaging the primordial treasure,” so progress was swift.

Currently, they were preparing for the first experiment.

“Should we start with the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber or the big-eyed planet?” Song Shuhang’s main body returned from the “fellow daoists’ discussion” to the research room, ready to become the experiment subject.

Father Goudan answered, “Let’s start with the big-eyed planet. The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber is actually a bit special... It’s not only a primordial treasure but also part of the plan for the Heavenly Dragon to free itself. So, let’s collect some data from the ‘big-eyed planet’ experiment first.”

“What does Senior Three Eyes think?” Song Shuhang asked.

“That works for me. I have no objections,” the three-eyed young senior nodded.

Immortal White Two, Golden Thigh, said, “Then do we need to move the test site? If I remember correctly, that big-eyed planet is quite large.”

At the time, he had his eye on the big-eyed planet and had wanted to capture it.

“Let’s go,” Senior White said as he pushed open a spatial passage, leading straight to the location of the ‘big-eyed planet.’

At the moment, the primordial treasure ‘big-eyed planet’ was anxiously serving as the ‘Cultivator Chat System client downloader.’

It did not yet know when it would be freed.

The big-eyed planet was also in despair.

What made it even more desperate was the fact that its ruler of the Netherworld, Old Lord Two, was obviously showing favoritism towards Tyrannical Song.

What was so good about Tyrannical Song? Were his eyes as cute as its own?

While it was pondering, suddenly the ‘big-eyed planet’ sensed a formidable enemy’s presence—it was the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber!

It instinctively wanted to rise up and confront the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

But the next instant, it also sensed that Old Lord Two of the Netherworld had crossed the spatial passages and arrived.

“Cooperate with Tyrannical Song,” the three-eyed young senior commanded.

The big-eyed planet blinked its cute eyes.

Its enemy was jumping around on it, yet it was helpless... It even had to cooperate with another enemy, Tyrannical Song.

What kind of tricks had Tyrannical Song used to bewitch its Old Lord?

Perhaps it should take this opportunity to secretly observe Tyrannical Song.

“So, let’s begin the first experiment... Who will record the process?” Father Goudan’s voice rang out.

The son of the Heavenly Emperor raised his hand, “I’ll do it. I seem to be the most suitable one present.”

Song Shuhang squatted down, placing his hands on the ‘big-eyed planet,’ and said, “I never imagined we would have a day of deep cooperation.”

The big-eyed planet: “...”

Song Shuhang maintained his squatting posture, his glassy eyes, the third divine eye on his forehead, and the Sage Eye Golden Core from the imitation Dragon Network system all began to shine brightly.

At the same time, his hands quietly lit up.

[Although I hate to admit it... I have to acknowledge that his various eyes are pretty.]

After seeing these beautiful eyes, the big-eyed planet’s aversion towards Tyrannical Song slightly decreased.

It even developed a bit of a favorable impression towards him.

—This must be out of respect for the ‘pretty eyes!’ The big-eyed planet thought to itself.

“Very well, so far, using Senior Tyrannical Song’s demonic technique to start things off and improve the synchronization rate seems to be the right choice,” the son of the Heavenly Emperor nodded and made a note of this.

“`

“However, the synchronization rate between the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber and Tyrannical Song was already quite high, so it’s recommended to enter the ‘human-saber fusion’ state when the time comes.” Father Goudan’s voice sounded.

“Continue.” The three-eyed young senior instructed.

Song Shuhang nodded, his ‘Hand of Tyrannical Song’ continued to swiftly flash over the body of the ‘big-eyed planet’.

About half an hour later.

The entire colossal ‘big-eyed planet’ began to light up, showing signs that the originally cold holy light was about to transform into a warm holy light, almost becoming a sun-like attack.

The Tyrannical Song of today was no longer the same as before. Every demonic technique he unleashed could spread across the entire ‘planet,’ and after a whole half an hour, even a primordial treasure would react.

Not to mention, the ‘big-eyed planet’ was actively relaxing under the orders of Senior Three-Eyed, cooperating with Song Shuhang.

The first step of the experiment went perfectly.

Big-eyed planet: “???”

My body feels so strange!

“About there, what do you think, Senior White?” The son of the Heavenly Emperor estimated.

Senior White casually tossed a coin.

The coin landed on the back of his hand.

It showed heads.

Senior White nodded in satisfaction, “Heads.”

“Then Senior Song, we can proceed to the next phase,” the son of the Heavenly Emperor said to Song Shuhang.

Only after becoming friends with Senior White would one experience his handiness!

Moreover, the experience is even better after becoming friends with both Tyrannical Song and Immortal White.

“Huu~” Song Shuhang took a deep breath, then used the innate ability of a Confucian Sage towards the ‘big-eyed planet.’

The big-eyed planet suddenly sensed an immense crisis.

It quivered, trying to shake off Tyrannical Song.

“Don’t move.” The three-eyed young senior commanded.

The big-eyed planet master could only stop reluctantly.

Woosh~

The innate ability of a Confucian Sage moved over the ‘big-eyed planet’ and cut off a ‘portio’ of ‘existence,’ bringing it back to Song Shuhang.

The next step was the most crucial.

After retrieving his innate ability... Song Shuhang did not directly absorb the ‘existence.’ Instead, he allowed this ‘existence’ to make a brief appearance in his energy system.

Then, he returned the ‘existence’ in perfect condition, sending it back.

Feeling that a part of its ‘existence’ had returned, the big-eyed planet let out a sigh of relief.

Above it, Song Shuhang closed his eyes in concentration, while the immortal energy within him surged and circulated.

“How does it feel?” asked Senior White’s legs.

A moment later.

Song Shuhang opened his eyes and nodded, “It’s feasible, but the efficiency isn’t very high.”

This efficiency couldn’t compare to when he and Senior White had executed a Joint Attack against the ‘Dark Sun.’

“Then let’s try Plan 2 and enter synchronization mode,” the three-eyed young senior suggested.

He had cast so many phases of the Saber-Nurturing Technique just for this moment.

Song Shuhang adjusted his consciousness, beginning to resonate with the big-eyed planet in a ‘human-artifact familiar feeling.’

Big-eyed planet: “!!!”

You actually want to enter a ‘human-artifact fusion’ state with me?

How preposterous!

The state of human-artifact fusion is not something you can just enter by saying so!

Although I agreed to cooperate with you completely under the orders of Lord Two of the Netherworld, your compatibility with me is nonexistent, we simply can’t achieve human-artifact fusion!

Just as the big-eyed planet was pondering this, suddenly... it found that it had lost control over its body.

It was the three-eyed young senior who had used his authority to take over the ‘big-eyed planet,’ and then he personally took the initiative to sync with Song Shuhang.

Big-eyed planet: “...”

This is too difficult.

Having a lord who bends the elbow outwards is too challenging.

A few breaths later.

Under the guidance of the experienced three-eyed young senior, Song Shuhang successfully entered resonance mode with the ‘big-eyed planet.’

Next, the fat whale golden core dove into the body of the big-eyed planet, setting up a layer of ‘Immortal Defense.’

Song Shuhang’s main body once again started to energetically apply the Sage’s talent to the ‘big-eyed planet.’

This was essentially copying the model used previously against the ‘Dark Sun.’

“How’s the effect?” Senior White inquired.

“The effect of a single application is weaker than Plan 1. However... it has the advantage of process simplification, eliminating the need to swallow ‘existence’ and then return it. That is to say, Plan 2 allows for rapid experience gain. As long as the hand speed is fast enough, the overall effect is much better than Plan 1,” Song Shuhang calculated and replied.

“Then we’ll go with Plan 2.” Senior White nodded, “Do you need me to help you execute a Joint Attack?”

“Let’s try, but Senior White, don’t activate the ‘immortality’ attribute during the spellcasting process,” Song Shuhang nodded.

And so...

The familiar scene unfolded once more.

AFK, enlightenment, understanding Sub-immortalization...

The big-eyed planet master remained silent.

It quietly observed the ‘undying fat whale golden core.’

Tyrannical Song had actually come up with such a thing?

So now if it went head-to-head with Tyrannical Song, it might be blown up by him?

Just a few months ago, from several planes away, it could blast Tyrannical Song to bits with a distant strike.

Now, as fate would have it, a head-on confrontation could see it being the one defeated.

Is this the heartless march of time?

Several hours later...

“It’s done.” Song Shuhang stopped the enlightenment process.

He opened his eyes.

This time, his eyes, third eye, Sage Eye Golden Core... everything on him related to eyes began to undergo Sub-immortalization.

The moment all the ‘eyes’ completed their Sub-immortal transformation, Song Shuhang faintly felt as if he had seen some images.

With the current ‘him’ and the Netherworld’s ‘Dark Song’ as nodes.

Using all the Sub-immortally transformed eyes and the big-eyed planet as tools.

Song Shuhang vaguely saw the river of time.

Unlike the Time River in my cognition, composed of ‘past, present, future.’

This time, what he saw was a ‘Time River’ that spread out like a sea urchin ball, with himself and Dark Song as the nodes.

“Is this thing the Time River? Or is it a time sea urchin?”

Song Shuhang was also puzzled in his heart.

But precisely at this moment, he could clearly understand that this urchin-like, sea-urchin-shaped thing was the Time River!

To understand is to understand, without even a reason why.

It’s just too vague...

Even if he strained all his ‘Sub-Immortal’ eyeballs, it still felt like looking at flowers through fog, like being severely nearsighted.

“Perhaps, I need a lens?”

While thinking this, Song Shuhang tried several more times, not willing to give up just yet.

But no matter how he operated his abilities, the limit of what Sub-Immortal eyes could see was only this much.

“If it’s just like this... it’s completely meaningless.”

Explaining things seen in a fog could only be done by one’s own imagination, or by wild guessing; it’s as unreliable as a low-end divination.

After having executed all of his meager methods, Song Shuhang finally gave up.

For now, it seems that being able to see a mosaic version of a sea urchin ball-shaped Time River is the limit of a ‘mortal’ like himself.

If he wanted to see more and further, he must ascend another level or rely on some other external force.

Depending on external forces is not something to be ashamed of.

Just like how humans became the top of the food chain after learning to use various tools, external forces can make one stronger.

In this regard, Tyrannical Song’s thoughts were especially clear.

As if sensing his thought... at his waist, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber vibrated slightly.

Although it too was a primordial treasure, unlike the ‘big-eyed planet,’ the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber needed to be refined by one generation of ‘Fourth Cultivator of True Virtue’ after another, undergoing the Eighth Revolution before it could achieve perfect form.

Moreover, it was also the ‘escape plan’ of the Wielder of the Will Striped Dragon. The third-generation Heavenly Dao was able to free itself from the Heavenly Dao seat with its help.

This time, the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber took the initiative to chime, urging Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang’s thought moved.

He laid his hand on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, and with a slide, a thousand cycles of the Saber-Nurturing Technique fell—incidentally, he didn’t play favorites, as his other hand also delivered a thousand cycles to Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword.

One must not forget old friends.

One can’t forget the old saber when a new one comes along.

In the next moment, the three of them entered the supreme saber mode of ‘human-saber fusion’ with practiced ease.

The saber is me, I am the saber, and still, I am me.

Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

What are you doing? Why drag me into it again?

Haven’t you seen how silent I’ve been today?

All the high-level events that occurred today felt out of its league.

As a ‘divine weapon,’ it felt like it had no place to intervene.

So unusually for today, it maintained silence, not even jabbing at Shuhang’s heart.

But when it came to a critical moment, Shuhang wouldn’t let it be, insisting on including it in the ‘human-saber fusion’ with the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber.

Now, Tyrannical Song was simultaneously in ‘human-saber fusion’ with two weapons, which was frankly terrible.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword panicked, “My instinct tells me that the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber needs your assistance right now.” Song Shuhang’s thought came through.

In human-saber fusion state, thoughts and spirit were in unison.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s inner complaints would also be reflected back to Song Shuhang.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber had not yet completed its final refinement, so it needed external assistance to activate certain functions.

At this moment, the best help for the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber from Song Shuhang was none other than Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword who was also a ‘saber’.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber thrummed excitedly, seemingly agreeing with Tyrannical Song’s statement.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

Well, considering the pleasurable one thousand casts of the Saber-Nurturing Technique just now, it wouldn’t stand idly by if it needed to help later.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword asked, “What are you planning to do next?”

“I don’t know.” Song Shuhang frankly replied.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword: “???”

You don’t know?

Then what are you doing with that hammer!

“But the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber should know what to do,” Song Shuhang added.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber continued to thrum excitedly.

However, it didn’t have the capability to speak like Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, and even in human-saber fusion mode, Song Shuhang and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword couldn’t understand what it was trying to say.

Just then, Father Goudan gave a hint: “Continue with your soulless ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’.”

Although soulless, Tyrannical Song’s Saber-Nurturing Technique was genuinely effective.

It had an outstanding effect in nurturing magical treasures.

Following Father Goudan’s reminder, Song Shuhang immediately reached out and placed his hands on the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, with the glow on his hands flickering continuously.

The high-frequency flickering made the faint glow of the Saber-Nurturing Technique dazzling.

Moreover, due to the ‘Sub-immortality’ of Song Shuhang’s whole body, each cast of his Saber-Nurturing Technique carried a trace of immortal information.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword could clearly feel the difference—it felt like it was about to break through its limit once again, even though it was already at the ‘Divine Weapon Limit’!

This kind of limit breakthrough, it had felt once before—when it evolved from a normal ‘sword’ form and developed a young girl’s head plus a giant sword form.

And this time, the feeling was even stronger.

It felt like it was about to break through the limitations of ‘saber and sword,’ to transcend the framework of being just a ‘weapon,’ and to enter an entirely new realm!

If this continues, what exactly will I become?

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s heart fluttered with both trepidation and anticipation.

In worlds across several planes,

Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven suddenly felt a movement in his heart, and he couldn’t help but stand up—Scarlet Heaven Sword was his life-bound magical treasure, and any change would provoke a reaction from Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven.

“Scarlet Heaven Sword, is it evolving?” murmured Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven.

The Scarlet Heaven Sword, being at the limit of ‘Immortal Divine Weapon,’ shouldn’t have any room for evolution—because the next step up would be a primordial treasure.

But a primordial treasure could not be forged by anyone other than the Heavenly Dao.

Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven began to calculate with his fingers.

Soon, he arrived at a conclusion.

The change in Scarlet Heaven Sword wasn’t an evolution towards a primordial treasure, but rather a different kind of evolution?

...

...

“I’m about to start evolving,” Scarlet Heaven Sword said to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang nodded, “Yes, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword, I’ve sensed it too.”

“What will I evolve into?” Scarlet Heaven Sword asked with a mix of anticipation and worry.

Song Shuhang was silent for a long time before he said, “Perhaps... you might evolve into a Saber woman?”

He remembered that his Saber-Nurturing Technique came from that giant ancestor, whose ultimate goal was to nurture a saber into a Saber woman.

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber: “Buzz buzz buzz~”

Song Shuhang remained silent, but the frequency at which he used the Saber-Nurturing Technique clearly sped up a notch.

“Wouldn’t a ‘Saber lad’ be okay?” After a while, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword suddenly asked.

It didn’t even ask about being a ‘Sword lad,’ but was willing to change to a saber, which was a huge concession on its part.

Song Shuhang thought for a moment and said, “Maybe ‘Saber lad’ might infringe on copyright?”

Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword: “...”

If it really turned into a Saber woman, it might die of embarrassment at the hands of Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven.

“Is the process of evolution irreversible?” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword couldn’t let go and asked.

After thinking it over, Song Shuhang said, “I’m sorry Senior, this Saber-Nurturing Technique isn’t originally mine. How about we stop ‘evolving’ and call it quits here?”

Although he really wanted to see what Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword would look like as a Saber woman, such things should ultimately depend on Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword’s own will.

After all, Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword had always taken good care of him.

“Let’s evolve,” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword made its final decision.

Not a single sword or other immortal divine weapons could resist the temptation of evolving to ‘break through their limits’!

Especially for a sword like Scarlet Heaven Sword that was at the ‘immortal divine weapon limit.’

Just like cultivators trapped at a limiting realm unable to break through, Scarlet Heaven Sword felt uncomfortable when stuck at a level and unable to advance an inch.

“Since that’s the case, please forgive my offense, Senior!” Song Shuhang immediately erupted with full hand speed.

With his current realm and ‘Sub-immortal’ Reinforcement, once his hand speed was fully unleashed, just by the act of stroking, he could flatten the world’s tallest peak in an instant!

For cultivators whose strength wasn’t enough, the caress of a top-tier expert was fatally tempting!

Currently, both Scarlet Heaven Sword and Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber were ablaze with fire out of nowhere.

That was the spark of Song Shuhang’s excessively fast hand speed.

“He’s gone completely crazy,” the three-eyed young senior commented.

“Actually, I’m quite tempted to try this exaggerated speed of the Saber-Nurturing Technique,” the Heavenly Emperor’s offspring suddenly said.

Father Goudan: “!!!”

From the words of the Heavenly Emperor’s offspring, had she endured the Saber-Nurturing Technique before?

Song Goudan, what have you done to Dada Egg?

“The transformation has begun,” Senior White said quietly as he gently pushed the wriggling Meteor Sword back to his waist.

Cut off from the outside world, it formed a ‘mini-reincarnation’ world of its own.

“Hang on, is this plane the Infernal Realm?” the self-corpse wondered, asking aloud.

“You guessed right, Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song. This indeed is the location of the Infernal Realm. But to be precise, it is located at a ‘Plane Barrier’ of the Infernal Realm. It’s the border between the Infernal Realm and another small world plane,” Su Clan’s Sixteen explained. “The Su Clan Ancestor Star is located within that small world plane. Additionally, the ‘Spirit River Secret Realm’ of the Su Clan on Earth is also connected to the Su Clan Ancestor Star through the channel I built.”

“Is the Su Clan Ancestor Star a special reincarnation land for the members of the Spirit River Su Clan?” the self-corpse wondered internally.

He actually didn’t want to delve too deeply into the secrets of others.

Knowing too much could easily lead to being silenced.

However, Su Clan’s Sixteen directly revealed these secrets before him, and he understood them at a glance.

“That’s right. Members of the Spirit River Su Clan, if they wish, can enter the reincarnation land of the Ancestor Star,” Su Clan’s Sixteen replied. “The foundation of the Ancestor Star’s reincarnation is built upon the relic of the Fifth Heavenly Dao.”

“The Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade, besides possessing the power of reincarnation, also has the power to peer into time and ‘see’ the different versions of oneself. The one Sixteen is to make contact with is it.”

Chapter 3083: Chapter 3081: Ancestor, I am a Rare Mutant
 

Great beauty?

For someone to be called a ‘great beauty’ by a major figure like Su Clan’s Sixteen, she must certainly have the looks of an immortal.

— But what does it have to do with me whether she is a great beauty or not?

Self Corpse was puzzled in his heart.

Moreover, to tell the truth, there are countless fairies in this world, but among the criteria that would move Tyrannical Song’s main body, ‘beauty’ is definitely not that important a factor.

Apart from that, which part of Tyrannical Song’s main body isn’t associated with a beauty-level big shot?

With so many ‘cheats’ equipped, one develops immunity to the ‘great beauty’ attribute.

Thus, Self Corpse didn’t have much of a reaction to this topic; he just nodded his head and hummed in agreement, considering the matter settled.

Ahead.

The guiding manifestation of Su Clan’s Sixteen, after intentionally revealing that the Reincarnation Blade was associated with the great beauty attribute, was slightly taken aback as she didn’t receive any feedback from the Tyrannical Song manifestation for a long time.

She then thought of a possibility, hastily turned around, and started looking around while her consciousness swept across the area.

In her hands, a shining thread appeared, gently tugging it.

Soon, she sensed Tyrannical Song’s Self Corpse a meter behind her.

Self Corpse looked at Su Clan’s Sixteen with a puzzled face as she went through her series of actions.

Su Clan’s Sixteen hid the ‘thread’ and complained softly, “Why did you suddenly stop responding? I thought I had lost you.”

“Ah, sorry?” Self Corpse felt wronged in his heart—when his main body cut his three corpses, he shouldn’t have used that ‘Forgotten Divine Technique’.

“What were we talking about just now?” Su Clan’s Sixteen continued to hook the thread with her fingers, leading Self Corpse so that she wouldn’t lose him.

“We were talking about the great beauty attribute,” reminded Self Corpse.

Su Clan’s Sixteen nodded and then asked back, “And you had no reaction when you heard that?”

“Reaction? Let me think.” Self Corpse thought seriously for a moment, then suddenly his eyes lit up: “The Reincarnation Blade is a great beauty, which means, is she a Saber woman? Is she also cultivated into the ultimate mode with the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’?”

Su Clan’s Sixteen: “???”

The ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ can cultivate sabers into Saber women?

What kind of ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ has such a terrifying feature?

I’ve lived so long, and I’ve never heard of such a thing; you better not fool me!

“No?” Seeing Su Clan’s Sixteen’s reaction, Self Corpse felt that his reply might have been wrong.

“I have never heard of ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ being able to cultivate sabers into Saber women,” said Su Clan’s Sixteen. “Where did you get such messy information?”

“I have cultivated one before, to be precise, my main body has, not long ago,” Self Corpse replied sincerely.

While speaking, Self Corpse stretched out his hand in a vacuum, using the power of ‘Defiant Whale Glove artifact spirit fairy,’ and cast the Shadow Casting Technique, playing out the scene where ‘Senior Scarlet Heaven was transformed into a sword woman.’

The figure of the Scarlet Heaven Sword stretched out in the light halo, finally transforming into a metallic young girl with long wavy hair.

Su Clan’s Sixteen’s eyes widened: “!!!”

This is unscientific, and it’s not even about cultivation!

It completely contravenes the laws of cultivation.

“Which ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ did you use?” After a long while, Su Clan’s Sixteen finally asked.

“Speaking of this Saber-Nurturing Technique... it should also be related to the Spirit River Su Clan. Fairy, you really don’t know?” the self-corpse asked in return.

In his memories, Tyrannical Song’s main body acquired this Saber-Nurturing Technique when he first entered the dreamland of Su Clan’s Seven and obtained it from that ‘whopper’ great master.

“Isn’t there a ‘whopper’ great master in the Spirit River Su Clan who is the founder of this Saber-Nurturing Technique? If I remember correctly, the great master’s saber has already been nurtured into a saber woman. Moreover, during the nurturing process, the saber woman could be ‘set’ up to have the appearance and personality that he likes most,” the self-corpse replied.

Su Clan’s Sixteen: “...”

When she heard this, the fairy’s expression became very complex.

After a while.

“From where did you meet this ‘whopper’ great master?” Su Clan’s Sixteen asked.

The Tyrannical Song’s Self Corpse explained in a way everyone could understand, “I used a special method to see a segment of the Spirit River Su Clan’s ‘whopper’ great master teaching his disciples, during which I heard about the ❮Three Thousand Sabers Scripture❯ and the Saber-Nurturing Technique. In the process, I also met the great master’s saber woman, a woman with short black hair, her entire being exuded an extremely sharp saber intent, she was absolutely a ‘saber’ without any doubt!”

He still vividly remembered that whopper great master’s saying: With love, all things are possible!

When Su Clan’s Sixteen heard this, her facial expression grew even more complex.

It was indescribable what she was feeling at that moment.

It was like one day, you jokingly bought a three-yuan toy bamboo-copter from the roadside and gave it to the cute neighbor’s kid, telling her that if she just spins the bamboo-copter above her head, she would be able to fly.

Then, the cute kid did as told... and she actually flew!

It’s that feeling of a mental explosion.

“Could there be some misunderstanding in this?” the self-corpse asked upon seeing Su Clan’s Sixteen’s complicated expression, immediately guessing the reason.

“That ‘period-ancestor’ saber woman you mentioned, in a certain sense, is indeed a saber woman,” said Su Clan’s Sixteen. “Come with me.”

Under the lead of Su Clan’s Sixteen’s manifestation, the two quickly passed through the ‘Blood-colored Reincarnation’ forbidden area and entered the atmosphere of the Su Clan’s ancestor planet.

Above the clouds of the Su Clan’s ancestor planet, a series of defensive measures were structured.

There were floating buildings similar to the ‘ancient Heavenly City’ floating in the clouds.

Above the clouds, some of the Su Clan’s disciples took turns guarding.

The self-corpse sensed the aura of the ‘Spirit River Su Clan bloodline’ from these disciples.

“Is the entire ancestor planet filled with members of the Spirit River Su Clan?” the self-corpse asked—considering this, how vast must the Spirit River Su Clan be?

“More or less... However, the members of the Su Clan on the ancestor planet are somewhat special. Also, besides rotational duties, they do not always live on the ancestor planet,” Su Clan’s Sixteen led the self-corpse, flying all the way.

Finally, they arrived at a palace in the clouds.

The gate of the palace was pushed open... and the self-corpse encountered an acquaintance.

The ancestor of the Spirit River Su Clan, Mister Knot.

“Senior Knot?” the self-corpse first froze, then said, “Is the one at the Su Clan’s territory your clone?”

“No, I was worried about Sixteen’s condition, so I came over using the internal Rainbow Bridge. After Fellow Daoist Song and Sixteen form a dao companion relationship, he will also be able to use the internal Rainbow Bridge passage to directly enter the Su Clan’s ancestor planet,” Mister Knot casually replied.

The self-corpse: “...”

“Knot, you’re just in time, cooperate with me,” Su Clan’s Sixteen’s manifestation waved at Mister Knot and said: “Transform into the heavenly saber!”

“Ancestor, I do not possess the function to transform into the heavenly saber,” Mister Knot reminded. “I have the rare mutated innate skill, my manifestation is that of the Heavenly Sword.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen: “...”

The self-corpse: “!!!”

Chapter 3084: Chapter 3082: The Disgusting Tyrannical Song, But Becoming Warm?
 

“Do you need me to demonstrate?” asked the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan, who had not transformed in many years.

“I think I’ve understood,” the self-corpse said, covering his forehead with one hand and rubbing it hard. “So, the giant ancestral master’s saber woman... wasn’t actually transformed from a saber? The Saber-Nurturing Technique he taught doesn’t actually have this function?”

Such a headache!

“Yes,” Su Clan’s Sixteen responded calmly, “His saber was his dao companion, a numerically-designated Fairy from the Spirit River Su Clan. The imposing saber intent you sensed was also innate to that numerically-designated Fairy.”

“So Fairy, can you also transform into a heavenly saber?” the self-corpse asked casually.

Su Clan’s Sixteen shook her head, “Unfortunately... not every member of the Spirit River Su Clan possesses this talent.”

The self-corpse looked up at the sky, “Then what’s the deal with my ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’?”

In fact, deep down, he had already begun to suspect—the Saber-Nurturing Technique of Tyrannical Song was definitely due to non-standard usage, lacking a soul and even wholesale ‘Cheap Love’, thus causing a mutation.

“You’re asking me? Who should I ask?” said Su Clan’s Sixteen. “Why not try using your ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ on the knot and see if there’s any difference?”

“No, no, no, I’d rather not,” the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan continuously waved his hands. Even though his mind was as calm as still water, the thought of a big guy using the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ on him sent shivers down his spine.

After transforming into a ‘Heavenly Sword’, his body theoretically could also accept ‘Saber-Nurturing Techniques’ or ‘Sword-Nurturing Techniques’ and other artifact nurturing skills.

But in the process of performing the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’, the caster must convey their own love to the ‘magical treasure’.

Just thinking about Tyrannical Song conveying various ‘affections’ to him made him feel terribly unsettled.

“There’s no need for so much trouble, just hand me any magical treasure, and I could demonstrate for the seniors,” the self-corpse waved his hand.

Su Clan’s Sixteen asked, “Any magical treasure will do? Not just sabers?”

“Yes, anything will do,” the self-corpse confidently stated.

His ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ had long transcended the category of ‘sabers’. Whether it be sabers, swords, pillars, shields, or even clones and seals—as long as his hands could touch, he could apply the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’.

Su Clan’s Sixteen smiled and then reached her hand out into the vacuum.

Subsequently, she pulled out an exquisite sword scabbard from the vacuum.

—On the surface, except for being slightly more refined, the scabbard seemed ordinary.

But beside them, the eyelids of the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan twitched slightly.

Seeing this, the self-corpse asked cautiously, “This scabbard... it’s not transformed by a numerically-designated Fairy from the Su Clan, is it?”

If it really was a Fairy from the Spirit River Su Clan, then his ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ would be hard to perform.

“Rest assured, this is a normally refined magical treasure, not a member of the Su Clan. If you sense carefully, you should be able to recognize it,” Su Clan’s Sixteen handed the scabbard to the self-corpse.

The self-corpse looked at the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan nearby.

“Indeed, this weapon is not a transformation of a Su Clan member,” the Knot ancestor replied.

But the more it was so, the less confident the clever self-corpse became.

So, he placed his hand on the ‘scabbard’ and first activated the ‘secret appraisal technique’—as for the cost of appraisal, it could be paid by the current main body.

The current main body was in a ‘Sub-immortal’ state, and even direct appraisal of the Will of the Heavens would not cause him to die on the spot.

Of course, such a matter needed to be pre-approved.

A moment later...

[Done!]Tyrannical Song’s main body sent a response.

So, the self-corpse happily executed the ‘secret appraisal technique’.

The light of the secret technique flashed by.

Intense pain affected his spirit... while physical pain was borne by the main body.

“Pain ranking, approximately 77 out of a hundred. It’s quite flavorful,” the self-corpse meticulously savored the spiritual pain and carefully rated it.

As long as it didn’t exceed 100 points, it was theoretically within the range Tyrannical Song could easily endure.

Appraisal succeeded.

The turntable of time began to reverse, and the appraisal information emerged in the mind of the self-corpse.

[Dao Artifact·Reincarnation Blade’s former sheath: Due to an uncomfortable style, it has now been upgraded and replaced. The creation of the scabbard employed special refining techniques of the Fifth Heavenly Dao...]

The appraisal results he received were very clear, yet quite brief.

Through the power of time, only so much information could be obtained.

Moreover, his self-corpse could sense that this information was what the “saber scabbard,” or rather, the Dao Artifact·Reincarnation Blade behind it, was willing to let him appraise. If the other party didn’t wish it, all information would be shielded.

Does that mean if the intimacy is sufficient, more information could be appraised?

Song Shuhang had never considered this possibility before.

Now it seems that “Saber Nurturing Technique” could also be used in combination with the “secret appraisal technique”?

“Fairy, then I am going to make a move. Once I do, you can’t regret it,” his self-corpse, holding the once saber scabbard of this ‘Dao Artifact·Reincarnation Blade,’ cautioned.

“Just go ahead, don’t worry, this scabbard is no longer in use. I have about seven or eight similar items in my possession, you don’t even have to worry about damaging it,” Su Clan’s Sixteen said generously.

“Then, excuse me,” his self-corpse flipped his head, first activating the “small hair growing technique.”

A head of jet-black long hair condensed into shape.

Su Clan’s Sixteen blinked, did the “Saber Nurturing Technique” also require growing a head of long hair first? This was something she had never seen before.

While she was pondering, his self-corpse’s long black hair condensed into a thousand tiny palms, roughly creating one small hand for every hundred strands.

These thousand palms, along with his self-corpse’s pair of arms, pressed onto the scabbard simultaneously!

Because the target was related to ‘primordial treasure’, and it was a scabbard once used by a Dao artifact and even used the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao’s refining techniques.

His self-corpse started by deploying his full strength.

Whoosh!

The radiance of the “Saber Nurturing Technique” exploded, turning into a sun-like attack.

Now, in just one second, his self-corpse’s palms could slide over the target a thousand times!

In a second, the scabbard endured a thousand instances of the “Saber Nurturing Technique”!

Su Clan’s Sixteen and Su Clan’s Knot felt as if their eyes were about to be dazzled blind...

They had never seen such a brazen use of the “Saber Nurturing Technique”.

Moreover, Song Shuhang’s “Saber Nurturing Technique” utterly exceeded the normal specifications of the Saber-Nurturing Technique.

What happened to the “love” that the “Saber Nurturing Technique” was supposed to involve?

This was a thousand bursts of ‘love’ in just one second, what kind of ‘love’ slides a thousand times in a second?

But, no matter what Song Shuhang’s ‘love’ was, its effect was undeniably real.

Three seconds later, a temporary seven-colored divine artifact appeared on the scabbard.

Su Clan’s Sixteen felt her worldview being challenged.

Meanwhile...

In some mysterious space, Dark Sun Big Shot was with the body of an Immortal Daoist.

Suddenly, Dark Sun Big Shot’s heart stirred.

In his mind, the image of a man kept emerging.

It was that detestable Tyrannical Song.

But for some reason, the originally loathsome Tyrannical Song suddenly seemed somewhat warm.

Dark Sun Big Shot: “???”

What happened?

Did something strange occur within my body?

Dark Sun Big Shot earnestly checked his body, but did not find any abnormalities from head to toe.

Could it be that my psychology has twisted?

Or maybe, did Tyrannical Song do something to me?

Chapter 3085: Chapter 3083: Are you afraid? I have seven more sword scabbards like this!
 

The Big Boss of the Dark Sun immediately activated its divination capability and began deducing the causality—his body had become so odd, it must definitely be the doing of Tyrannical Song and Immortal White!

Regardless of the reason, as long as the source of the anomaly cannot be found, the blame could be pinned on Tyrannical Song and Immortal White.

Because during this period, only these two individuals had been meddling with him for several days!

Big Boss of the Dark Sun’s divination started, and its level of divination was completely different from that of ordinary people; the initial array of its divination spanned the area of a major city!

True massive calculation power was all poured into the divination array pattern, deducing the causality.

However, halfway through its deduction, it discovered that the causalities were blocked and the Heavenly Mechanism was obstructed.

“Buzz!” The Dark Sun forcefully shattered the divination array pattern.

It was the current Fifth Heavenly Dao, who was concealing the Heavenly Mechanism, plotting secretly!

Besides the current Fifth Heavenly Dao, someone else was severing the chain of causality in the shadows, preventing him from tracing this segment of causality.

However, the more the Heavenly Dao concealed, the more it inadvertently revealed the identity of the schemer—it was Tyrannical Song!

In the myriad practitioners in the universe, only Tyrannical Song could make the Heavenly Dao intervene to help him scheme.

This place holds no silver three hundred taels.

Moreover, when his body underwent transformation, it was only the favorability toward Tyrannical Song that was changing, which served as even stronger evidence.

“One day, one day, I will...” He paused midway again, hesitating for a moment: “Forget it, both Tyrannical Song and that Immortal White seem too dangerous. Before my grand plan succeeds, it’s best to avoid the two of them to prevent unnecessary complications.”

It was not because his favorability toward Tyrannical Song was continuously increasing, but rather, after losing a ‘burden’ on his body, his mind had become clearer, making him think rationally and understand what needed to be forsaken.

Rather than seeking trouble with ‘Tyrannical Song’ and ‘Immortal White’ and investing a lot of energy in retaliating against them, it was better to avoid them and scheme in the shadows.

This was how the Dark Sun reconciled it with himself internally.

“Stay calm, calm down. Do not be influenced by external information, prepare again for the annihilation plan, but this time, be more cautious.” The Dark Sun seemed to be talking to itself, yet also seemed to be communicating with the unresponsive body of the ‘Immortal Daoist.’

[Ding~ Are you afraid?] A woman’s voice abruptly resounded beside its ear.

The Dark Sun was startled: “!!!”

The fact that this woman’s voice had directly reached his ear implied that his hiding spot had been detected by someone.

If this woman could detect his hiding spot... then the Heavenly Dao would also have methods to pinpoint his location.

Having barely escaped from a wool-plucking operation jointly organized by Immortal White and Tyrannical Song, he had no desire to go back.

[But I must tell you, I still have seven similar sword scabbards!] The woman’s voice came through again.

The Dark Sun was utterly bewildered.

What was this similar sword scabbard thing, and did the recent strange transformation of his body have something to do with the ‘sword scabbard’ the woman mentioned?

Moreover, as there were still seven similar ‘sword scabbards’, did that mean he had to endure seven more transformations?

“Had it not been for the Heavenly Dao blocking the Heavenly Mechanism, my divination technique alone would have been sufficient to lock down the location and gather more information. What exactly is the current Fifth Heavenly Dao plotting?” the Dark Sun said in a deep voice.

At the same time, it called out into the void, “Who are you?”

[Ding~ Are you afraid?] It seemed to trigger a kind of ‘cycle mechanism’, as the woman’s voice echoed again.

About two seconds later.

[But I must tell you, I still have seven similar sword scabbards!] It was the same phrase, the same lines, even the tone had not changed at all.

Was it a recording?

This meant ‘she’ had recorded this long ago and left it behind... thus, this was likely a trap laid for him a long time ago.

Oh no, here it comes again.

Another wave of ‘subtly increasing Tyrannical Song’s favorability’ is attacking.

The effect this time is stronger than the last.

In the air, it almost seems like there is the scent of ‘Tyrannical Song’s favorability +1’.

“Continuing like this, I will be at a disadvantage. I need to set up a plan, secure a ‘hostile state’ towards Tyrannical Song, and not be influenced,” Dark Sun quickly made a decision and calmly chose the most rational option.

...

...

Elsewhere.

Self-corpse initially intended just to demonstrate ‘one-second’ of the Saber-Nurturing Technique to Su Clan’s Sixteen and mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan, and to exhibit his proficiency in the Saber-Nurturing Technique.

However, due to a slip of the hand, he accidentally slid and two extra seconds passed.

After stopping the Saber-Nurturing Technique, the self-corpse returned the sword scabbard, which radiated the ‘temporary divine artifact rainbow light,’ to Su Clan’s Sixteen.

In the process of handing back the scabbard, it made a buzzing sound as if it was reluctant to part ways with Tyrannical Song.

Su Clan’s Sixteen: “...”

She had lived so long and had never seen such a domineering Saber-Nurturing Technique; it had already transcended the scope of Saber-Nurturing Techniques and touched the level of ‘principles and laws.’

[It’s a good thing I didn’t let Tyrannical Song try this Saber-Nurturing Technique on me. Otherwise...], the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan thought, imagining herself radiating multicolored light all over, which would have been a sheer embarrassment.

“Although I completely fail to understand the principles of your Saber-Nurturing Technique, if it is your Saber-Nurturing Technique that cultivates magical treasures into a ‘Saber woman’ state in your mind, maybe it really is understandable,” Su Clan’s Sixteen eventually concluded.

She took back the glowing scabbard, intending to put it back in her storage space.

Just then, a woman’s voice came into her mind, conveying a vague intention — to ask her to help out and pass on the remaining seven scabbards to the fellow friend exhibiting the Saber-Nurturing Technique.

Su Clan’s Sixteen: “???”

This woman’s voice was likely from the sentient treasure of ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade.’

The always dormant Reincarnation Blade had awakened?

For Su Clan’s Sixteen, this was a beneficial matter.

A fully awakened Reincarnation Blade could bring greater advantages and opportunities to Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Moreover... with the Reincarnation Blade asking her to hand over all the scabbards to Tyrannical Song’s manifestation, could the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ for the scabbards also be effective for her?

If this continues, would the Reincarnation Blade turn into the shape of Tyrannical Song?

Tyrannical Song’s Saber-Nurturing Technique is really eerie!

Many thoughts flashed through Su Clan’s Sixteen’s mind, but ultimately, she took out the remaining seven ‘sword scabbards’ from her storage space and handed them to Tyrannical Song’s manifestation.

Self-corpse, puzzled, asked, “Fairy, why is this?”

“Why don’t you brush up each scabbard with the Saber-Nurturing Technique again? Although I can’t explain the principle, it would be greatly beneficial for Su Clan’s Sixteen!” Su Clan’s Sixteen said.

She felt uneasy explaining this scabbard to Tyrannical Song’s manifestation.

But on the other hand, self-corpse slightly smiled, seemingly grasping her intent in a second.

Song Shuhang already knew that Su Clan’s Sixteen was going to meet the ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade’ left behind by the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

And since the scabbards in his hand had once housed the Reincarnation Blade and were somehow connected with it,

Thus, applying the Saber-Nurturing Technique to these scabbards might influence the ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade’ and bring benefits to Su Clan’s Sixteen.

Song Shuhang had great confidence in his Saber-Nurturing Technique—using it on a dao artifact wasn’t his first time. Both the buzzing, cute-sell ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ and the cool, big-eyed planet had endured the Saber-Nurturing Technique.

“Leave it to me,” replied his self-corpse.

He took the seven scabbards and grabbed them all in one breath.

“Not one by one?” Su Clan’s Sixteen inquired.

“No need. Just now I was only demonstrating my Saber-Nurturing Technique to the seniors, without exerting my real strength. So not just seven scabbards, even if you multiply that number by ten, it wouldn’t be a problem for me,” the self-corpse replied confidently.

When it comes to the cultivation of the Saber-Nurturing Technique, his main body, Tyrannical Song, is at the great master level.

[That one-thousand-strikes-per-second Saber-Nurturing Technique just now wasn’t his real strength? Moreover... this isn’t even Tyrannical Song’s main body, but one of his Three Corpses Avatars.] The mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan was astonished.

In the future, even shaking hands with Tyrannical Song’s main body must be done cautiously. A handshake might take about three seconds, and in that time, Tyrannical Song’s main body could do a lot—this thought made the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan extra cautious.

Whoosh~

Opposite, the self-corpse went all out.

One-thousand strikes per second in the Saber-Nurturing Technique was something Tyrannical Song’s main body could achieve at the Eighth Stage Realm.

Now, his main body had surpassed ordinary immortals, reaching the ‘Sub-Immortal’ state. A thousand strikes per second were as effortless as breathing for him.

Nowadays, as long as the material of the magical treasure could endure it, ten million strikes per second were just basic operations for Tyrannical Song’s main body.

Being an avatar, the self-corpse, when going all-out, could achieve this number too.

This time, the objects to be nurtured were Dao Artifact scabbards; there was absolutely no need to worry about them being damaged.

Thus, the self-corpse went all out.

If it could be said that the splendor of the Saber-Nurturing Technique previously demonstrated by the self-corpse resembled the early morning sun... then the radiant splendor of the technique at this moment was like the scorching midday sun of summer.

Su Clan’s Sixteen and the mysterious ancestor were enveloped by this brilliance, feeling an intense heat and... an intangible increase in their favorability towards Tyrannical Song.

“So far apart, and still affected?” the mysterious ancestor of Su Clan exclaimed in surprise, stepping back a bit more.

Whoosh whoosh whoosh~

This time, Su Clan’s Sixteen had not set an ‘end’ time, and the self-corpse, reveling in freedom, simply could not stop.

...

...

Meanwhile, elsewhere.

The Dark Sun had completely gone mad.

It had just been preparing to research a magical technique to lock Tyrannical Song in a ‘hostile state,’ but at this moment, a woman’s voice relentlessly echoed in its mind.

Those two sentences, with a pause of 2-3 seconds between them.

Yet this time, each utterance of these sentences came with its own echo, six echoes to be exact.

[Ding~ Are you scared? Scared, scared, scared, scared, scared, scared?]

[But I must tell you, I have seven more similar scabbards! Each, each, each, each, each, each!]

The Dark Sun’s mind was filled with ‘scared, scared, scared’ and ‘cut, cut, cut’...

After struggling against this devilish echoing female voice, the Dark Sun gritted its teeth and developed a rudimentary form of the ‘lock Tyrannical Song in a hostile mode’ magical technique.

A big boss is truly a big boss; a few simple spells could be figured out just with a few thoughts.

The moment the rudimentary form of the spell was completed, the Dark Sun couldn’t wait to apply this technique to itself to test the effects—it just wanted to resist the shocks of physical anomalies, and could upgrade it slowly later on.

The magical technique was significantly effective.

After using this technique, its deep inner allegiance to Tyrannical Song was locked in ‘hostile mode.’

However, that function of ‘favorability towards Tyrannical Song +1’ seemed to be continuing still.

This function, within its body, was divided into two parts.

One part acted on the ‘ruler of the Netherworld’ segment of its body and produced a continuous effect.

The other part landed on the ‘Immortal Sand,’ and was quickly neutralized by the ‘eternal’ characteristic, losing its effect.

The eternal attribute, theoretically a good thing, should eliminate all adverse status effects.

But now, the ruler of the Netherworld segment continued to be affected... The eternal attribute part remaining unharmed, a subtle balance between the two was subtly being disrupted.

[This time, the most correct choice is to retreat the ruler of the Netherworld part back into the ‘Immortal Material.’ By the protection of the eternal attribute, separate the impacts brought by the physical anomalies.] The Dark Sun was very calm internally, knowing what the most correct choice was.

But...

Its subconscious seemed somewhat resistant to this choice!

Just as the Dark Sun was feeling conflicted... The woman’s voice next to its ears and the body’s anomalies suddenly disappeared.

Had Tyrannical Song stopped his actions?

Or had the duration of the trap’s effects come to an end?

[It’s good that it’s over.] The Dark Sun thought to itself.

Thus, it need not be conflicted about whether to retreat into the ‘Immortal Material’ to eliminate the impact Tyrannical Song had left.

...

...

At the Su Clan’s Ancestor Star.

“It should be about enough,” the self-corpse suddenly stopped the delightful action of nurturing the scabbards.

He could have continued to nurture endlessly as long as Su Clan’s Sixteen did not call a halt—he could directly induce anomalies in those seven scabbards!

But a certain intuition transmitted from his main body made the self-corpse stop his actions.

That intuition seemed to be entangled with a ‘lucky karmic connection.’

[Is it the part of me affected by Senior White calling for a halt?] A realization dawned in the self-corpse’s mind.

At this moment, stopping the Saber-Nurturing Technique was the luckiest choice for him?

“Not continuing anymore?” asked Su Clan’s Sixteen—Reincarnation Blade had not alerted her about halting, and honestly, she was quite curious to see if the ‘scabbards’ could transform into Saber women just like in Tyrannical Song’s hologram.

“It’s about enough, moderation is key, and slow is smooth,” the self-corpse slightly smiled, his expression brimming with reliability.

As he smiled, his presence gradually diminished...

[Does his presence weaken when not demonstrating the Saber-Nurturing Technique, meaning the sole purpose of Tyrannical Song’s this avatar is to nurture sabers?] Su Clan’s Sixteen thought to herself, while quietly pulling on that invisible thread, preventing Tyrannical Song’s avatar from wandering off.

...

...

Deep within the Su Clan’s Ancestor Star.

Su Clan’s Sixteen was led by another avatar of Su Clan’s Sixteen to the palace where the ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade’ was located.

“I won’t go in any further,” said Su Clan’s Sixteen with a smile.

Chapter 3086: Chapter 3084: Shocking, Reincarnation Blade Fairy actually refined the Sword Scabbard like this!
 

Before entering, Sixteen of the Su Clan had already mentally prepared herself for various challenges.

“And the mysterious First Heavenly Dao,” replied the White Dragon sister.

During this time, apart from accompanying Sixteen from the Su Clan, she spent her other time either discussing ‘fellow daoists’ with Song Shuhang’s self-corpse or following Song Shuhang’s main body to watch dramas, thus she was quite aware of Song Shuhang’s condition.

Currently, Song Shuhang’s condensed ‘Sub-immortal’ body had almost gathered all the attributes of the Heavenly Daos from past generations, lacking only the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao Relic’ and the Mountain Opening Heavenly Dao that Sixteen was about to come into contact with.

“If possible... think of a way to get the ‘Reincarnation Blade’ to agree to meet Song Shuhang,” Sixteen whispered softly.

She had a bit of a collecting obsession and hoped to gather some things as perfectly as possible.

Well, the above is just an excuse.

She simply wanted to do her best to let Song Shuhang gather all sorts of ‘Immortal Information’ from the different Heavenly Daos.

Softly tugging at the White Dragon sister’s scarf, pulling the White Dragon sister flatter and longer, Sixteen nervously entered the ‘Reincarnation Blade Palace.’

Pushing open the grand doors... what met her eyes was not the spacious palace space she expected, but instead, the originally grand palace space was blocked, leaving only a narrow corridor.

It was extremely narrow, feeling only an inch wide, and even Sixteen from the Su Clan could only squeeze in sideways.

If it were Soft Feather, upon seeing this corridor, she would only bow her head in a sigh and leave disappointed.

The corridor was also filled with a lot of fog, severely limiting visibility.

Sixteen from the Su Clan squeezed sideways into this corridor and slowly moved forward.

“Speaking of which, is this corridor some kind of special seal or something?” Sixteen asked doubtfully as she advanced.

The White Dragon sister shook her head: “No, it’s just a regular narrow corridor, possibly a hobby of the palace’s owner. Maybe if you go further, it will become more spacious?”

In this palace, even the consciousness of immortals was suppressed, and the consciousness of the White Dragon sister could only sweep an area about ten meters ahead.

Sixteen sighed, forcefully inhaled, and cooperated with techniques like the ‘bone shrinking technique’ to make her advance smoother.

After walking for a long while, there was no sense of the path ahead becoming ‘spacious’ at all.

From the entrance all the way here, the long narrow corridor felt like it was inside a huge scabbard.

A metallic echo returned from the walls.

Was this corridor really transformed from the ‘Reincarnation Blade’s’ scabbard?

“White Dragon sister, I suddenly have a bold idea,” Sixteen said after pondering for a moment—more precisely, it was an idea discussed by her auxiliary personality and the more than a hundred Sixteens.

The ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ she was referring to was not the one used by Song Shuhang, but a very orthodox saber technique from the world of cultivation—as a talent who had realized ‘saber intent’ at a very young age, she naturally knew the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique.’

Su Clan’s Sixteen nodded slightly—in such a confined space, even the degree of her nod was affected. If she nodded too vigorously, her little dragon horns would hit the wall.

About ten breaths later, a bright light from the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ emerged from Su Clan’s Sixteen’s hands.

The gentle light first appeared between Su Clan’s Sixteen’s fingers, enveloping her pink fingernails, gradually spreading to her entire palm.

Afterward, the light from the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ continued for about twenty breaths before slowly stopping. This duration alone was enough for Song Shuhang to perform ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ billions of times.

But the actual ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ process was only just beginning—after the light ceased, it was necessary to use the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ to establish a connection with the magical treasure, conveying the caster’s ‘intention’ to the magical treasure, strengthening the bond between the magical treasure and oneself, and nurturing the magical treasure with one’s spiritual power bit by bit!

Senior cultivators commented that Song Shuhang’s ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ was ‘soulless’ precisely because it lacked this process.

It’s like a true author, who needs to draft a detailed outline before starting to write, considers the plot details, reviews the comments from readers, summarizes the previous part of the story, then disconnects from the internet and seriously starts writing.

But a false author just opens Word and starts writing.

Su Clan’s Sixteen continued with the follow-up steps of the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ as she advanced.

Moments later, a tranquil female voice came from the end of the passage: “Are you a disciple of the Su Clan? Your ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ seems a bit off; even though it’s the same Su Clan’s ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’, your results aren’t quite up to par.”

Su Clan’s Sixteen’s motion of executing the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ stiffened slightly.

“However, not long ago, while I was asleep... suddenly a disciple of the Su Clan performed the Su Clan’s ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ on my retired ‘Sword Scabbard.’ His nurturing was performed to the utmost perfection, with outstanding results, which I greatly appreciated,” the tranquil female voice slowly said: “It was because of his ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ that I was able to awaken from my tens of thousands of years of slumber. You are very lucky to be the first Su Clan’s disciple to contact me in my awakened state.”

This was the ‘benefit for Sixteen’ that Su Clan’s Sixteen had told Song Shuhang about.

Opposite.

Chapter 3087: Chapter 3085: The Curse of Being Scammed
 

The whole head of hair was thus lifted up by the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

At that moment, her skull was smooth and bare.

If everyone’s speculations are correct, then the ‘Dark Sun’ would correspond to the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

Is it its fault again?

Because it was black, it seemed that all the blame in the myriad practitioners in the universe could be thrown onto its head.

Moreover... it was added secretly either right before my main body ‘proved its Dao’ or in the very moment of ‘proving the Dao’. Fortunately, this curse doesn’t seem to have been fully researched and developed. After my main body successfully proved its Dao, it detected the existence of this curse.”

Taking advantage of the fact that the Sword Scabbard was still being forged, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy began to explain the history of the curse in detail to Sixteen.

The Fifth Heavenly Dao initially didn’t know who crafted this ‘curse’.

It was only after proving her Dao and her immortal body actively began to expel the ‘curse’ within that she realized she had been cursed clandestinely. Furthermore, this curse obviously carried the power of ‘eternity’, strong enough to affect existences at the level of Heavenly Axioms.

Afterward, following a lengthy period of covert research, the Fifth Heavenly Dao managed to trace some clues and deduced that her assailant might have been her predecessor, the Fourth Heavenly Dao — although the Fourth Heavenly Dao had stepped down, he seemed to have retained some ability to act in the mortal world.

To counter the ‘curse’ of the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’, the Fifth Heavenly Dao began to research a specialized primordial treasure.

She activated a ‘resurrecting formation’ that she had used when she was in the Immortal Realm before proving her Dao... After becoming pseudo-immortal, this Immortal-formulation had lost its ‘resurrecting’ function.

However, with the modifications of the Fifth Heavenly Dao, this resurrection formation eventually condensed into a special ‘manifestation’.

This ‘manifestation’, with an empty consciousness and carrying the bloodline power of the Fifth Heavenly Dao, is the current ‘Reincarnation Blade Fairy’.

The Fifth Heavenly Dao did not obliterate the curses expelled from her ‘immortal body’ but instead transferred them into this manifestation of herself and step by step refined this body into a special primordial treasure.

In targeting the ‘curse’, she was also scheming to trap the Fourth Heavenly Dao in the distant future.

The Saber-Nurturing Technique passed down in the Su Clan was just an insignificant part among the many schemes laid out by the Fourth Heavenly Dao—the retaliation of the Fifth Heavenly Dao was stronger than that of all the previous Heavenly Daos combined.

During her tenure, she actively struck against anything related to the ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’, attempting several times to obliterate the contingency plans left behind by the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

Even after stepping down, many of her preparations to target the Fourth Heavenly Dao have yet to be activated!

Even the Reincarnation Blade Fairy doesn’t know exactly how much the Fifth Heavenly Dao prepared in secret against the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

The White Dragon nodded and said, “So, as someone who inherits the bloodline of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, can Su Clan’s disciples also use the power of the ‘curse’ to activate their innate skill within? But wouldn’t the power of the curse turn around and invade Su Clan’s disciples?”

After all, the ‘curse’ is a product of a Heavenly Axiom-level power.

“This curse lost its ‘invasive’ feature a long time ago... In fact, the ‘Curse Power’ you now see is no longer the original work of the Fourth Heavenly Dao. The true ‘Fourth Heavenly Dao’s Curse’ was exhausted during the process of my main body refining the Reincarnation Blade. The ‘Curse Power’ you see now has been engendered by my power. Like reaping leeks, what has been clipped is a force under the control of my and Su Clan’s bloodline power,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said with a slight smile.

She was a primordial treasure created by the Fifth Heavenly Dao specifically to target the ‘curse’.

“A curse clipped like reaping leeks?” When the White Dragon heard this, for some reason, she thought of the Inner Demons being reaped by Song Shuhang.

Chapter 3088: Chapter 3086: Tens of thousands of years ago, my main body had not been born yet

Even a “curse” created by the Will of the Heavens, if luck is against it, can become like leeks—continuously harvested.

This world is just that cruel and unfeeling.

On the other side, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was taken aback.

Eat?

What would be delicious?

Was she hinting that I have been a poor host by not serving tea and snacks to my guest?

The hundreds of little Sixteen personalities were scattered irregularly at Sixteen’s sides, with each connected to the auxiliary personas by numerous ‘spikes.’

It held a sense of sci-fi.
