“You go in and meet the Reincarnation Blade Fairy yourself now. I won’t accompany you inside,” Su Clan’s Sixteen told her left side.

Self-corpse: “...”

Su Clan’s Sixteen, I am on your right side! And there are lines connecting us!

Moreover, the self-corpse glanced at the Reincarnation Hall; the doors that Sixteen had previously pushed open had not yet closed.

So he immediately spotted the narrow passage.

How do I get into this passage?

“As for how you’re going to enter this passage, it’s up to you to figure out,” Su Clan’s Sixteen continued to speak towards her left side.

The Self-Corpse Tyrant Body: “...”

After a brief contemplation, he borrowed the power of his main body and summoned the “Sub-immortal Sage Golden Core” to look at the narrow passage.

The strange fog within the passage could not confuse the Sage’s eye anymore.

“Is that a sword scabbard?” The thought crossed the mind of the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body.

If it is a scabbard... should I use the “Saber-Nurturing Technique”?

Since Su Clan’s Sixteen had already said to rely on his own methods to enter,

without a word, the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body rolled up his sleeves, his long hair whirling, and it fell upon the narrow passage.

The radiance of the “Saber-Nurturing Technique” bloomed, as dazzling as a little sun.

At the same time.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy had just finished communicating with the White Dragon and snapped her fingers lightly, casting a spell to bring ‘little friend Song Shuhang’ directly into the Reincarnation Hall.

Therefore...

After the instant teleportation magic concluded, the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body was instantly transferred beside the true body of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

Those hundreds of millions of “Saber-Nurturing Techniques” that were supposed to fall upon the narrow passage, all landed on the main body of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

The dazzling light of the Saber-Nurturing Technique nearly blinded the White Dragon’s eyes.

“You’re starting off with ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’ upon meeting? Isn’t that a bit direct?” the White Dragon commented.

The Self-Corpse Tyrant Body awkwardly retracted his palms and hair.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

Although she had already sensed little friend Song Shuhang’s “Saber-Nurturing Technique” through her former ‘sword scabbard,’ the experience of taking the technique head-on without the scabbard and from the main body itself is entirely different.

“Are you Song Shuhang?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked softly.

“Replying to the Reincarnation Blade Senior, I am one of the three corpses of my main body, the Self Corpse Tyrant Body,” the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body greeted the Reincarnation Blade Fairy with a bow—present were only Senior White, Sixteen, and the ‘great beauty’ before him.

Therefore, there’s no doubt that this fairy must be the primordial treasure, the Reincarnation Blade.

While he spoke, his presence began to diminish again.

When he’s not casting the “Saber-Nurturing Technique,” he becomes nearly invisible.

“Not the main body?” The Reincarnation Blade Fairy peered at Song Shuhang’s Self-Corpse, scrutinizing him.

After a long while.

“Can I see your main body for a while?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked.

“That will take a short while, is that okay?” the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body responded. Right now, Tyrannical Song is with Senior White, visiting the Ancient Nether in the ‘Black Dragon World,’ setting up columns.

“It’s possible, I have a period of time I can wait before Sixteen completes her evolution. But don’t make me wait too long,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said.

The Self-Corpse Tyrant Body nodded, “My main body will come as quickly as possible.”

“Hmm,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy nodded her head.

What followed was a lengthy silence.

“By the way, have we met before? Maybe tens of thousands of years ago, or even earlier?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy suddenly looked up and asked.

“I don’t think so,” the Self-Corpse Tyrant Body replied, “Tens of thousands of years ago, my main body hadn’t been born yet.”

Chapter 3089: Chapter 3087: Is Your Real Target to Covet My Body?
 

The self-corpse’s answer was very conservative.

If this was asked a few months ago, at the end of his response, the self-corpse might have added: “My main body Tyrannical Song is nineteen this year.”

But now, the self-corpse was feeling rather insecure.

Although there was no indication in his memory that he had encountered the Fifth Heavenly Dao... it couldn’t guarantee that the future ‘Tyrannical Song’ wouldn’t come into contact with the Fifth Heavenly Dao from ten thousand years ago!

This dreamland skill, despite its concealment, would still be detected by truly top-tier big shots.

What if one day in the future, the main body Tyrannical Song had an impulse and entered a dream of the past, encountering the Fifth Heavenly Dao from ten thousand years ago, and then got his tracks captured?

Even without entering a dream, what if there was a situation similar to that of ‘Song Woodhead’?

Thus, as the most cautious and wise among the three corpses, the self-corpse dared not speak too confidently.

Upon hearing this, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy blinked in surprise.

She sized up the increasingly less conspicuous self-corpse and nodded after a long while: “Not bad, not even ten thousand years and you’ve already embarked on your own path to immortality, proving the Immortal Realm. Such innate skill and cultivation speed are extremely rare across the myriad realms.”

“Thank you for the compliment, Senior,” the self-corpse said modestly.

The corner of the White Dragon’s mouth twitched: “...”

But she didn’t verbally point it out.

To realize but not speak out, to avoid heartache.

“Since you weren’t even born ten thousand years ago, my sense of familiarity with you might stem from other aspects. It’s possible that I’ve met your predecessors, or that your techniques are somehow familiar to me,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said casually: “In any case, we are somehow connected.”

Living long, one meets many; it’s understandable to occasionally feel a mysterious familiarity towards some things.

“Could it be the techniques from the Xingri Hermit lineage that seem familiar to you, Senior? Have you ever come across a cultivation technique related to my invisible state?” the self-corpse followed up on the topic.

Self-corpse: “...”

And while talking, the self-corpse noticed that the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was somewhat distracted.

Could the numerous Sixteens also be related to the ‘Time River’?

The self-corpse was dragged several meters, a puzzled look on his face: “???”

Before, Su Clan’s Sixteen had done the same thing.

The White Dragon tightly curled her dragon mustaches to keep herself from laughing inappropriately.

“Don’t worry, Senior Reincarnation Blade. The main cultivation technique of my main body is not this technique but mainly the ‘Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique,’ and ‘Forgotten Divine Technique’ is a secondary technique, all passed on to me through the cutting of the three corpses,” said the self-corpse, weary at heart.

“Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy propped her cheek with one hand, supporting herself on the round table, falling into meditation.

When the Self Corpse saw this scene, his emotions accelerated, and he started moving—Reincarnation Blade Fairy was obviously reacting to the “Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique.”

But the problem was, the creator of these techniques was Wielder of the Will White.

After nearing transcendence, Wielder of the Will White used the “Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique” and the Combined Magical Treasure as coordinates, casually throwing a brick into the past, aiming for the distant future.

In other words, this technique was a product of the Seventh Heavenly Dao.

Yet, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, being a primordial treasure of the Fifth Heavenly Dao, showed a significant reaction to it.

—When there was nobody else to blame, just let White two take the blame, and you can’t go wrong.

For the Self Corpse, Tyrannical Song could be the one to take the blame.

At that moment, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy looked up and asked, “When is your main body coming over?”

But I need to exchange space coordinates with my main body, Reincarnation Blade Senior, please grant me the space authority,” the Self Corpse replied.

He was merely a Three Corpses•Self Corpse, and manifestations needed to act like manifestations. Significant responsibilities didn’t need to be borne by them; it was better to leave them to the main body.

“Granted.” The Reincarnation Blade Fairy nodded, granting the Self Corpse ‘space authority,’ allowing him free access to and from the ‘Spirit River Su Clan • Reincarnation Hall’ area.

The next moment,

Space was swapped, the coordinates of the Self Corpse and Song Shuhang’s main body were exchanged.

The Self Corpse went to assist Senior White, waiting for the column insertion process to buffer.

Meanwhile, Song Shuhang’s main body crossed space to arrive, accompanied by a heavy spiritual pressure, making the air around him seem thick.

This was an aftereffect of ‘Full Body Semi-Immortal.’

If he wasn’t careful, an invisible spiritual pressure would continuously release.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy’s eyes widened: “!!!”

Aura of eternity?

Fully resembling immortality?

Was this an Immortal?

Except for not having the ‘laws of the Heavenly Dao’ accompanying his body, this was simply the spitting image of a junior Heavenly Dao.

“I am Tyrannical Song, honored to meet you, Senior,” Song Shuhang strived to contain his aura of spiritual pressure as he bowed with his fists clasped.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy rubbed her eyes—It wasn’t an illusion.

If not for the fact that the Heavenly Dao was incapable of reproduction, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy almost wondered if this ‘Tyrannical Song’ in front of her might be the Heavenly Dao’s own son.

“Fellow Daoist Song, with your current state, if I were not a primordial treasure, I probably couldn’t stand it,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy sighed. “Without proving the Heavenly Dao, how did you manage to reach this stage?”

You should know that even the current Heavenly Dao couldn’t turn its ‘manifestation’ into something like this. At most, it could only reach the level of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, turning into a ‘primordial treasure’ was already the limit.

Tens of thousands of years, was it really enough time for someone to cultivate to the extent of this ‘Tyrannical Song’?

Moreover, an existence that had reached this realm, it could be said to surpass even the limits of an Immortal.

This kind of existence was interested in a Sixth Stage fairy maiden from her Spirit River Su Clan... Could it be that Fellow Daoist Song had known about her existence beforehand, and had come specifically for her?

After all, she too was a primordial treasure; such beings also held research value. Was he coveting her body?

Chapter 3090: Chapter 3088: You really have a network of the path to immortality, huh?
 

The existence of a ‘primordial treasure’ slumbering within the Ancestor Star of the Spirit River Su Clan was something that very few in the myriad practitioners in the universe knew about, and even those who knew were among their own.

Had it not been for the nearly hundred million laid down previously, Reincarnation Blade Fairy would probably already be deeply suspicious of Tyrannical Song, and might even have isolated him by now.

To gather such a collection of support...

Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

You really do have a network-based method for immortality!

Could one really grasp multiple ‘immortal paths’ within ten thousand years?

“Did you indeed reach this level within ten thousand years?” Reincarnation Blade Fairy looked at Song Shuhang with complexity in her eyes.

Song Shuhang paused slightly, then nodded, “Yes, it was within ten thousand years, no fraud involved.”

“So, your real goal in contacting Su Clan’s Little Fairy was to reach me?” Reincarnation Blade Fairy stared at Song Shuhang, her eyes intently digging deep.

It wouldn’t be something mundane like falling in love with Su Clan’s Little Fairy.

Song Shuhang shook his head and said, “Before today, I was not aware of the fairy’s existence.”

“Then why did you contact the Little Fairy of my Spirit River Su Clan? An entity like you, with ten thousand years of experience in proving his Dao and undergoing full body semi-immortalization, would you have a common crush on my Su Clan’s Little Fairy, ordinary love?” Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked earnestly.

Across the round table, Song Shuhang spoke seriously, “Reincarnation Blade Senior, do you want to hear the truth?”

“Naturally,” replied Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

The White Dragon sister silently regarded Reincarnation Blade Fairy—she had tried not to disclose, but unexpectedly the fairy still bumped into the muzzle herself.

“In fact, it was just last year that I got to know Sixteen,” Song Shuhang said with a gentle smile on his face as he reminisced.

[Last year? That means, at most only a year’s time?] Reincarnation Blade Fairy raised an eyebrow... A ten-thousand-year cultivator becomes intimately involved with Su Clan’s Little Fairy within just one year—is she supposed to believe it was love at first sight?

[Yes my head! Last year, you were at the Foundation Establishment stage, but now you are at the Immortal Realm, full body semi-immortalized, and you have mastered multiple immortal paths?!] Reincarnation Blade Fairy stared at Song Shuhang.

“Do you think I would believe what you’re saying?” The Reincarnation Blade Fairy said.

Song Shuhang generously said, “If the fairy doesn’t believe me, she can fully use her means to test my words.”

If ‘Tyrannical Song’ really was a cultivation newbie who just started last year, then his relationship and feelings with Sixteen could be understood.

But how is it possible to achieve such a thing within one year?

“Come here, hold my hand... I still want to test it using my own methods,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said, extending her hand toward Song Shuhang.

“There’s no need to grab the neck?” Song Shuhang asked subconsciously.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “???”

Why would you want to grab my neck?

[It seems he’s different from Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword?] Song Shuhang revealed a gentle smile to ease the awkwardness.

Then, he reached out and grasped the Reincarnation Blade Fairy’s wrist.

A halo of light enveloped the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

After the halo dissipated, a three-meter-long giant blade appeared in Song Shuhang’s hands.

On the body of the blade, there were designs of the Infernal Realm, Hell Channel, Paradise, and so on.

“My principles are related to reincarnation and also to time,” the voice of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy rang out. “Do you know how to use primordial treasures?”

“I do, I currently have two primordial treasures in my possession,” Song Shuhang answered.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

The next moment, Song Shuhang sat straight, adopting the ‘saber meditation’ posture: “The next step, human-saber fusion!”

A dazzling flash of light went by.

Then, Song Shuhang and the Reincarnation Blade Fairy entered the state of human-saber fusion that sabersmen dream of.

“Is this how you always use primordial treasures?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked with a complicated expression.

“Instinctual hand slip,” Song Shuhang said with embarrassment.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy sighed, “Forget it, the state of human-saber fusion is fine too. Get ready, I’m going to start running it.”

While talking, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy began to activate the full extent of her ‘Reincarnation’ power, covering Tyrannical Song.

——However, this step was actually an ‘security check’!

First, she had to see whether this Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song had been possessed by someone.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy wasn’t guarding against Song Shuhang, but the sly Fourth Heavenly Dao.

The power of the laws flashed past.

The next moment, a piercing alarm sounded from the Reincarnation Blade!

Chapter 3091: Chapter 3089: Transforming into Reincarnation, Experiencing Countless Lives
 

“`

Among them was the phantom of the Dark Sun, which hwo was familiar with as the Fourth Heavenly Dao.

She really did not know how to follow up on Tyrannical Song’s words.

Ever since her interaction with Tyrannical Song began, she felt that he was never not showing off. What made her even more uncomfortable was that it all had been her either actively cooperating with him or forcing him to show off.

I had no idea that the Spirit River Su Clan was concealing the Fifth Heavenly Dao,” Song Shuhang shook his head, “Moreover, my Full Body Semi-Immortal Transformation is already complete; my bones, muscles, skin, and flesh have all achieved Semi-immortalization and no longer lack immortal information.”

This was merely her looking for an excuse to fulfill Sixteen’s wish—in fact, it was not difficult for her, with her state of ascension, to regrow any lost hair.

After looking through ‘small hair growing technique’, the sentient treasure of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy nodded in satisfaction, “The Daoist friend who invented this technique is quite interesting.”

In the meantime, she silently practiced the ‘small hair growing technique’, and red hair that reached her back quickly regrew. However, her main body was still transformed into the blade in Song Shuhang’s hand, so no visible changes could be seen for the time being.

The principle that the Fifth Heavenly Dao attained immortality through was ‘Reincarnation’, and her reason for stepping down was also due to ‘Reincarnation’,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy explained.

If that was the case, the Fifth Heavenly Dao was indeed a unique existence among the previous Heavenly Daos.

Eventually, she found that the rules of death in the myriad practitioners in the universe were too simplistic and disorganized, lacking a comprehensive system. Thus, during her tenure, apart from confronting the remnants of the Fourth Heavenly Dao, she spent the rest of her time perfecting the ‘Reincarnation System’.”

In the final step, the Fifth Heavenly Dao transformed herself into the cycle of reincarnation, using her body of the Heavenly Dao to cast the foundation of reincarnation!

“The very foundation of reincarnation is what I am about to introduce you to now,” said the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, and utilizing the ‘human-saber fusion’ state, she led Song Shuhang’s consciousness downwards.

They plunged into an endless abyss...

Chapter 3092: Chapter 3090: Tyrannical Song, you’ve finally come to pick me up!
 

This “sinking” was also not a physical descent, just as when Song Shuhang’s consciousness had “sublimed” and come into contact with the “Divine Show Saint Rules.”

He had originally thought that he would have to “sink” until reaching the foundation of Reincarnation before coming in contact with the “Immortal Information” of the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

But during the process of sinking, Song Shuhang’s consciousness was already continuously coming into contact with the data of “Reincarnation + Immortality.”

The “passage” through which he sank was infused with the “law and dharma” of the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

The Immortal Information belonging to the Fifth Heavenly Dao kept emerging.

Then... they actively reached out to Song Shuhang, through his consciousness feeding back to his fleshly body on the Su Clan’s Ancestor Star, reinforcing his “mental energy.”

Now that Song Shuhang’s entire body, flesh, bones, and skin had completed Sub-immortalization, even the “Calculation Ability” that needed to be connected later already had Daoist Senior waiting to load cheats for him.

Now, even the last flaw, “mental energy,” has begun to sub-immortalize, transitioning from Immortal-level “immortal yuan” to “Sub-immortal Power.” Combined with the fat whale golden core, its power could rise to another level.

If this wave of Reinforcement is completed and after having the “Daozi calculation cheat” loaded, Tyrannical Song would truly be a little immortal.

Apart from the Will of the Heavens, there would be no one else who could harm him!

...

...

In Song Shuhang’s hands.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy had been paying close attention to his state.

When she saw the “Immortal Information” of the Fifth Heavenly Dao actively making contact with Song Shuhang, her eyelids twitched slightly.

The affinity was too strong!

The “Immortal Information” of the Fifth Heavenly Dao had no conflict when merging with Song Shuhang, as if it were returning to its mother’s home.

“If you weren’t male, I’d have suspected that you might be a reincarnation of my true self,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said aloud.
