In the process of coming into contact with Reincarnation Immortal Data, he could clearly sense the gentle emotions contained within this power of immortality.

—To use his own “Immortal Body” as foundation to perfect the Reincarnation System for the myriad practitioners in the universe was, in itself, a very compassionate act.

As an Immortal Heavenly Dao, having already detached from Life and Death and out of sympathy for all beings, at the cost of its own “Body of Eternity,” it perfected the Reincarnation System to complete the cycle of life for all beings in the Myriad Realms.

To have such a “Heavenly Dao” is the fortune of all beings.

“By the way, was the Reincarnation System imperfect during the reign of the 1-4th Heavenly Daos?” Song Shuhang asked again.

The 1-4th Heavenly Daos, that’s half the number of the Heavenly Daos.

Yet it wasn’t until the Fifth Heavenly Dao that the Reincarnation began to be perfected?

“In ancient times, there might have been a ‘Reincarnation System’ for that era. However, as times changed, the old Reincarnation System seemed too simple and chaotic, unable to meet the demands of the new era, and even leading to the collapse of reincarnation in some worlds,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said.

These problems exploded in the era of the Fifth Heavenly Dao—she even suspected whether the malfunction was caused by the predecessor Will of the Heavens messing things up during his term.

“So, is the Reincarnation System running smoothly now?” Song Shuhang asked.

“It’s running smoothly, but even the current Reincarnation System can’t be called ‘perfect.’ Over these many years, the system centered on the eternal body of the Wielder of the Will is still evolving and being completed... We’re here,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said softly.

“Still evolving and being completed?” The next moment, Song Shuhang felt his consciousness hit the bottom.

At the same time, everything around him began to brighten.

The source of the light was a huge ‘seal.’

The body of the seal was like glass gemstones, with ice crystal-like energy flowing within.

Countless passages were connected to this great seal.

This was the foundation of Reincarnation, evolved from the “Body of Eternity” of the Fifth Heavenly Dao and manifested as the “Reincarnation Seal.”

Song Shuhang could vaguely sense that all planes of the myriad practitioners in the universe were connected to this “Reincarnation Seal.”

Countless passages on the seal manifested the Six Paths of Reincarnation.

However, Song Shuhang couldn’t see the details of these “Reincarnations”—the Reincarnation Blade Fairy brought him to see the ‘seal,’ not the process of Reincarnation.

“Is the body of the Fifth Heavenly Dao in this ‘seal’?” Song Shuhang clasped his hands together and bowed to the Reincarnation Seal.

“That’s right.” The Reincarnation Blade Fairy said, “Come closer, hold one hand on me and lightly touch the seal with the other. The time you can touch it is limited, so how much ‘Immortal’ related information you can get depends on your own fortune. You only have one chance.”

Song Shuhang nodded, followed the instructions of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, approached the Reincarnation Seal, and gently touched it.

“Slip your hand a little,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy reminded.

Song Shuhang was stunned: “That doesn’t seem very nice?”

As they spoke, his current fleshly body, due to the ‘Sub-immortalization’ of immortal energy, began to automatically operate the “Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique.”

The Reincarnation Seal seemed to react as well, resonating faintly with Song Shuhang.

“Eh?” Song Shuhang exclaimed—”The Fifth Heavenly Dao, does it resonate with my ‘Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique?”

In his mind, he immediately recalled the figure of Senior White.

The “Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique” was a masterpiece of Wielder of the Will White.

Could it be that because it’s also a creation, it resonated?

As he pondered, the Reincarnation Seal actively transmitted a large amount of “Immortal Data,” rushing toward him.

More importantly, Song Shuhang sensed that this “Immortal Data” seemed adjusted especially for him—it matched him perfectly!

On the side.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy furrowed her brow—was the seal being too proactive today?

From start to finish, it seemed to be cooperating with Song Shuhang’s actions.

Did Tyrannical Song possess a charm specifically for primordial items?

Would other primordial weapons, primordial treasures, or rulers of the Netherworld also unwittingly aid Tyrannical Song, allowing him to gather an unprecedented Sub-immortal Body?

“You’ve come to fetch me!” At that moment, a voice came from the seal.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “???”

Song Shuhang was also startled: “Fetch you? Me?”

“Yes... Tyrannical Song, you have finally come to fetch me,” the voice continued.

It was calling ‘Tyrannical Song.’

Which meant the other party recognized him and had not mistaken him for someone else.

“It’s me, it’s me, I am buzzing—” the voice said anxiously.

Song Shuhang: “...”

“Unseal! Unleash the secret techniques! Let the memories return!” the voice kept reminding. It seemed unable to call out its own identity, so it could only hint and remind desperately.

As Song Shuhang heard this, a possibility suddenly struck him.

He raised his index and middle fingers in his consciousness: “Clone, unseal.”

Chapter 3093: Chapter 3091: Memories of Tens of Millions of Screens and the Respectable Fifth Heavenly Dao
 

Clone Song Two—this was Song Shuhang’s bold guess!

—The clone Song Two that had previously gone missing along with Lady Onion, Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, and the inner demon of Scarlet Heaven Sword!

Why had the ‘immortal information’ from the Fifth Heavenly Dao been flocking to him as he came along?

Moreover, why did this ‘immortal information’ seem as though it had been adjusted to specifically suit him?

Could it be that in the shadows, there was already someone silently completing everything for him?

Establishing a good relationship with the Fifth Heavenly Dao on his behalf, adjusting the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s ‘immortal information’ ahead of time, and then waiting here for him to catch up?

Thus, he thought of Song Two.

If it were a few months ago, Song Shuhang’s thoughts would not have been so bold, nor his imagination so expansive.

But ever since he found out that the pot Song Muhead was actually his own big pot, Song Shuhang became more daring in his ideas and thoughts about the ‘past’.

Therefore, he attempted to form handprints, unlocking his ‘clone’.

Whoosh whoosh whoosh—

A tide-like surging sound emanated from the Great Seal, the secret clone technique took effect!

Not long ago, ever since clone Song Two had disappeared, Song Shuhang’s ‘secret clone technique’ skill had ‘greyed out’—becoming non-activatable and unable to cancel the clone.

But now, this ‘greyed out’ secret technique was reactivated.

Amidst the surging roar of waves, a joyful voice faintly transmitted, “I’m back.”

—Song Shuhang had guessed right!

The voice from inside the Great Seal was undoubtedly that of clone Song Two.

“Although I don’t know what happened to you during this time... welcome back,” Song Shuhang, maintaining the handprints for ‘retrieving the clone’, said softly.

Rustle rustle—In those waves of cheerful tides, from the ‘Great Seal’, a continuous flow of power began to merge into the main body of Song Shuhang.

...

...

By his side, Reincarnation Blade Fairy was completely stunned.

Why was Tyrannical Song’s clone inside the Great Seal formed from her main body’s Fifth Heavenly Dao using the ‘Immortal Body’?

Aren’t you just nineteen years old this year?

“What on earth is going on?” Reincarnation Blade Fairy tried to remain calm and asked composedly.

If not for the foundations laid down by hundreds of millions of activations of the ‘Saber-Nurturing Technique’, being a primordial treasure herself, she would have already drawn a saber and slashed upon seeing another’s clone hidden within the Great Seal formed by her main body!

“Reincarnation Blade Fairy, please be patient. Let me finish receiving my clone and synchronize the memories. Then, I will explain everything to you,” Song Shuhang said gently.

At the time, both Lady Onion, Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, the inner demon of Scarlet Heaven Sword + clone Song Two had simultaneously vanished.

Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber reappeared at the original spot just moments later, and even accomplished Lady Onion’s ‘eighth transformation,’ allowing Song Shuhang, this ‘Nine Transformations,’ to inherit him.

Moreover, regarding Lady Onion, Song Shuhang also obtained information from Loli Shi and Loli Zhu—Lady Onion appeared to be in a distant future and had undergone a huge transformation, turning into a short-haired young woman.

However, there were no updates regarding Inner Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword and clone Song Two.

Now it seemed, Song Two might have returned to the past and made contact with the Fifth Heavenly Dao?

Whoosh—

The water sound inside the Great Seal stopped.

After a long separation, clone Song Two finally completed the ‘liberation’, the secret clone technique was unlocked, and he merged back into the main body.

At the same time, he brought with him a flood of memories + a massive amount of immortal information.

This section of immortal information was a gift from the Fifth Heavenly Dao and also the effort of Song two’s clone, having already been polished by him and perfectly adapted to the main body of Song Shuhang.

Upon entering his body, Song Shuhang’s fleshly body on Su Clan’s Ancestor Star perfectly received this “immortal information,” and the “immortal energy” inside his body completely transformed, originating from the source of energy, into “sub-immortal.”

The change in energy caused Song Shuhang’s consciousness to shake, and he was in a trance for a moment.

In that moment of distraction, the memories brought back by the clone, Song two, transformed into numerous images before him.

These images did not play in sequence but instantly became thousands of snapshots, forming screens, and projected into the memories in Song Shuhang’s mind.

These screens spoke simultaneously, each playing their content...

What Song Shuhang saw was not only Song two’s memories but also some other images.

For example, on a particularly large and conspicuous screen, he saw an exceptionally beautiful Fairy, barefoot descending into the depths of the abyss.

This Fairy bore an eighty percent resemblance to the “Reincarnation Blade Fairy”—capable of pulling off a bald hairstyle attractively.

Was it the Fifth Heavenly Dao?

At that time, in the image, the Fifth Heavenly Dao had all her “immortal information” converged.

If his guess about her identity was not made, it would have been impossible to discern her identity as a “Heavenly Dao.”

At this time point... she was already in the final step of perfecting “reincarnation,” nearly ready to step down from the seat of Heavenly Dao.

After arriving in the endless abyss, the form of the Fifth Heavenly Dao began to crystallize, quickly transforming into a “Giant Seal.”

Based on this Giant Seal, a new cycle of reincarnation was constructed!

Embodied in reincarnation, her virtue was boundless.

The Giant Seal formed, but the Fifth Heavenly Dao seemed to have paid a great price—not even a single Heavenly Dao’s immortal form could construct the entire “reincarnation” structure in one breath!

After investing her all, what was constructed was merely the rudimentary form of reincarnation.

And it seemed that the Fifth Heavenly Dao was already prepared for this.

Once the Reincarnation Seal was formed and the Reincarnation System was established, “light points” from the Fifth Heavenly Dao emerged from within the Reincarnation Seal, proactively entering into the Reincarnation System, and began to gradually evolve and finalize the system.

Song Shuhang’s gaze shifted from the giant screen to several smaller screens beside it.

In the main world, the Human World, a Fairy was born... Years later, she grew into a petite and cute Fairy, her surname Su.

Years later, in the Dragon Realm, a white real dragon with exceptionally pure bloodline was born, eventually evolving into one of the leading clans of the White Dragon Clan.

After an even longer time, in the Beast Realm, a simple and innocent young girl was born... Unlike the girl surnamed Su and the white real dragon, this simple young girl lived an ordinary life, married ordinarily, had children ordinarily, and ended her ordinary life.

Song Shuhang continued to move his gaze across these smaller screens.

He discovered that the girls on these small screens were from different times and eras.

The time span covered was immense, stretching continuously from the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

The one commonality was that, after their lives ended, they would return to the “Reincarnation Seal,” to supplement and evolve the Reincarnation System.

“Is this the method by which the Fifth Heavenly Dao perfected ‘reincarnation’?” Song Shuhang felt increasing admiration for the Fifth Heavenly Dao in his heart.

This benevolent Heavenly Dao, her actions are worthy of respect by any being in the myriad realms of the universe.

While pondering, Song Shuhang’s gaze fell upon a particularly small screen.

This time, what was born into the world was not a young girl.

From humans, to dragons, to beast cultivators, to other races, the Fifth Heavenly Dao had nearly experienced them all.

And this time... she transformed into an inanimate object.

Song Shuhang’s expression became complex.

He saw the Fifth Heavenly Dao begin to transform into a plant.

Chapter 3094: Chapter 3092: Spirit of Self-Sacrifice
 

“`

The amount of information was overwhelming, and the impact was too intense.

It was so extensive that Song Shuhang’s face couldn’t properly express the ‘meaning’, even if he stood there without wearing a mask, his expressions couldn’t be read! This was a very rare occurrence.

It’s an onion...

On the smallest screen, what the Fifth Heavenly Dao Fairy had transformed into was a green onion shoot, which could be seen everywhere, with nothing special about it.

——I don’t want to be human anymore!

Seeing this scene, Song Shuhang immediately thought of Lady Onion.

Was it a coincidence?

“There usually aren’t such coincidences in this world. The reincarnations constructed by the Fifth Heavenly Dao include the Spirit River Su Clan and the White Dragon Clan, which means that even through reincarnation, as long as she comes into contact with cultivation, her aptitude will still be top-notch. As for Lady Onion... no, her aptitude... it’s top-tier,” Song Shuhang murmured softly.

As soon as he finished speaking, in the plot shown on the small screen, a pair of thick and powerful hands grabbed the green onion shoot, laying it flat on the chopping board, with a shiny kitchen knife about to come down.

Just as the mighty avatar of the Fifth Heavenly Dao was about to be chopped...

But at that moment, the owner of the powerful hands stopped and said aloud, “Wielder of the Will.”

Song Shuhang pressed a hand to his forehead and gently massaged it.

There was no doubt about it.

It was Lady Onion!

The owner of those powerful hands... was Daoist Priest Scarlet Heaven!

Although I don’t know how Senior Scarlet Heaven was able to see that a green onion shoot had the ‘Wielder of the Will’.

But I must say, his discernment was incredibly sharp!

This onion indeed has the foundation of the ‘Wielder of the Will’—because she is the Heavenly Dao! Ahhh!

The Wielder of the Will is not necessarily about becoming the Heavenly Dao after proving one’s Dao and achieving eternity. She came down from the position of the Will of the Heavens, so saying she has the Wielder of the Will is not wrong at all.

If she doesn’t have the ‘Wielder of the Will’, then there wouldn’t be many in the myriad practitioners in the universe who could be called ‘Wielder of the Will’.

That being said.

Since Lady Onion is the reincarnation of the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

“Am I doomed?” Song Shuhang rubbed his cheeks.

My employee is actually an incarnation of the Heavenly Dao.

Yet, I often pinch her green onion shoot.

And even practice the Saber-Nurturing Technique on her.

I’ve turned her, who clearly has the ‘Wielder of the Will’, into a homebody onion.

Moreover, I still owe her part of her salary, which I haven’t been able to pay up to now.

To dare not pay the salary of Lady Onion, who possesses the ‘Wielder of the Will’...

Question: How much longer can I, Tyrannical Song, survive?

How can I explain my relationship with the Fifth Heavenly Dao to the Reincarnation Blade Fairy so she won’t cut me down?

Do I have to wait until I truly prove my Dao and achieve eternity?

Because, only the Heavenly Dao can get away with not paying the Heavenly Dao a salary!

In a flash, Tyrannical Song’s thoughts were in turmoil.

“If... there is still a chance, I have to prepare a batch of spirit stones to properly pay Lady Onion her salary,” Song Shuhang chuckled.

Though, I don’t know if I could save up enough spirit stones.

To be honest.

Even knowing Lady Onion’s identity, Song Shuhang’s heart couldn’t immediately bring together the silly onion and the image of the Fifth Heavenly Dao; the gap between the impressions they gave was too vast.

Actually, these two indeed could be considered as two separate entities prior to the return. However, the ‘beautiful lady’ visual of Lady Onion did share a striking resemblance with the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

“Speaking of which, Lady Onion seems to have changed a lot in the future...”

Perhaps, when we meet again, she’ll reveal her innate skills and become a very dependable ally?

Song Shuhang’s gaze began to move away from the ‘Lady Onion’ screen, starting to search for information about his clone, Song Two—Lady Onion’s and the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s relationship was unexpectedly deep.

“`

But there were other matters that captured his attention.

How had clone Song Two ended up in the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s “Reincarnation Seal,” and how had he become a link in the Great Seal?

In the scene where the avatar of the Fifth Heavenly Dao transforms into the Reincarnation Seal, there was no trace of clone Song Two.

That is to say... did clone Song Two enter that “Great Seal” later on?

What had he experienced during that period?

Song Shuhang’s gaze searched swiftly.

During this search, his gaze once again swept over the images of the White Dragon and Su Clan’s Little Fairy—The White Dragon sister being able to become the guardian of Sixteen without any mutual rejection might be because the Spirit River Su Clan and the real dragon, White Dragon Clan, could trace their origins to a common source.

The White Dragon sister, Su Clan’s Sixteen, Lady Onion, they all had ties with the Fifth Heavenly Dao.

There wouldn’t happen to be yet another fairy by my side who is connected to the Fifth Heavenly Dao, would there?

While he was pondering, the screen that belonged to clone Song Two finally appeared before his eyes.

To be precise, it was the screen about this segment of memory that actively surfaced in front of Song Shuhang—it had a built-in search function.

The starting point of clone Song Two’s memory was when he split from Song Shuhang and was engulfed alongside Lady Onion and the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber into the dimensional vortex.

This was also the point where their memories diverged.

On the screen of memories, Lady Onion is sucked into the dimensional black hole caused by the explosion of the Void Sun, screaming in a high-pitched voice.

The Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber automatically unsheathed to protect her master.

Clone Song Two, grabbing the Scarlet Heaven Sword of the Inner Demon, also entered the black hole vortex, trying to fish out Lady Onion.

However, just as they were clutching Lady Onion and attempting to pull her out, the dimensional black hole suddenly closed, severing their retreat.

The exit disappeared, and they were sucked into the dimensional black hole, drawn by the swallowing power, sinking deeper into the abyss.

Clone Song Two held tightly onto Lady Onion the entire time.

“Boss Song, don’t let go... never let go,” Lady Onion cried out in panic.

“I... I’ll try my best,” clone Song Two gritted his teeth, dragging Lady Onion along.

A man, a green onion, a saber, and a sword struggled desperately in the dimensional black hole.

No one knew how much time had passed.

In the vortex of the black hole, another anomaly occurred—some mechanism within Lady Onion was activated.

Clone Song Two felt a force pulling at Lady Onion, wanting to drag her away, to swallow her.

His instincts told him that if Lady Onion was dragged away... she would likely disappear without a trace.

“I am in clone form; even if I vanish, my main body can use secret techniques to summon me again. But Lady Onion doesn’t have this capability.” Thinking this, clone Song Two made his final decision.

He forcefully pulled Lady Onion away and tossed her aside.

Then, embracing the thought of self-sacrifice, he hurled himself at that “swallowing power.”

If something must be swallowed, let it be me, release my hardworking Lady Onion!

Like the virtuous lamia, being a clone that could be infinitely resurrected through the main body, Song Two faced self-sacrifice without changing his expression.

And then... he lost consciousness.

By the time he awoke, he was already within the “Giant Seal.”

He had not died nor vanished.

It was merely a form of “return.”

Taking with him “the experiences and insights of a lifetime,” he returned to this Reincarnation Seal to perfect the cycle of reincarnation.

In the process of perfecting it.

The names such as Song, “Thirty-Three Divine Beasts’ Technique,” “Saber-Nurturing Technique,” and so on, were all recorded within the “Reincarnation Seal.”

From the Reincarnation Seal, “immortal information” reciprocated, nourishing clone Song Two’s body.

This process lasted a very long time... it felt as long as two or three hundred years!

Two to three hundred years was about the time when Lady Onion came into existence.

Chapter 3095: Chapter 3093: Agreements and Commitments
 

“So that’s how it is, the one who should have ‘returned’ to the Reincarnation Seal was supposed to be Lady Onion. When the time was ripe—after Lady Onion’s cycle of reincarnation ended, she would return to the Reincarnation Seal, feed back her life’s experiences to it, becoming a part of the ‘Reincarnation System’ completion.”

“Moreover, Lady Onion was the final stop for the completion of the ‘Reincarnation System’... which means, after her return, the Fifth Heavenly Dao would no longer continue with the reincarnation and transmigration project.”

“Because the entire Reincarnation System was nearing perfection. Unless something unexpected occurred, the system could meet the needs of the myriad practitioners in the universe. Therefore, after Lady Onion’s return, the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s Reincarnation Cycle would be sealed, forming a perfect loop, with beginning and end interlocking like an Ouroboros, transforming into a circle.”

“And this was why the clone Song Two had an intuitive hunch, feeling that once Lady Onion returned, she would completely disappear. Because once Lady Onion returned, it marked the end of the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s cycle of reincarnation. So, it gave Song Two’s clone a kind of illusion.”

“In fact, under normal circumstances, after Lady Onion’s cycle of reincarnation ended, she, like previous avatars of the Fifth Heavenly Dao, would return to the Reincarnation Seal, guarding the Six Paths of Reincarnation, becoming part of the Reincarnation System which is an aspect of the Fifth Heavenly Dao. Essentially, it’s almost like returning home to inherit the throne.”

“But because of the misunderstanding caused by this intuition, as Lady Onion was about to be consumed, Song Two’s clone forcefully pushed her away, taking her place in returning to the Reincarnation Seal...”

“The life experiences of Song Two’s clone merged into the ‘Reincarnation,’ becoming a part of completing the Reincarnation System... However, he was not Lady Onion, not an incarnation of the Fifth Heavenly Dao Reincarnation. So, he couldn’t become the last part of the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s Reincarnation Cycle, the final bite of the Ouroboros didn’t quite latch on.”

“Fortunately... from what we see now, the Reincarnation Seal is very satisfied with the life experiences of Song Two’s clone. So instead of directly grinding him into dust, it took him in, allowing him to stay within the Reincarnation Seal and even giving him the chance to be nourished by the immortal information.”

When it came to ‘life experiences’ and ‘understandings of death,’ Song Shuhang had confidence in himself.

He didn’t dare say he was the one who died the most throughout history, but over the past year, his number of deaths definitely topped the charts in the myriad realms.

These painful past experiences are an additional harvest for the Fifth Heavenly Dao’s perfection of the ‘Reincarnation System.’ So, even though the last bite of the Ouroboros wasn’t securely fastened, the Reincarnation Seal still treated Song Two’s clone kindly.

“Although the Reincarnation Seal is very satisfied with the life experiences of Song Two’s clone, Lady Onion still needs to be found,” Song Shuhang gently pressed on the ‘Reincarnation Seal’ and nodded his head.

No one can replace the significance of Lady Onion’s existence.

Now that Lady Onion has disappeared... she might have reached the ‘distant future,’ perhaps appearing at some node there.

“I will find a way to bring her back,” Song Shuhang promised to the Reincarnation Seal.

Bringing back Lady Onion isn’t about having her immediately end her ‘reincarnation’ and return to the Reincarnation Seal.

There are two conditions for returning to the Reincarnation Seal.

One is the natural end of Lady Onion’s life cycle, the completion of her onion life.

The other is for Lady Onion to step onto the immortal path, to prove her Dao and become an immortal onion.

After proving her Dao and attaining immortality, there would be more choices available. Lady Onion could choose to return in her onion form, or ‘cut’ out the Fifth Heavenly Dao Reincarnation Light, letting that Reincarnation Light carry the mark of her life cycle back to the Reincarnation Seal.

Song Shuhang hoped to have Lady Onion return to the Reincarnation Seal through the second method—so, if he found Lady Onion, he would use all his efforts, resources, and connections to develop her. He was determined to make her prove her Dao and achieve immortality in the shortest possible time!

After receiving Tyrannical Song’s promise, the energy inside the Reincarnation Seal churned joyfully. She had a good impression of Tyrannical Song and was willing to believe his promise at this moment.

The task of finding Lady Onion, she gladly entrusted to Tyrannical Song.

To facilitate future contact, the Reincarnation Seal left a ‘mark’ on Tyrannical Song’s arm.

Then, Song Shuhang’s consciousness returned.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy gently led him, as his consciousness left the Reincarnation Seal and returned to the Reincarnation Hall on Ancestor Star.

...

...

In the Su Clan’s Ancestral Star, within the Reincarnation Hall.

Song Shuhang’s entire body once again entered the pure lustrous body state, in which all his immortal yuan was transformed into a ‘Sub-immortal’ state within his glass-like body.

The Sub-immortal energy incessantly circulated within his lustrous body, as beautiful as a work of art.

“It’s a success,” The White Dragon murmured softly.

She knew that with Tyrannical Song taking action, he would never return empty-handed.

To this point, Song Shuhang had assembled the immortal information from the 2nd to the 8th Heavenly Dao... Soon after, he would gain an additional cheat from the 8.5th Heavenly Daozi.

“Yes, it was a success,” Song Shuhang opened his eyes, the flawless state of his glass-like body slowly fading away.

“Can you now explain what’s going on? Why was your clone in the Reincarnation Seal?” the voice of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy resonated from his hand.

“Fairy, please be patient,” Song Shuhang released his grip, letting go of the blade.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy transformed into her human form, her dazzling red hair flying about.

“My ‘clone’ entering the Reincarnation Seal was actually due to a ‘misunderstanding’. It should have been my... dear friend Lady Onion who was supposed to return to the Reincarnation Seal, but since my clone did not understand the situation, thinking that Lady Onion might encounter an accident, he pushed her aside and took her place. Then, he was absorbed by the Reincarnation Seal,” Song Shuhang explained.

The White Dragon: “...”

Since when did Lady Onion become your dear friend?

And how could Lady Onion be related to the ‘Fifth Heavenly Dao’?

There’s so much information here.

“After being absorbed by the Reincarnation Seal, the ‘lifetime experiences’ of my clone were also absorbed, becoming material to perfect the Reincarnation. I believe, Fairy, your familiarity with me and the feeling toward my techniques all stem from this,” Song Shuhang added.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy tapped her chin thoughtfully, nodding slightly.

“Regarding Lady Onion, you can rest assured, Fairy. I will find a way to bring her back,” Song Shuhang continued.

He glossed over some content while explaining his clone.

The ‘Ouroboros’ Reincarnation of the Fifth Heavenly Dao might likely trigger a temporal loop.

The disappearance of clone Song Two in the main world was an event that happened this year, yet the time he spent inside the Reincarnation Seal was entirely unsynchronized with the main world. This was also why he reacted so emotionally upon meeting with his main body.

However, these aspects are something the Reincarnation Blade Fairy might understand even more about, and so Song Shuhang didn’t waste too many words on them.

“So, essentially, the ‘immortal information’ of the Fifth Heavenly Dao has belonged to you all along. Your coming here was just a formality,” The White Dragon said.

The clones of the Tyrannical Song family and those of Fellow Daoist White’s family shared a curious similarity. Both belonged to a very capable series, where the main body could just lie down and relax while the clone silently took care of everything, an enviable situation.

Song Shuhang gave a sheepish smile, then he turned his gaze toward Sixteen’s location.

“The evolution aspect for Sixteen, I can also lend her a helping hand,” Song Shuhang extended an arm, revealing the mark of the Reincarnation Seal.

Chapter 3096: Chapter 3094: Seven Blade Tyrannical Song
 

After recalling his clone, Song Two, a vast array of memories returned to him, along with fragments of memories from the “Fifth Heavenly Dao Reincarnation”.

Therefore, Song Shuhang was well-versed in the “Transformation Process” that Su Clan’s Sixteen was currently undergoing—it was all thanks to Song Two.

The Spirit River Su Clan was the first stop in the reincarnation project initiated by the “Fifth Heavenly Dao” and held a particularly special strategic position.

As this was the first experiment, the Fifth Heavenly Dao made extensive preparations before reincarnation and endowed the initial reincarnated beings with a lot of innate powers. This also led to the descendants of the Spirit River Su Clan inheriting some special innate abilities.

Among them, the talent to transform into a saber, just like the “Dao Artifact·Reincarnation Blade”, was the strongest hidden innate skill of the Su Clan.

However, because the Fifth Heavenly Dao was a fairy herself, this talent was slightly biased towards females over males, with most of the awakeners of this hidden talent being the fairy maidens of the Su Clan.

The ability was inherently more suitable for those with a “Fairy Physique”.

The number of male immortals in the Su Clan who could awaken this talent was relatively small.

The mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan, Su Clan’s Knot, was one who awakened this talent, but he was a mutated version—a Swordsmen.

If nothing unexpected happened, with Sixteen’s character and innate skill, upon activating her talent, she could potentially transform into a godly weapon similar to the Reincarnation Blade.

Normally, if a Saber woman had a dao companion, the two could grow together and rely on each other. The level of emotional closeness between them could exceed that of ordinary dao companions by several times.

—Because, aside from the typical romantic relationship, a Saber woman and her dao companion could also attain a state of “human-saber fusion” both physically and mentally, something ordinary dao companions could not achieve.

Moreover, there were techniques like the “Saber-Nurturing Technique” that could increase their daily closeness.

Even for those sabersmen who are like “Lonely Swordsmen” and have only their saber in their heart, desiring nothing else, obtaining a Saber woman would allow them to reap the benefits of both career and love.

However... between Song Shuhang and Su Clan’s Sixteen, there wasn’t any more time for “growing together”.

Time, that stingy boss, was always reluctant to give him more time to grow slowly.

If Su Clan’s Sixteen were to transform into a proper Saber woman, she could only add in some adult fun for Song Shuhang, but wouldn’t be able to join in the grand scheme that Song Shuhang was about to face.

It was all the world’s fault!

But deep down, Song Shuhang still hoped that in the upcoming events, he and Su Clan’s Sixteen could face them together just like any ordinary dao companions of a Saber woman.

—Hand in hand, retreating or advancing together, is also a pleasure for mature dao companions.

“Sixteen.” Song Shuhang softly called out to Su Clan’s Sixteen, who was in the midst of her transformation.

“Hmm.” Su Clan’s Sixteen, in the middle of her transformation, softly responded.

In this call and response, they had already completed a mental exchange.

Understanding is also a form of pleasure.

Song Shuhang rolled up his sleeves, revealing his “Reincarnation Seal” mark that was sparkling.

He took the initiative to partake in Sixteen’s transformation process.

“What does he want to do?” The White Dragon, resting on the neck of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, habitually coiled around—it was primarily because the aura on the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was somewhat similar to Sixteen’s, provoking an instinctive reaction from the White Dragon.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy seems to enjoy it, gently rubbing against the white dragon around her neck, and replied, “He probably wants to push Sixteen’s transformation even further. With the mark of the Reincarnation Seal, it might actually be successful.”

“What will happen if it goes one step further?” the White Dragon asked.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy herself was not sure and answered, “Become a top-tier Saber woman?”

“That sounds pretty good... but unfortunately, even a top-tier Saber woman seems to be lacking a little,” the White Dragon whispered.

She was well aware that the situation Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song was about to face would require at least Immortal-level strength to participate, and not even average Immortals could get involved.

Therefore...

The White Dragon sighed, “It would be nice if she could become a primordial treasure.”

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

You guys still dare to say you’re not after me?

Even a top-tier Saber woman isn’t good enough, are you planning to fight the will of the heavens?

Wait a minute.

Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song seemed to actually plan to go against the Will of the Heavens.

Moreover...

Reincarnation Blade Fairy glanced at Tyrannical Song—his whole body in a Sub-immortal Mode was akin to a minor Will of the Heavens walking the main world.

For Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, it seemed that even top saber women were somewhat lacking in interest.

Only weapons at the pinnacle of Immortal level or dao artifacts would suit his hand.

“Actually, if the fairy maidens from the Spirit River Su Clan evolved their ‘innate abilities’ to the limit and transformed into top saber women, they could borrow my power at critical moments,” revealed the Reincarnation Blade Fairy—she wouldn’t let anyone underestimate the function of a saber woman!

The disciples of the Spirit River Su Clan, once they awoke their hidden innate skill, it was just like ‘Ancestral Return’.

At critical moments, by transforming into blades and connecting with her power, they could bring her power into the main world, allowing the Su Clan’s saber women to transform into Reincarnation Blades.

Moreover, since both parties were originally ‘of the same origin,’ their powers did not repel each other. The Reincarnation Blades transformed by the Su Clan’s saber women in a short span of time were no different from the true Reincarnation Blades and were indeed at the ‘dao artifact’ rank.

“I see, in that case, Sixteen and Shuhang have the opportunity to join hands and advance or retreat together,” The White Dragon smiled in relief, her smile akin to that of an old mother.

“Speaking of which, what dao artifacts does Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song possess?” asked the Reincarnation Blade Fairy—if Sixteen evolved into a top saber woman, perhaps she would soon have the chance to meet the other two dao artifacts in Tyrannical Song’s possession. As dao artifacts themselves, it would be good to get to know some information in advance, so things wouldn’t be too awkward when they met.

“They should be those two dao artifacts, first is the ‘big-eyed planet’ from the Second Wielder of the Will, a strategic weapon. Second is the ‘Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber’ from the third Heavenly Dao, which has already completed the Ninth Revolution,” replied The White Dragon.

“He already has a saber? And also a dao artifact-grade one? Then why is he flirting with the Spirit River Su Clan’s fairy maidens? What a scoundrel among sabersmen,” said the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

After thinking for a moment, The White Dragon said, “Double saber attack?”

Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

“Actually, beside the Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, Shuhang also has a special sword, the Scarlet Heaven Sword. Although it appears as a sword, it’s actually a saber at heart. So, Triple Sword Style?” pondered The White Dragon.

Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “...”

“Right, within the Combined Magical Treasure of the thirty-three animals, there’s also ‘The Tyrant Cuttlefish’s Twin Blades,’ which are dual sabers in one. Tyrannical Song has two sets, making it four blades. So... Seven Blade Style?” The White Dragon got more excited as she spoke.

One saber in each hand, another gripped in the mouth, two sabers on the left leg, and two on the right leg, with a full split.

Seven Blade Tyrannical Song, scary, isn’t it?

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy was at a loss for words.

Clang~

At that moment, from the location of Song Shuhang and Su Clan’s Sixteen, a sharp sound of a blade unsheathing rang out.

Sixteen stretched out her arms, and a phantom of a saber emerged from her chest.

However, before Sixteen could fully transform into a saber woman, Song Shuhang stepped forward, extending his palm towards the phantom of the saber.

The phantom of the Reincarnation Seal brightened upon his arm.

Human-saber fusion.

A dazzling light halo enveloped Song Shuhang and Sixteen.

After a few breaths...

A small ‘Great Seal’ appeared before The White Dragon and the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

Reincarnation Blade Fairy: “???”

The White Dragon: “???”

Where’s the saber woman? What happened to the promised top saber woman? Where did she go?

And what about Tyrannical Song?

Where did that big Tyrannical Song go?

“Fusion?” The White Dragon wondered aloud.

Was this ‘Great Seal’ the Combined Evolution of Sixteen plus Song Shuhang?

Chapter 3097: Chapter 3095: The Only Guess in All Realms
 

Why would the Saber woman mode of Sixteen + Song Shuhang turn into a Great Seal?

What is the principle behind this?

I can understand even if you transform into a Mother and Child Saber, or even dual swords.

But turning from a saber into a Great Seal, isn’t that a bit of a stretch? What is the connection between the two?

“The only connection between the two... might just be the Reincarnation Seal,” said the Reincarnation Blade Fairy as she looked up at the sky, her mood complex. Apparently, she hadn’t anticipated this scene either.

The White Dragon sister looked puzzled: “???”

She hadn’t dived into consciousness with Song Shuhang, nor had she come into contact with the Fifth Heavenly Dao, so she was unaware of the ‘Reincarnation Seal.’

But hearing the name ‘Reincarnation Seal,’ it clearly seems to be something that complements the Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade or something from the same origin, right?

Could it be that the Fifth Heavenly Dao has two Dao artifacts?

“The Reincarnation Seal is the foundation of the reincarnation reforged by the main body of my Fifth Heavenly Dao, transformed from her Body of Eternity. I just took Tyrannical Song there,” explained the Reincarnation Blade Fairy.

The White Dragon sister blinked her eyes.

She had still underestimated the ability of Tyrannical Song to stir things up.

Is it worthy of being ‘Song•Anything-Can-Rub•Shuhang’?

—A top-notch Saber woman? A Saber woman who can temporarily manifest as a Dao artifact?

For Song Shuhang... it’s not just that!

Anything he comes into contact with, he always manages to rub a little something from it.

So, after assisting Sixteen in becoming a top-notch Saber woman, Song Shuhang even threw himself into the mix, using the Reincarnation Seal’s power to further himself and Sixteen, achieving a Combined Evolution.

Then the ‘Reincarnation Seal’ was conjured forth.

Just like the projection of the ‘Dao Artifact•Reincarnation Blade,’ the Combined Evolution of Tyrannical Song + Su Clan’s Sixteen materialized as ‘Reincarnation Seal,’ with power almost equal to the Reincarnation Seal itself.

“It can probably attack 2-3 times,” said Song Shuhang’s voice from within the Reincarnation Seal.

“It’s because my power is still too low. If I were stronger, we could bring forth more power,” said Sixteen somewhat unsatisfied, feeling discontent with the speed of her advancement, although she was already advancing rapidly.

“No worries, about power... we have plenty of opportunities to enhance it. The main thing is not to leave behind any hidden dangers but to take it step by step, steadily and surely,” Song Shuhang consoled.

Moreover, being able to hit the Reincarnation Seal 2-3 times after one fusion, the effect was already awesome. At a critical moment, it might even turn the tables—especially since the Fifth Heavenly Dao always bears a grudge against the Fourth Heavenly Dao. Power against the Fourth Heavenly Dao might at least double!

The White Dragon sister rolled her eyes.

In all the myriad realms, only you, Tyrannical Song, are not in a position to say that.

“Shuhang, next time before we merge for an evolution, let me do an experiment first. I have a conjecture that might enhance the ‘Reincarnation Seal’s’ power,” pondered Sixteen.

“I also just had a bold idea,” Song Shuhang said with a smile.

Then the two simultaneously voiced in unison as if by tacit agreement, “Before merging for an evolution, first maximize the ‘Saber Transformation’ power, borrowing the power of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy to evolve temporarily into a Dao artifact. On this basis, perform a Combined Evolution.”

By doing so, they could possibly bring the Reincarnation Blade’s power to its limits.

The Reincarnation Blade Fairy said discontentedly, “Do you guys see me as a tool person?”

“My condolences,” consoled the White Dragon sister.

Whether a tool person or not, it didn’t really matter to the White Dragon sister. She felt that as long as Tyrannical Song’s Saber-Nurturing Technique was up to the mark by then, the Reincarnation Blade Fairy would be very willing to lend Tyrannical Song and Sixteen a helping hand.

After all, Tyrannical Song’s “Saber-Nurturing Technique” is a demonic technique considered secret by the Heavenly Dao and many rulers of the Netherworld.

“That’s about it, let’s end this mode for now. Maintaining this mode puts a lot of pressure on your body, Sixteen,” said Song Shuhang aloud.

“Release!” Sixteen softly exclaimed as the two exited the “Reincarnation Seal Mode”.

In the halo of light, Sixteen’s figure also transformed back to her human form.

The White Dragon danced around, leaving the neck of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, and landed back on Sixteen.

The abandoned Reincarnation Blade Fairy touched her neck—strangely enough, she felt somewhat nostalgic about the White Dragon entangled around her neck.

The White Dragon scarf provided warm and intimate protection.

“Could it be because part of the White Dragon Branch from the Dragon Realm, also has the bloodline of the Fifth Heavenly Dao reincarnation in their main body? Is that why I feel this nostalgia? Should I consider going to the Dragon Realm to find a White Dragon to bring back?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy thought to herself.

The White Dragon, unaware of the Reincarnation Blade Fairy’s lingering attachment, returned to Sixteen’s neck, coiled around it, and asked, “After becoming Saber Woman, do you feel any different? Has your body undergone any changes?”

“Hmm, besides the ‘dantian’, it seems there’s also another type of energy core in my body. I share the power of this energy core with all the other Sixteens; it’s also the foundation of my ability to transform into a blade,” Sixteen replied.

Besides that, her strength had also slightly increased.

Moreover, this trend of increase was still gently rising and hadn’t stopped.

Could this be the reward for her decision to preserve all ‘Sixteen personalities’?

“No other changes?” the White Dragon asked—she seemed to be expecting more significant reactions.

Sixteen shook her head.

The White Dragon looked somewhat disappointed.

Then, she turned to Song Shuhang and asked, “What about you, Shuhang? When you transformed into the Reincarnation Seal, did you feel any changes in your body, or did you have any special sensations?”

“I was just aiding Sixteen in evolving, transforming into the ‘Reincarnation Seal’, I actually only borrowed the Sub-immortal attribute of mine... so, in fact, my body didn’t undergo any changes,” Song Shuhang replied with a smile.

And now, as his entire being had turned ‘Sub-immortal’, his body was already hard to alter—even heavenly punishment couldn’t faze him now!

When the opportunity arises, he could cooperate with Daozi to try out the top dog of heavenly tribulations—the heavenly punishment.

“As for special sensations, there might be some,” Song Shuhang said, stroking his chin and closing his eyes to recall the sensations he felt during their combined evolution with Sixteen.

The biggest sensation should have been the overwhelming feeling of being connected with hundreds of ‘Mini-Sixteens’ and Su Clan’s Sixteen.

After a while,

Song Shuhang tried to summarize, “Unique in all the Myriad Realms, a legend amongst myriad practitioners in the universe?”

This was an experience that even Daozi, who utilized a loophole to prove his Dao as the 8.5th Heavenly Dao, had never felt.

Heavenly Dao does not necessarily possess or understand the ‘principles of Time’.

But every Heavenly Dao might interfere with ‘Time’.

This interference might even go unnoticed by the ‘Heavenly Dao’ itself.

For instance... the ‘Time River Sea Urchin Spur’ that he saw back then. If it truly exists and isn’t just conjecture, every sea urchin spur on the river of time undergoes many different changes.

But perhaps all ‘Historical Heavenly Daos’ on each sea urchin spur are the same?

Of course, this was Song Shuhang’s speculation.

It’s not certain.

“Anyway, let’s go back to the ‘Ancient Nether World’ and continue planting columns,” Song Shuhang opened his eyes.

Historical ‘Prospective Heavenly Dao’ all went to the Ancient Nether to plant columns.

Senior White is still waiting there.

Chapter 3098: Chapter 3096: The Stage Is Set, Just Waiting for the Actors to Take Their Places
 

“You’re leaving so soon, don’t you want to stay a bit longer?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy asked.

In the past, when disciples from the Su Clan finished their evolution with her, they would try to stay longer.

If she was awake, she could take some time to give speeches and provide guidance to the disciples of the Su Clan.

If she was asleep, just observing the nature of the primordial treasure itself could bring endless enlightenment to the Su Clan’s disciples.

But now, after the evolution was complete, Tyrannical Song and Su Clan’s Sixteen seemed eager to leave, causing her to feel a touch of disappointment—a twinge in her heart. Even if you have two primordial treasures at home, making such treasures seem less precious, you could still show some respect and stay a bit longer, just for courtesy.

“There’s no need to be polite, Reincarnation Blade Senior, just leave us an access permission... We’ll come to visit whenever we can. We’re a bit busy today, we have to go to the Ancient Nether and plant some pillars,” Song Shuhang replied with a smile.

Well, when someone says ‘don’t stay any longer,’ it’s generally just being polite, so he figured the Reincarnation Blade Fairy was probably just being courteous with them as well.

“Fine, I’ll give you the permission to open the door. But every time you come over, give me a shout first. If I’m awake, then come over,” the Reincarnation Blade Senior declared.

“Then Senior, we’ll see you in a bit,” Song Shuhang waved his hand—he would definitely come over whenever he was free. Even if his main body was busy, he could use a clone to accompany Su Clan’s Sixteen and observe the form of the Reincarnation Blade’s primordial treasure, which would be beneficial for Sixteen’s cultivation.

“By the way, if you’re leaving, does Fellow Daoist White Dragon have any business here? If not, stay behind and chat with me for a bit?” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy added at the last moment, unable to help herself.

The White Dragon was clearly puzzled: “???”

Why did the Reincarnation Blade Fairy suddenly become so familiar with her? Were they even that compatible in conversation?

“No, I have some things to deal with as well. I feel I’m about ready to resurrect,” replied the White Dragon after some thought, tactfully refusing: “I’ll come and chat with you after my resurrection, Reincarnation Blade Daoist.”

Now, in her current state of being a body of virtue, being away from Sixteen for extended periods of time would eventually prove inconvenient... Once her real body was resurrected, she would come and keep the Reincarnation Blade Fairy company, to see if it was possible to take her out for a stroll.

“Then it’s settled,” the Reincarnation Blade Fairy said cheerfully.

The White Dragon nodded in response.

—By the way, am I really that charming?

The White Dragon became curious about herself.

...

...

After getting the access permission from the Reincarnation Blade Fairy, Song Shuhang took Sixteen and traversed through space to arrive outside the Reincarnation Hall—Su Clan’s Shield Maiden and Su Clan’s Knot were waiting for them outside.

“Has Sixteen completed her metamorphosis?” Su Clan’s Shield Maiden caught a glimpse of Sixteen and affirmed instantly.

“Yes, thanks to the blessings of the Fairy and the Ancestor,” Sixteen responded with a bow toward her two ancestors.

“What are your plans next?” asked Su Clan’s Knot Ancestor.

“First, we need to take a trip to the Ancient Nether to establish a root pillar...” Song Shuhang replied softly.

After that, their time was limited.

Daoist Senior was already preparing his plans for abdication.

“Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, you’re always so busy... I envy you young folks, always brimming with endless tasks and seemingly inexhaustible vigor,” mused Su Clan’s Knot Ancestor.

He hadn’t known Tyrannical Song for very long, but from their interactions, he always got the impression that Tyrannical Song was perpetually ‘running.’

Rushing forward without ever stopping.

It was only during the Su Clan’s annual gatherings, when members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group took the time to rest together, that he saw Tyrannical Song’s ‘overbearing run’ come to a brief pause—that group was the haven for Tyrannical Song’s soul.

This relentless version of Tyrannical Song reminded the Knot Ancestor of himself from a very long time ago, when he was also young and full of vigor.

“Actually, I’m not as great as you make it sound,” Song Shuhang said modestly.

“A motivated salted fish.” the White Dragon said slowly.

Song Shuhang: “...”

“When you’re done with your busy schedule, if you have time, come find us at Su Clan.” Su Clan’s Knot said. “After that, let’s form a group and go check out the ‘Gem Domain’ together.”

“Gem Domain? Is that Spirit River Su Clan’s territory?” Song Shuhang asked.

Su Clan’s Knot was taken aback and asked in confusion, “Fellow Daoist Tyrannical Song, you don’t know?”

Song Shuhang: “???”

“In the Gem Domain, there are ‘Tombs of Immortality’ of both the Second Wielder of the Will and the Third Wielder of the Will showing their divinity at the same time. This news has already spread throughout the myriad practitioners in the universe... Right now, many Immortals and Tribulation Transcenders must have gone to the Gem Domain. After all, they are relics of two Wielders of the Will.” Su Clan’s Knot replied.

Song Shuhang stroked his chin, contemplating.

The ‘Tombs of Immortality’ of Senior Three Eyes and Heavenly Dao Father Goudan?

And they both appeared in the same place?

This must be a trap!

Because, if Senior Three Eyes’ Tomb of Immortality was in the ‘Gem Domain’, the first thing Heavenly Dao Father Goudan would do is definitely to dig up Senior Three Eyes’ ancient tomb and scatter the ashes. Then he would transform Senior Three Eyes’ tomb into his own and install himself inside.

There can be no second possibility. Heavenly Dao Father Goudan would certainly do something like that.

So, the simultaneous appearance of two tombs is absolutely impossible!

At this thought, Song Shuhang’s mind stirred, and he remembered the words of ‘Daozi’ Senior—Daozi Senior was secretly scheming a ‘premature retirement’ plan. Moreover, he was secretly trying to gather all the ‘Immortals’ from the myriad practitioners in the universe.

Now it seemed that this might be the trap that Daozi Senior, Heavenly Dao Father Goudan, and Senior Three Eyes had set up together.

“I’ll go. If I return early, I’ll make arrangements with the Seniors and head there together,” Song Shuhang nodded.

Once the ‘Immortals’ of the heaven and earth gathered enough, according to Daozi Senior’s script, it would be his or Senior White’s turn to make an entrance and accept challenges from the big shots of the myriad practitioners in the universe, right?

The stage was already set.

Just waiting for the actors to take their places.

...

...

Black Dragon World • Ancient Nether

The self-corpse maintained a power-output posture, sustaining a pillar that resembled an ‘Overlord God Pillar’ with energy.

Senior White squatted on the ground, drawing a circle with a branch.

Inside the circle, some of the ‘Ancient Nether’ special creatures were hopping around—it was something like a small crayfish, milky white in color, and possessing great jumping strength.

Senior White confined them within the circle, and any creature that jumped out was promptly flicked back into the circle with the branch.

Chu Pavilion Master’s Dumb Hair was stuck to Senior White’s head, constantly swaying, its tip penetrating the vacuum and occasionally capturing new ‘small crayfish’ to bring over for Senior White to play with.

“They look quite tasty.” Scarlet Heaven Sword returned to its sword form, floating in the vacuum.

Meteor Sword followed behind it, seeming envious of Scarlet Heaven Sword.

At that moment, a space gate opened.

“I’m back.” Song Shuhang stepped through the space gate and said, “Senior White, I have some new insights regarding the ‘Sole Dominator of Myriad Realms’ concept. It might relate to the Ancient Nether’s pillar insertion. I’ll transmit these insights to you, please receive them!”

“Sole Dominator of Myriad Realms? Are you going to kill all the other Song Shuhangs?” Senior White looked up, his face full of confusion.

Chapter 3099: Chapter 3097: Sorry, Please Forgive Me... For Giving You All the Pressure and Burden
 

“How could that be possible... Moreover, I don’t have the ability to do that,” Song Shuhang waved his hand and said.

Previously, with the help of the seniors’ power, he could briefly see the other ‘Song Shuhangs’ on the ‘time river sea urchin spines’.

But that kind of seeing was just like sitting in front of a screen watching a ‘movie.’ It was impossible to interfere with the world inside the movie.

Let alone kill off all the ‘Shuhangs.’

There are dimensions of distance involved.

Besides, it was not in his nature to do such a thing.

It’s said that men should be a little cruel to themselves.

But cruelty should have purpose and direction.

Not senseless, constant cruelty to oneself... that would be masochistic.

“I’ll transmit my new insights about ‘The Only One in Myriad Realms’ to you, Senior White,” Song Shuhang said, activating the data transfer mode between himself and Senior White.

Their data transfer didn’t need to go through the ‘Cultivator Chat System.’

With the mutual assimilation of ‘Confucian Saint Talent,’ they developed a unique ‘direct connection’ mode of communication. Data transfer was faster, almost to the level of synchronization between a clone and the main body.

“I see,” Senior White nodded after receiving the data.

This portion of insight was summarized by Song Shuhang after his encounter with the ‘time river’ plus ‘Su Clan’s Reincarnation Seal.’

There was a process to becoming ‘The Only One in Myriad Realms,’ extending from the Netherworld Realm to the heavens.

Song Shuhang speculated that from ancient times to the present, all ‘Heavenly Dao Candidates’ came to the Ancient Nether world to insert pillars, which likely related to the process of ‘descending to the Netherworld.’

Thus, at this moment, Song Shuhang had an idea—could he transmit the seed to all the ‘Song Shuhangs’ by inserting pillars in the ‘Ancient Nether World’?

By utilizing the power of the ‘seed,’ could he achieve a singular ending without changing all the ‘Shuhangs’?

“Maybe it could work, projecting your seed into the time river,” Senior White felt the proposal was feasible.

“Shuhang’s... seed?” Sixteen’s cheeks flushed.

The White Dragon also circled around Sixteen’s neck somewhat awkwardly.

“If we’re going to do this, the form this ‘pillar’ takes will have to change,” Senior White said as he dropped a branch and looked at the ‘pillar’ maintained by his self-corpse.

The pillar erected by the self-corpse, like those placed by ‘Heavenly Dao candidates’ of previous generations, was there to leave one’s information at the world’s node, leaving a footprint.

“How should it change?” Song Shuhang asked.

He was just putting forward suggestions and ideas, as for how to actually operate, he was powerless.

“If it were before, sealing you within the pillar and leaving behind a ‘Tyrannical Song’s Body’ would have been the most convenient operation. But now, that can no longer be done,” Senior White said regretfully.

Song Shuhang, now with a full body semi-immortal, no longer had the option to leave behind a body.

“Then, shall I send my clone in my stead?” Song Shuhang suggested.

“No need, I’ll carve a few spots on this pillar, and you just need to stamp your ‘Sage Seals’ inside. The effect might be a bit less, but it should be sufficient,” Senior White waved his hand and replied.

Sage Seal of Tyrannical Song, Tyrannical Scholar Demon Seal, Tyrannical Dragon Ancient Seal, Tyrannical Demon Sage Seal, Dao Seal of Tyranny, Tyrannical You Tai Seal, Tyrannical Saber’s Seal, Seal of the Overlord World, and Ba Mei’s Sage Seal.

Song Shuhang in one breath brought out the Nine Great Sage Seals, following Senior White’s instruction, stamped his own Sage Seals at various positions on the ‘pillar.’

Finally, Song Shuhang asked, “Senior White, do you need to stamp a Sage Seal as well?”

“I don’t need to,” Senior White shook his head: “Moreover, I have already participated in the erecting of the pillar, that is enough.”

He had no need for the option of ‘The Only One in Myriad Realms.’

Song Shuhang nodded thoughtfully.

“Let’s go, to the next node.” After the pillar was established, Senior White beckoned.

As with the pioneers of the past, the nodes that needed to have pillars inserted were more than just one.

Senior White and his self-corpse worked together to forge the pillar, and it was Song Shuhang’s main body’s responsibility to go up and stamp the nine seals in quick succession.

After a day and a night...

All nodes, and the erection of the pillars, were completed.

Song Shuhang reached out and branded a Sage Seal on the last ‘pillar’: “It’s over.”

“It’s just begun,” Senior White reminded him.

After the pillars were erected, the plan Song Shuhang wanted – to project the seeds into the river of time – could begin.

Song Shuhang put away the Nine Great Sage Seals and then closed his eyes, gathering his focus to brace for any possible changes.

After a long while...

“Do you feel anything?” Chu Pavilion Lord’s Dumb Hair asked.

Song Shuhang shook his head.

This time, he hadn’t sensed the ‘river of time’; he couldn’t see parallel versions of himself on the sea urchin spines.

“Did it fail?” Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword asked.

“I’m not sure,” Song Shuhang looked towards Senior White.

“It’s already a success,” Senior White spoke softly.

In those brief moments, Senior White had seen many scenes.

Each one was related to Song Shuhang.

Song Shuhang while eating.

Song Shuhang while asleep.

There was Song Shuhang doing homework.

And Song Shuhang taking a bath.

There was Tyrannical Song who couldn’t be reflected in mirrors.

There was Tyrannical Song sitting face-to-face with Fairy Soft Feather, talking.

Some were smiling joyfully, others were crying out loud.

A myriad of life vignettes composed the kaleidoscopic Song Shuhang.

And at this moment, every Song Shuhang was paired with a seed.

Each seed contained Song Shuhang’s intentions.

...

...

In a world of grey hues.

Lady Onion, with short hair and clad in white skinny jeans and high heels, jumped from the air with style, striding forward with elegant catlike steps into the depths of the world.

Behind her rode Soft Feather on a multicolored butterfly.

Her long hair covered half of her face, giving her an appearance of being still half asleep.

“Soft Feather, did you use the power of time again?” Lady Onion, at the front, turned her head, her short hair swishing as she asked.

“Sorry, but this is the last time,” Soft Feather looked up, responding.

After this, she no longer had the chance to visit that peaceful world of Senior Song again.

Lady Onion sighed.

She had wanted to scold Soft Feather a bit, but seeing her worn-out appearance, suppressed the words that had almost reached her lips.

“Forget it, let’s go... Let’s check on Boss Song and see if his retreat has ended yet. He owes me wages, and it’s time he paid up.” Lady Onion handsomely tucked her hands into her pockets and continued forward with long strides.

‘Creak~’

Ahead, the heavy sound of a stone gate opening resonated.

Then, a warm-smiling Song Shuhang who looked slightly aged emerged from behind the gate.

Lady Onion, who had been moving forward with her stylish catwalk, was suddenly suspended mid-step and didn’t land for several moments.

“Sorry for worrying you all,” Shuhang said in a gentle and dependable voice.

In his hand, a bright seed flickered faintly.

“I’m sorry, please forgive me for passing all the pressure and burdens onto you...” he said softly with palms pressed together.

Everything was about to start... and then, it was also about to end!

Chapter 3100: Chapter 3098: The War Begins!
 

“It took a whole day and night, the time it took to plant the column was longer than I expected,” Senior White rubbed his eyes.

Then, Senior White transmitted the information about the ‘Kaleidoscope Tyrannical Song Life’ he had just witnessed back to Song Shuhang, so he knew the seed had reached the end of the river of time.

[Fortunately, Senior White was here, as he could see the ‘seed’ projected onto the river of time.]

Song Shuhang closed his eyes and began to search within the ‘Kaleidoscope Tyrannical Song Life’... Soon, he found an older version of himself that resembled Tyrannical Song.

“So, it has been conveyed!” Song Shuhang murmured, a smile appearing at the corner of his mouth.

This older Tyrannical Song should be himself from the world where ‘Future Child’ is, right?

The Future Child could no longer come over due to the restrictions of the ‘space spell’... So now, let me convey my ‘intent’ and ‘response’ over there!

Distant Future Child, on my end, war... is about to begin!

Did you receive the message?

“What has been conveyed?” Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair bent down, its tip asking the question.

“Belief, or rather, my decision,” Song Shuhang laughed and then said, “Next, the following step... are we going to the Gem Domain?”

At the location of the Gem Domain, Daoist Senior and Father Goudan, along with Senior Three-Eyes, had set up a plan, drawing all immortals and top Tribulation Transcenders from myriad practitioners in the universe to give Song Shuhang a chance for a swift resolution.

If they were to go to the Gem Domain, he was also preparing to take Sixteen back to Su Clan’s Ancestor Star to meet up with Su Clan’s Sixteen and the mysterious ancestor of the Su Clan.

“Don’t rush, first check if the ‘Domination Secret Method•Reverse’ is ready,” Senior White reminded.

Their advantage lay in having mastered the information and actions of the ‘Dark Sun’ and the hidden Fourth Heavenly Dao ‘Dark Giant’, even conducting targeted research on the ‘Domination Secret Method’.

Intelligence is the utmost importance in modern warfare.

Know yourself and know your enemy, and you are halfway to winning the war.

Song Shuhang extended his hand and opened the ‘Confucian Sage Eye Research Group’ with a point in the vacuum.

“@White from the Netherworld, @My Family Has a Twin Eggs, Father Goudan, Senior White, regarding the research on the ‘Domination Secret Method,’ do we have any results yet?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Mister Song, did you and Fellow Daoist White finish planting the column?” Heavenly Daizi responded with a question.

“All set, and now getting ready for the next step,” Song Shuhang replied.

Senior White two: “The Domination Secret Method deconstruction is complete, Domination Secret Method•Reverse has been structured successfully, you can come back and try the effect of the secret technique.”

All the seniors, being in the ‘Heavenly Dao Time Secret Realm,’ multiple times the duration of a day and night in the main world had already passed in the secret realm. With the support of the ‘Heavenly Dao Calculation Ability’ backed by Daoist Senior, the research to break the Domination Secret Method was going smoothly.

Now, it was just a matter of putting it into practice.

“If that’s the case... the war has begun!” Senior Three-Eyes stated gravely.

Next, it’s Tyrannical Song’s war.

“We have already directed most of the immortals in the ‘Gem Domain’ from the myriad realms. A portion of them were politely invited by your ‘fat ball’ and have been engaging in discourse with your manifestation. Now, returning and mastering both the ‘Domination Secret Method’ and the ‘Domination Secret Method•Reverse’... the next step, we head to the Gem Domain,” Daoist Senior spoke.

He was already prepared and standing by, waiting to step down.

“I’ll learn the secret technique myself, and once I have, I will simplify it,” Senior White said at that moment.

There was no time for Song Shuhang to personally learn the intricate process of the secret techniques... He would simplify the secret techniques down to two formation symbols, then teach them through transferral.

“Tyrannical Song has become spoiled because of you, Fellow Daoist White,” Pavilion Master Chu commented.

“It’s okay, if I don’t have enough basic knowledge, I’ll catch up after achieving immortality. It’s a crisis right now, and we need extraordinary measures!” Song Shuhang made a quick decision.

“Alright, then I’ll set my retirement for tomorrow. Today, you return to the secret realm and nurture all of the ‘Combined Magical Treasure’ along with Fellow Daoist White’s Meteor Sword into human forms,” Daoist Senior decided.

One day in the external world is enough time in the time-distorted secret realm for Song Shuhang to nurture all of the magical treasures to their ultimate potential!

...

...

The day had passed in the main world,

It was February 4th, 2020, the beginning of spring in China.

Tyrannical Song sprang up with a carp’s flip, leaping to his feet.

Behind him, exactly three sets of ‘Combined Magical Treasure of Thirty-Three Beasts’ transformed into tiny metal figures the size of thumbs, circling around him and emitting a series of tinkling laughter.

They were like mythological flower elves.

In Song Shuhang’s hands, a light blade conjured a light wheel, coalescing into the form of Su Clan’s Sixteen.

“You young people really know how to have fun,” Pavilion Master Chu’s dumb hair slowly said.

Using the state of ‘human-saber fusion’ to cultivate human emotions was something unheard of.

“Have you mastered the secret formation techniques that White taught you?” The White Dragon lazily asked, draped around Song Shuhang’s neck.

“Mastered.” Song Shuhang confidently replied.

His talent for saber techniques was strong, his innate skill in fist techniques was not bad, and his talent for learning Senior White’s simplified formation techniques fell somewhere in between his saber and fist talents, also fairly strong.

“Then, go meet up with White and set off,” the White Dragon said. “It’s about time.”

“Mhm.” Song Shuhang nodded in agreement.

He beckoned with his hand, and two sets of the Combined Magical Treasure landed on him; 32 of the items entered his dantian, while the Defiant Whale Glove artifact spirit fairy armed his right hand.

Fellow Daoist Stone Tablet, Nine Virtues Phoenix Saber, and Senior Scarlet Heaven Sword all hung at his waist.

“Main body!” Song the fat ball bounced over from afar.

Song Shuhang beckoned, and Song the fat ball transformed into a cloak that draped over him.

The fat ball cloak fluttered majestically.

Accompanying Song the fat ball were Senior White and Senior White Two, walking side by side.

When the two Senior Whites walked together, the rest of the world paled in comparison.

The fully evolved Meteor Sword, carrying a set of the Combined Magical Treasure, returned to Senior White’s side, dancing joyfully.

Senior White affectionately patted Meteor Sword.

“Time flies.” Senior White looked at Song Shuhang and Sixteen, his eyes drifting slightly.

In a trance, he seemed to return to the time when he had just come out of secluded meditation and was picked up by Song Shuhang.

Back then, Song Shuhang barely knew anything and had just started on his path of cultivation, extremely interesting.

The Song Shuhang of today was still interesting, yet without realizing it, had grown so much.

The still innocently smiling Song Shuhang before him had quietly become a reliable fellow daoist.

“You’ve grown up, Shuhang,” Senior White suddenly said happily.

“Yes, Senior White,” Song Shuhang said with a smile, showing six teeth.

Memories, as if returning to last year.

Senior White had just exploded out of his statue form.

“Hello, Fellow Daoist Shuhang.” At that time, the indescribably handsome Senior White greeted him with a daoist handprint.

“Hello, True Monarch White Senior.” Back then, junior cultivator Song Shuhang imitated Senior White’s gesture and returned the courtesy.
